**Marcus**: Only a third of the picture can be "read" ... But I can see it clearly.

**马库斯**：唔！巧妙的几何排布，达到了视觉上的平衡。但是他的创作者贪图形式，忽略了表达。边框的材质……啊，这个不重要，下一页。\
**Marcus**: Mmm! An ingenious composition that balances the different elements of the picture. Sadly, the creator focused too much on the form and overlooked the content. The frame is made of ... Ah, not important. Next page.

**马库斯**：这幅幸运得多，它还有一半，画中的女子只剩下了半身。但是——呃，看来西奥菲尔是位风流的贵族先生。这不是他第一个骚扰的女模特了。\
**Marcus**: This one is luckier. Half of it survived the fire, so we can see the lower half of the lady in the picture. But ... eh, Theophil certainly had a way with women. She was not his first prey.

**马库斯**：呀！这幅甚至只有个边框。这些作品被火焰损坏得太严重了。我记得，刚才哪个方向有一幅完整的……\
**Marcus**: And this one, only a frame remains. The rest of his works are too damaged, but I do remember an intact one somewhere ...

**马库斯**：……但除此之外，没更多的东西了。下一页。\
**Marcus**: ... But aside from this, I don't see anything else. Next page.

**马库斯**：……！\
**Marcus**: ...!

她转过身，撞入一双浅色的瞳孔。\
She turns, colliding with a pair of light-colored eyes.

远远的，伊索尔德仿佛在望着她。\
Despite the distance, it feels as though Isolde is gazing back at her.

**马库斯**：人也是可阅读的。这位就是，伊索尔德小姐……\
**Marcus**: People can be "read" too. That person, Ms. Isolde ...

深呼吸。页面再次于眼前展开。\
A deep breath. The page unfolds before her eyes once again.

**马库斯**：她没有追逐巴黎的流行，依然穿着保守的束胸衣，只是在腰间佩戴了一些新艺术风格的珠宝……就像一只苍白的蝴蝶。\
**Marcus**: Unlike other ladies pursuing the latest fashions in Paris, she still wears the corset, with only some Art Nouveau jewelry by her waist. She's as delicate as a butterfly.

**马库斯**：她是一个人尽皆知的灵媒。据说迪塔斯多夫家族都十分擅长通灵技艺。如今，他们主要用此从事艺术……呼唤一个灵附身自己，从而完成诗歌、演唱、绘画。\
**Marcus**: She is a renowned medium. The Dittarsdorf family is well known for their mediumship. Nowadays they use that power mostly for art. That is, they summon a spirit to possess their body so they can sing, write, and paint like no other.

**马库斯**：而通灵能力的强大，也让他们饱受神经衰弱和歇斯底里症的折磨。这一古老家族的人丁并不兴旺。\
**Marcus**: They also suffered for this power. Wracked by neurosis and hysteria, the family has had very few members despite its long history.

**马库斯**：等一等……\
**Marcus**: Wait a minute ...

**马库斯**：她身后那幅画是完整的！而且……如此庞大——\
**Marcus**: That picture behind her is still intact! And ... it is enormous ...

**马库斯**：这就是《拯救》……？\
**Marcus**: It that ... The Salvation?

**马库斯**：奇怪。这幅画……？\
**Marcus**: Strange. This painting is ...?

翻页特效-滤镜关闭

**海因里希**：小姐，您真有眼光。\
**Heinrich**: You have a keen eye for art, Miss.

**马库斯**：啊！\
**Marcus**: Ah!

声音自背后响起，脸上带着雀斑的男人露出一个和煦的微笑。\
A voice leaps up behind her, bursting from behind the warm smile of the freckle-faced man.

**海因里希**：这幅画，我的挚友——齐格蒙德的《拯救》！他唯一留下来的，最完美的作品。\
**Heinrich**: This painting is the work of my dearest friend, Siegmund—The Salvation! The only piece he left behind that survived the consuming flames.

**海因里希**：一个又一个、充满魅力的魔力圆——噢，这是卡卡尼亚小姐的话！我们都很热衷于这一概念。\
**Heinrich**: These enchanting, magical circles, one next to another ... Oh, I was only reciting Ms. Kakania. We're both passionate about the subject.

**马库斯**：……！\
**Marcus**: ...!

**海因里希**：真可惜，如果她还在的话便能为您做更好的讲解了，她的话语总能令人心潮澎湃。\
**Heinrich**: How regrettable, she would've given you a much better explanation if she were here. Her words can easily stir one's soul.

**马库斯**：您说，卡卡尼亚？您有一个朋友叫卡卡尼亚？\
**Marcus**: Did you say Kakania? You have a friend called Kakania?

**海因里希**：噢！是的，艺术家都偏向拥有一个独特的代号！我还认识“橙骑士”、“莱茵河的维克多”、“苹果卷”【Apfelstrudel】……\
**Heinrich**: Oh, yes. Every artist has their own nickname. I also have the honor of knowing the Orange Knight, Victor of the Rhine, Apfelstrudel ...

**海因里希**：您认识她吗？真不凑巧，她才刚离开，约摸现在已经和施瓦茨医生在会议大堂见面哩！\
**Heinrich**: Are you a friend of Kakania? Too bad she just left. She should be meeting with Dr. Schwartz by now.

马库斯抬头，导师的目光投向这里，轻轻地摇了摇头。\
Marcus looks up. Her mentor casts her eyes to the same spot and shakes her head gently.

**马库斯**：不，我也是第一次听说……谢谢您的介绍，先生。\
**Marcus**: No, the name sounded a little strange to me, that's all ... But I appreciate the explanation, sir.

空气中，弥散的孢子微不可察地轻微骚动着。\
In the air, the dispersed spores stir imperceptibly.

“砰砰啵啵！”\
*bang! bang! crash!*

爆破产生的粉尘对鼻腔而言颇具侵略性。\
The dust from the explosion pervades the air, sucking deep into nostrils and open mouths.

**基金会分部专员**：咳咳，出了什么事？！\
**Foundation Staff**: *cough* What happened?!

音效、特效-有灵体出现的感觉

**伊索尔德**：……！\
**Isolde**: ...!

**基金会分部专员**：……游灵？！不是说没有降灵仪式？……迪塔斯多夫小姐，我需要一个解释。\
**Foundation Staff**: Are these ... ghosts? Didn't you say there wasn't a seance? Ms. Dittarsdorf, I would very much like an explanation.

**海因里希**：唔噢！它们怎么还在追着我……\
**Heinrich**: Whoa! They're still chasing me.

**霍夫曼**：……是“砰砰孢子”起了反应。马库斯，你还能继续“阅读”吗？\
**Hofmann**: ... The "Detection Spores" have taken effect and enveloped the ghosts. Marcus, can you still "read"?

**马库斯**：嗯……我想还可以！\
**Marcus**: Hmm ... I think so!

**霍夫曼**：很好，我来牵制它。神秘术相关就交给你了。\
**Hofmann**: Good. I'll draw its attention. You take care of the arcanum part.

**基金会分部专员**：迪塔斯多夫小姐，您对我说这只是彩排。可眼下出现了这样的情况——更要紧的是，我的两位助手还在这里！\
**Foundation Staff**: Ms. Dittarsdorf, you told me this was just an opera rehearsal. Now look at this mess—and more importantly, my two assistants are still here!

**基金会分部专员**：我需要一个向上级汇报的可靠理由。\
**Foundation Staff**: I must ask you for a good reason to report to my superior.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

肤色苍白的女孩沉默着，微微低下了头。\
The pale girl remains silent, bowing her head.

音效-大门打开，稳步进来

**卡尔**：哦！伊索尔德，我可爱的、令人怜爱的小女儿——\
**Karl**: Oh! Isolde, my dear, lovely girl.

熟悉的面孔不请自来。\
An all-too-familiar mustachioed face arrives without invitation.

卡尔步伐稳健，走上前，亲昵地拉起了伊索尔德的手。\
Karl's steps are at a steady trouncing waddle as he approaches and takes Isolde's hand.

**伊索尔德**：卡尔先生……！\
**Isolde**: Mr. Karl!

**基金会分部专员**：卡尔部长。\
**Foundation Staff**: Director.

**卡尔**：瞧你的脸色，怎么这样苍白？一定是为剧团忧心造成的，过来，孩子，过来……\
**Karl**: Look at you, so pale! The play is sapping your strength. Come, child, come to me.

**卡尔**：我早就叫施瓦茨好好照应你！他一定是太忙了才疏忽了对你的照料。约莫是这样频繁的公开诊疗对一名贵族医生而言有些繁重。\
**Karl**: I told Schwartz to take good care of you! Well, I guess he can't be in two places at once. The frequent presentations must've been too much for a doctor such as he.

**卡尔**：尽管你已经痊愈了，但答应我，还是好好照顾自己，好吗？你的母亲已如此令人惋惜，帝国不能再缺少一颗明珠。\
**Karl**: I've learned that you've recovered from hysteria, which is good, but promise me that you'll look after yourself, will you? Your late mother suffered a tragic end, and it'd be unbearable for the Empire to lose another star.

**伊索尔德**：您过誉了……\
**Isolde**: You flatter me.

**卡尔**：约瑟夫。\
**Karl**: Joseph.

**基金会分部专员**：是……卡尔部长。\
**Foundation Staff**: Yes, director.

**卡尔**：别对艺术如此严苛，那只是一些精妙的舞台效果！海因里希是专门研究这个的，不是吗？重视艺术正是我们自由意志的体现。\
**Karl**: Don't be so hard on them, those were wonderful stage effects! Heinrich is an expert at this, yes? What better demonstrates our free will than respecting the artists and their work?

**卡尔**：我们都不介意这点小插曲！\
**Karl**: None of us would mind an episode of excitement every once in a while!

卡尔的目光迎向霍夫曼。\
Karl meets Hofmann's eyes in another overly affable attempt at good nature.

**卡尔**：即便是总部的老爷们来了，也会理解的，不是吗？\
**Karl**: Even the gentlemen from the headquarters would agree with me, don't you think?

**基金会分部专员**：是，是……\
**Foundation Staff**: Yes, you're right ...

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

**卡尔**：我们人手这样紧，助手们应当投入更多的精力到更要紧的事务里去。\
**Karl**: We are short on manpower, and the assistants should focus on more important matters.

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

**霍夫曼**：呵，我们该离开了。\
**Hofmann**: Hm. We should leave.

## 6TH-07 公正的决斗 / A "Fair" Duel

音效-使用通讯器的电子音

**马库斯**：您好，我想查找一本小说的写作年代。\
**Marcus**: Good day. I would like to check the date of a novel.

**马库斯**：是的，罗伯特·穆齐尔的《没有个性的人》……\
**Marcus**: Yes, it is The Man Without Qualities, by Robert Musil.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**马库斯**：哦，好的，好的……\
**Marcus**: Oh. I see, I see ...

**霍夫曼**：消息如何？\
**Hofmann**: What did they say?

**马库斯**：同我印象中的一样……\
**Marcus**: Just as I remembered it ...

**马库斯**：这本小说写作于1930年，“卡卡尼亚”这个词也源于罗伯特·穆齐尔的发明。\
**Marcus**: The novel was completed in 1930, the word "Kakania" was also created by Robert Musil.

**马库斯**：在1914年，理应没有这个名字，这是一个不属于这个时代的笔名。\
**Marcus**: Kakania should not be a nickname for anyone in 1914.

**霍夫曼**：一个不属于这个时代的信息。\
**Hofmann**: It doesn't belong to this era.

**霍夫曼**：那么，这条线索给了我们两种可能性：一，她隶属于重塑之手；二，她接触过重塑之手的相关成员。\
**Hofmann**: She could be with Manus Vindictae, or, at least is associated with their people.

**马库斯**：还有……刚才我在分离派之家，“阅读”了那幅《拯救》。\
**Marcus**: What's more ... When we were at the Secession Building, I "read" that painting, The Salvation.

**马库斯**：那些画作中，唯有它有些……格格不入？西奥菲尔似乎在《拯救》上尝试了一种全新的处理方式，笔触更加舒展——甚至是，放肆……\
**Marcus**: It seemed ... out of place compared to the other paintings. Theophil may have applied a new technique on The Salvation, a more daring kind, audacious, even.

**马库斯**：那是很细微的差别……我无法确定。我被那位语气奇怪的绅士先生打断了施术，没能读完全部的信息。\
**Marcus**: But these are only subtleties ... I can't be too certain. I was interrupted by that strangely speaking gentleman, so I didn't get everything.

**马库斯**：而且，它的画作内容，让我想起“魔圈”组织的标志……\
**Marcus**: Another thing, its content reminds me of the symbol of "The Circle."

马库斯在书箱中进行翻找，很快在那叠厚厚的名册中摸到了这张夹带的传单。\
Marcus rummages through the bookcase, finding the pamphlet tucked within the thick register.

**马库斯**：这个扭曲的圆圈形状，和《拯救》中出现的很像。\
**Marcus**: This twisting circle resembles the circles in The Salvation.

**马库斯**：海因里希说，这是一个又一个的魔力圆。我想它一定有什么深刻的寓意……\
**Marcus**: Heinrich called them magical circles, one next to another. They must be more than just circles, I think ...

**马库斯**：是想表达激情的癫狂吗？不，这些圆的线条很干净。还是一种永恒的纯净？不，这样它的轮廓又太扭曲了……\
**Marcus**: Was he demonstrating the madness of passion? But the lines are clean. Perhaps the purity of eternity? No, the circles are too twisted for that ...

**马库斯**：又或者，它只是代表一种原始的生命力……？\
**Marcus**: Or, was he just representing a primitive state of being ...?

**霍夫曼**：我完全看不懂。\
**Hofmann**: I don't understand any of it.

**霍夫曼**：所以，这应该是艺术。\
**Hofmann**: So, this must be art.

**马库斯**：哈哈哈，霍夫曼女士，您真幽默……\
**Marcus**: Hahaha, ma'am. You're funny sometimes.

**霍夫曼**：……？我刚刚并不是在开玩笑。\
**Hofmann**: ...? I wasn't joking.

**马库斯**：……？\
**Marcus**: ...?

**霍夫曼**：仅凭现有的线索，尚不能断定这个青年神秘学家团体和重塑的关系。不过心怀不满、渴望变革的年轻人，从来都是他们动员的第一对象。\
**Hofmann**: Based on what we know, we can't be sure if this group of young arcanists and the Manus are connected. But we all know that the latter is eager to win over the cynical, revolutionary youth.

**霍夫曼**：你做得很好，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: You did well, Marcus.

**霍夫曼**：“魔圈”名单上的几位重要人物：伊索尔德、海因里希，甚至是已经亡故的西奥菲尔……我们刚刚都接触到了。\
**Hofmann**: The important figures of "The Circle"—Isolde, Heinrich, and even the late Theophil—we have made contact with them all.

**霍夫曼**：只有卡卡尼亚……从她的资料中我们能得到什么？\
**Hofmann**: Only this Kakania ... What does the intel say about her?

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚——也就是克拉拉小姐。她的神秘术传承自自己的家族，可以用镜子映射人们内心的图景。她曾就读于一所医学院，但是中途就辍学了。\
**Marcus**: Kakania, also known as Ms. Klara, inherited her arcane skills from her family. She's able to reflect people's thoughts in a mirror. She was once a medical student, but dropped out halfway through.

**马库斯**：如今她似乎仍以心理医生的身份活动，基金会在行医许可证方面和她纠缠了许久。\
**Marcus**: These days, she shows up at various social events as a psychiatrist, which the Foundation tries to prohibit because she doesn't have a license.

**马库斯**：还有，她另外的身份是一名——社会活动家。\
**Marcus**: And she is also ... an activist.

**霍夫曼**：社会活动家……？\
**Hofmann**: An activist?

**马库斯**：我刚才从海因里希先生那里听到，她去找一位名叫施瓦茨的医生了。\
**Marcus**: According to Mr. Heinrich, she is meeting with a doctor named Schwartz today.

**霍夫曼**：施瓦茨……卡尔口中的那位贵族医生。\
**Hofmann**: Schwartz ... The family doctor Karl mentioned.

**霍夫曼**：——我们去碰碰运气。\
**Hofmann**: Let's try our luck there.

音效-嘈杂白噪音\
公开诊疗厅

**公证人**：那么，克拉拉女士，施瓦茨先生。\
**Notary**: Now then, Ms. Klara, Mr. Schwartz.

**公证人**：只有三种合法的武器：第一，军刀；第二，剑；第三，手枪。\
**Notary**: Only three weapons are allowed in the duel—the army knife, the sword, and the pistol.

**卡卡尼亚**：由施瓦茨医生决定吧，贵族中的决斗老手。我当然很荣幸能登上您的名单，同时，也很荣幸成为您连胜记录的终结者。\
**Kakania**: I will leave the choice to Dr. Schwartz, for he has more experience in these duels than I do. It's an honor to fight you, and I look forward to ending your winning streak.

**施瓦茨医生**：对我来说则正相反！\
**Dr. Schwartz**: Not so much an honorable thing for me.

**马库斯**：让一让……劳烦您……\
**Marcus**: Excuse me ... Please ...

霍夫曼伸出手，无情地劈开了一条道路。\
Hofmann extends her hand, mercilessly cleaving a path through the crowd.

**霍夫曼**：请问，这里发生了什么事？\
**Hofmann**: Pardon me. What is happening?

**路人Ⅰ**：是荣誉决斗，女士！\
**Passerby I**: A duel, ma'am!

**路人Ⅰ**：方才施瓦茨还在诊疗，克拉拉小姐直接闯了进来！争执之后就是您现在看到的这样了。\
**Passerby I**: Just as Dr. Schwartz was demonstrating his therapy, Ms. Klara barged right in! They were arguing, and this is how they decided to end it.

**路人Ⅰ**：尽管为了防止双方的朋友从中作梗，任何决斗的发起都不能超过四十八小时……但我还从未见过如此速战速决的……\
**Passerby I**: To ensure fairness of the duel, the combat must happen within 48 hours of the challenge ... But I've never seen one take place on the spot.

**路人Ⅱ**：哦，希望他们的手法好些，别误伤到我们。\
**Passerby II**: Well, I hope they know what they're doing. I don't want to get caught as collateral damage.

**马库斯**：那件绿色的衣服——原来她就是卡卡尼亚小姐！怎么办，如果她不幸受伤，我们的任务……\
**Marcus**: That green dress ... So she is Kakania! What do we do? If she gets injured, our mission will ...

**霍夫曼**：……不要太为时代里的人担忧，他们有自己的生活轨迹。\
**Hofmann**: Don't worry about people in their time. It is their life to live.

**霍夫曼**：而且，如果你无法确切评估自己的行为会造成怎样的后果，那就不要行动。比起干涉历史所代表的负面影响，一时的线索中断是可容忍的。\
**Hofmann**: Never intervene if you don't know the exact consequences of your actions. The course of history is more important than our investigation.

音效-委外合约小队特殊通讯器联络音，这个需要特殊做，肉鸽也能用到

**霍夫曼**：调查员格蕾塔·霍夫曼，请讲。\
**Hofmann**: This is investigator Greta Hofmann.

**霍夫曼**：什么……？稍等。\
**Hofmann**: What ...? Hold on.

**霍夫曼**：我需要离开一下。\
**Hofmann**: I'll be right back.

**马库斯**：您要去哪儿？\
**Marcus**: Where are you going?

**霍夫曼**：委外合约小队的专员有要事联络。我不会离开太久，也不会太远。\
**Hofmann**: The Field Agent Squad needs to speak to me. This won't take long.

**霍夫曼**：在我回来之前，这里就交给你了。牢记我说的话，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: I will leave this to you. Remember what I said, Marcus.

**马库斯**：是，是的，霍夫曼女士。\
**Marcus**: Yes, madam.

霍夫曼转身，向着那面桃花心木的巴洛克式木门走去，背影没入了人群之中。\
Hofmann turns toward the Baroque wooden door made of mahogany, before her figure disappears amidst the crowd.

只留下了青涩的助手小姐。\
Only her still-unfledged assistant remains.

**马库斯**：交给我了，交给我了，交给我了……\
**Marcus**: Leaving this to me, to me, to me ...

马库斯默念了三遍，试图让自己心跳平稳下来。\
Marcus recites it to herself as a mantra, attempting to slow her racing heart.

**马库斯**：深呼吸，马库斯！这没什么好紧张的，你不能总指望着霍夫曼女士。你早晚要独当一面！\
**Marcus**: Breathe, Marcus! There's nothing to be nervous about. You can't be an assistant forever. There will come a day when you're all on your own.

**马库斯**：和在分离派之家一样，只要看着就好了……如果有机会和卡卡尼亚小姐搭话，就伪装成普通的基金会职员——简单！\
**Marcus**: Just like at the Secession Building, I only have to watch her. If I end up talking to Ms. Kakania, I'll just pretend to be an ordinary employee of the Foundation ... Easy!

**马库斯**：你以前不也是一个人吗？在灯塔，在森林……“阅读”……\
**Marcus**: You used to do well on your own, when you were reading in the lighthouse and the forest ...

特效-翻页

**马库斯**：唔，施瓦茨医生……他曾决斗过三次，无一败绩——真了不起！他这次仍决定用手枪。\
**Marcus**: Mm, Dr. Schwartz ... Three times he has been involved in duels, and three times he has won—impressive! This time, he's still going for the pistol.

**马库斯**：可是……卡卡尼亚小姐并没有带助手，他们两人还只有一名证人。这应当是不合规的，难道她认可了这种行为？\
**Marcus**: But ... Ms. Kakania does not have an assistant. And she has only one witness in this duel. This is not right. Why did she agree to this?

**马库斯**：这个决定鲁莽而危险。即便是神秘学家，在枪械决斗中也至少必须有一名助手在身边。\
**Marcus**: She's being reckless. Even an arcanist should have at least one assistant in a duel.

**马库斯**：施瓦茨医生的助手拿来的是成对的手枪……型号是……勃朗宁M1910，唔，它能作为决斗手枪吗？\
**Marcus**: Dr. Schwartz's assistant brought them a pair of pistols ... FN Model 1910. Hmm, is that a right weapon for a duel?

**马库斯**：好挤，有点看不清楚……\
**Marcus**: It's too crowded here. I can't see ...

**马库斯**：嗯？\
**Marcus**: Hmm?

音效/特效-那种纸上有标注的感觉

**马库斯**：……不对——卡卡尼亚小姐的那把枪有问题……\
**Marcus**: No, the pistol given to Ms. Kakania ... something's wrong with it.

**马库斯**：这些子弹……糟了，决斗一旦开始……她真的会出事的！\
**Marcus**: The bullets ... Her life is in danger if the duel begins!

**马库斯**：但是霍夫曼女士告诫过我……\
**Marcus**: But Madam Hofmann warned me about the consequences of intervention ...

特效-翻页-变为正常

**马库斯**：如果，如果只是像刚才，在分离派之家里那样，以分部职员的身份，进行简单的交流呢？\
**Marcus**: What if, what if, I just go and talk to her as an employee of the Foundation branch, like I did at the Secession Building?

**马库斯**：目前来看，海因里希言行古怪，卡尔先生又不愿让我们与伊索尔德小姐接触。\
**Marcus**: So far, Heinrich has been difficult to communicate with, while Mr. Karl doesn't want us to get in touch with Ms. Isolde.

**马库斯**：她还与“魔圈”有关，且和西奥菲尔有所接触的，只有眼前这位“卡卡尼亚”。这个名字……又如此特殊。\
**Marcus**: Ms. Kakania is the only person who is both a friend of Theophil and associated with "The Circle." But I have to be careful with this name.

**马库斯**：可是，万一她就是重塑之手的人，惊动她就会让任务失败的风险上升……不！但卡卡尼亚也不知道我是总部的职员，所以我搭话成功的概率也会上升……\
**Marcus**: If she is indeed one of the Manus Vindictae, I will be jeopardizing this mission by going near her ... But wait! She doesn't know that I'm from the headquarters, so she probably will talk to me.

**马库斯**：不，但我怎么知道卡卡尼亚不知道我是总部的职员？也许卡尔先生并不值得信任？嗯？难道卡卡尼亚和卡尔先生是一伙的？他们都是“K”开头……\
**Marcus**: But how do I know she doesn't know my identity? What if Mr. Karl is not to be trusted? And what if Mr. Karl and she are in this together? Their names both start with a "K" ...

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**马库斯**：我在想什么？\
**Marcus**: What am I thinking?

马库斯伸出双手，奋力拍了拍脸颊，成功地引来旁人侧目。\
Marcus patting her cheeks with an unaware gusto, drawing side glances from the others present.

**马库斯**：不不，不！这里不是弗兰南群岛了，我不能再像以前那样漫无止境地过度思考了！\
**Marcus**: Stop, stop! I'm not on the Flannan Isles anymore. I can't waste my day on endless thoughts!

**马库斯**：想想霍夫曼女士的话，想想目前最要紧的任务，我得阻止卡卡尼亚在决斗中丧命，我得从她嘴里得到西奥菲尔的线索……\
**Marcus**: Remember what Madam Hofmann said, think of the immediate mission. I have to prevent Kakania from getting killed in the duel. She has the clues about Theophil that I need ...

**马库斯**：……如果你无法确切评估自己的行为会造成怎样的后果……\
**Marcus**: Never intervene if you don't know the exact consequences of your actions ...

深呼吸一口气。\
A long, deep breath.

**马库斯**：我评估完毕了，霍夫曼女士。\
**Marcus**: I have assessed the risks, madam.

**马库斯**：如果我只是一个什么都不知道的基金会职员……我也会这么做的！\
**Marcus**: I will not stand by and watch this happen ... even if I don't know the consequences!

音效-挤入人群

**施瓦茨医生**：我需要向您说明，此次事件不光关系到迪塔斯多夫小姐——这不是您第一次对我名誉进行羞辱了。\
**Dr. Schwartz**: I need to make this clear to you. Not only have you hindered Ms. Dittarsdorf from getting the treatment she needs, but you have repeatedly defamed me.

**卡卡尼亚**：噢，如果您把“事实”与“另一种学术观点”当作是羞辱的话。\
**Kakania**: Oh, I can only admit that you're right if you have to call a different academic perspective slander.

**施瓦茨医生**：“另一种学术观点”……？！您管弗洛伊德那套神棍玩意儿称之为“学术”吗？\
**Dr. Schwartz**: "A different academic perspective" ... ?! Do you really think Freud and his petty tricks are "academic"?

**施瓦茨医生**：这真是对科学最大的侮辱！\
**Dr. Schwartz**: One could hardly find a worse insult to science than this!

**卡卡尼亚**：是吗，您真这样认为？我的同僚在闲话时曾向我提及——您向军方出售了催眠技术，这是否属实呢？\
**Kakania**: Is that so? Do you really mean that? Rumor has it that you taught the military the method of hypnosis for a price. Do you wish to clear things up here?

**施瓦茨医生**：……\
**Dr. Schwartz**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：哈哈，您默认了。您没贩售最为“先进”的电疗，却用您看不上的“神棍玩意儿”去巴结大臣吗？\
**Kakania**: Hah, your silence is a resounding "yes." Tell me, why did you please the ministers with these "petty tricks," but not with your "most advanced" electrotherapy you've been touting?

**卡卡尼亚**：您对弗洛伊德先生的鄙夷，是否也与他公开摒弃催眠有关呢？\
**Kakania**: Do you harbor negative feelings towards Mr. Freud because of his open rejection of hypnosis?

**施瓦茨医生**：……这和你又有什么关系？\
**Dr. Schwartz**: ... What does any of this have to do with you?

**卡卡尼亚**：当然有，施瓦茨先生。您的行径严重损害了神秘学家同胞们的利益。\
**Kakania**: Many things, Mr. Schwartz. Your behavior has greatly undermined the interests of arcanists, who are your own people.

**卡卡尼亚**：而且，催眠是最应被摒弃的手段——它完全无视了人的自由意志！\
**Kakania**: Not to mention that hypnosis is a violation of a patient's free will!

**卡卡尼亚**：我有理由认为您发起决斗是因为私人恩怨——我需要澄清，您妻子来我这里接受谈话治疗，和维也纳人都觉得您那方面“能力”欠佳毫无关联。\
**Kakania**: And I have reason to believe that this duel is entirely personal. I must make it clear that your wife's appointment with me has nothing to do with the rumors of your ... lackluster performance in the bedroom.

**卡卡尼亚**：施瓦茨先生，您的矛头对错了人，您更应该去找那些在小报上编排您的人！\
**Kakania**: I'm not the real enemy, Mr. Schwartz. The gossipmongers and the tabloid writers are!

**施瓦茨医生**：你，你——\
**Dr. Schwartz**: You, you ...

**公证人**：双方准备完毕了吗？\
**Notary**: Are both duelists ready?

**施瓦茨医生**：完全好了，先生。\
**Dr. Schwartz**: Perfectly ready.

**卡卡尼亚**：我这边也——\
**Kakania**: I'm ready too—

**马库斯**：不——没有！\
**Marcus**: No! She's not!

**卡卡尼亚&施瓦茨医生**：……？\
**Kakania & Dr. Schwartz**: ...?

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚小姐还没有准备好！\
**Marcus**: Ms. Kakania needs another minute!

众人的目光让她的嗓音微微发抖。\
Their collective gaze causes her voice to tremble slightly.

**马库斯**：呃，呃呃啊，好多人……好想死，好想回家……我，我为什么要递交外派申请……\
**Marcus**: Err, ahh, the crowd ... shoot me, I want to go home ... Why oh why did you apply for this mission, Marcus ...

尽管有如此的心理活动，她还是颤颤巍巍地伸出手，试图体面地、不靠爬行地走到那个台上去。\
Despite her mental turmoil, she extends her hand, attempting to ascend with some dignity intact, or at least without resorting to crawling.

**马库斯**：我，我是她的助手，我来……\
**Marcus**: I-I am Ms. Kakania's assistant. I'm here to ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：很抱歉打断您，小姐。但就我所知，我应当没有实力聘请一位圣洛夫基金会的在职人员来当我的“决斗助手”。\
**Kakania**: Sorry to interrupt, miss. But the last time I checked, I couldn't possibly afford a St. Pavlov Foundation member to be my aide.

**马库斯**：啊！糟糕，我的徽章……\
**Marcus**: Ah! Darn it, I forgot about my badge ...

卡卡尼亚收回勃朗宁，绕在指头上转着圈儿。\
Kakania retracts her pistol, twirling it around her finger.

**卡卡尼亚**：所以我猜，这很可能是某种具有官僚风格的管理手段。您为何要担心呢！请您看清，这场决斗用的全然是人类手法——不含任何神秘术！\
**Kakania**: So the Foundation is trying to intervene. Don't worry, Ms. Foundation staff! Look around, we're doing it the human way—no arcane skills involved!

**卡卡尼亚**：分部的总负责人不该是您的榜样。领了施瓦茨的克朗，您便会失去一部分正直！这不是笔划算买卖。\
**Kakania**: The head of the Foundation branch should not be your role model. Mind you, you're giving up a part of your integrity for taking his Krones! A terrible deal indeed.

**马库斯**：我……\
**Marcus**: I ...

**卡卡尼亚**：而且，这场决斗是真枪实弹。它不涉及任何神秘术许可证的办理！您找不到能诬陷我的由头。\
**Kakania**: Besides, we're using human guns! We don't need the Foundation's license to use these. I'm not doing anything against the Foundation's rules, am I?

勃朗宁又旋了一圈儿，完美的圆形。\
The Browning pistol spins once more in a perfect circle.

**卡卡尼亚**：如果有什么要紧事，等我处理完这场决斗如何？您得往后让让，子弹可不长眼睛——\
**Kakania**: If it's urgent, can we wait until after the duel? Please stand back, the bullets can't tell the difference between friend and enemy.

**马库斯**：我，我……\
**Marcus**: I, I ...

马库斯再次被对方连珠炮似的发言打断。\
Marcus is again interrupted by the rapid-fire speech of the other party.

**马库斯**：……你不要再转了——这里面的子弹有问题！\
**Marcus**: ... Please don't use that gun! The bullets in it are dangerous!

**卡卡尼亚**：……什么？\
**Kakania**: ... What?

**马库斯**：这把枪的子弹有问题！直接开枪会炸膛的！\
公证人先生，我要求检查……\
**Marcus**: The bullets are wrong! The gun will burst if you pull the trigger!\
Sir, I demand that the gun be checked ...

卡卡尼亚将已经转了半圈的手枪握紧，利落地取出了弹匣。\
Kakania grips the half-turned gun tightly, before deftly removing the magazine.

**卡卡尼亚**：……！\
**Kakania**: ...!

**卡卡尼亚**：这些子弹的型号……\
**Kakania**: The size of these bullets ...

卡卡尼亚感觉后背流下冷汗。\
A cold bead of sweat drips down her spine.

**卡卡尼亚**：施瓦茨，这是怎么回事？我原以为您至少会保持绅士的底线。\
**Kakania**: I need an explanation, Mr. Schwartz. I thought you had at least the integrity of a gentleman.

**卡卡尼亚**：可是您给我的这把枪……里面的子弹是不符合标准的。如果我使用了它——正如这位政府小姐所说，它会炸膛的。\
**Kakania**: The bullets in my gun are wrong. If I pull the trigger, as Ms. Foundation here said, the barrel will burst.

**路人Ⅱ**：炸膛？我想起来了，安东那个小子就是因为炸膛输了决斗——这竟是施瓦茨动了手脚？这名公证人也是他的人？\
**Passerby II**: A bursted barrel? I remember now. That Anton boy lost the duel to Schwartz for the same reason! Did Schwartz do something to his gun, too? And was the guard in on it too?

**公证人**：……！\
**Notary**: ...!

**施瓦茨医生**：该死……这是污蔑！我并没有……！\
**Dr. Schwartz**: D**n! ... This is defamation! I have never ... !

**维也纳警卫**：停止！谁在这里进行私人决斗——\
**Vienna Guard**: Freeze! Who is dueling here?!

**路人Ⅰ**：啊，卫兵来了——！\
**Passerby I**: Ahhh! The guards are here!

**路人Ⅲ**：当心些，别踩到我的裙摆！\
**Passerby III**: Hey, don't step on my dress!

**马库斯**：糟了！霍夫曼女士还没回来，霍夫曼女士——！\
**Marcus**: Not good! Madam Hofmann has not come back yet. Madam Hofmann ...!

年轻的助手被淹没在了混乱的人潮中。\
The young assistant is engulfed within the chaotic crowd.

**卡卡尼亚**：嘿，小姐！帮了我的政府小姐！\
**Kakania**: Hey, miss! The helpful Ms. Foundation employee!

**马库斯**：……？！卡卡尼亚小姐？\
**Marcus**: Ms. Kakania?

绿衣服的决斗者向她伸出手来。\
The green-clad pistoleer extends her hand.

**卡卡尼亚**：别呆站着——过来！\
**Kakania**: Don't stand there ... Come here!

她牵着马库斯的手，狠狠一拽，二话不说将她抱在了臂弯。\
Kakania grabs the shy assistant's hand, pulling her into a fierce embrace without a second word.

**马库斯**：唔啊啊！\
**Marcus**: Aahh!

卡卡尼亚轻轻一跃，如一只鸟儿般轻盈地落到了窗框上。\
Kakania leaps, alighting herself onto the window frame with the lightness of a bird.

**卡卡尼亚**：好，这条路还算安全……要跳了，政府小姐！三，二，一——当心！\
**Kakania**: Okay, this is a quiet road ... We're going to jump, Ms. Foundation. Three, two, one ... Here we go!

## 6TH-08 镜面与提灯 / Mirror and Lantern

**小贩Ⅰ**：卡卡尼亚！这儿，这儿！\
**Vendor I**: Kakania! This way! Over here!

**卡卡尼亚**：伊里奇！你这次帮大忙啦。谢谢你！这道具真好用……\
**Kakania**: Illich! Thanks a lot! The prop sure came in handy.

卡卡尼亚撕下了假胡子，用手给自己扇着风。\
Kakania tears off her fake beard, fanning herself with her hand.

**马库斯**：唔——呃！呼，下来了，我今天嘴上怎么一直有东西……\
**Marcus**: Mmm ... Ugh! Phew, finally. Why do I keep having things stick to my lips ...

**小贩Ⅰ**：哈！当然啦。我的这个胡子，它可不是一般货色！它的每一根毛都在添加过血根草、蟾蜍心和龙蛇胆的波西米亚药水中充分浸泡过……\
**Vendor I**: Hah! Be careful with that. It is no ordinary beard! Every single strand was soaked in a Bohemian potion mixed with bloodroot, toad's heart, and javangall ...

**小贩Ⅰ**：你们是怎么招惹上卫兵的？\
**Vendor I**: Why were the guards after you?

**卡卡尼亚**：那就说来话长了——\
**Kakania**: That's a long story.

**卡卡尼亚**：噢，不用这样谨慎地盯着这位小姐。她救了我一命，人还算不错，算是半——三分之一个朋友吧！\
**Kakania**: And oh, don't worry about this kind little lady. She saved my life, and she's a half ... a third of a friend!

**马库斯**：三分之一……\
**Marcus**: A third of ...

马库斯在口袋里轻轻松开了通讯器的按钮。\
She discreetly releases the button of the communicator in her pocket.

**马库斯**：呜……这下糟了，通讯线路一直无法连接，根本联系不上霍夫曼女士。\
**Marcus**: Ugh ... This is bad, the connection is down, I can't get in touch with Madam Hofmann.

**马库斯**：她或许在和委外合约小队的专员谈很重要的事，所以启用了屏障模式……\
**Marcus**: She's probably in an important conversation with the Field Agent Squad and has calls on block ...

**马库斯**：没问题的，马库斯，你一个人也没问题的，先和任务目标保持交流……！只是交流而已，这有什么难的呢？没问题的，你演练过……一定没问题的！\
**Marcus**: It's okay, Marcus, you can do this yourself, just stay in the conversation! Communication is not that hard. You've done this through before. You can do it!

她设想了一千种搭上话的可能，却没想到最后是这样的场合。\
Despite having written about a thousand ways to start a conversation, she never expected to find herself in a situation like this.

马库斯开始在脑中疯狂地搜寻话题。所幸，在场的人全都比她健谈得多。\
Marcus frantically racks her mind for topics to discuss. Fortunately, everyone present is far more talkative than she is.

**小贩Ⅰ**：卡卡尼亚，你现在也变成和官老爷做朋友的人了！\
**Vendor I**: My, my, Kakania! Are you friends with government officials now?

**小贩Ⅰ**：真新奇！我在这待了一年，还从未见过嘴上没毛的基金会成员呢！\
**Vendor I**: Times have changed indeed! I've been here for a whole year, but I've never seen an official without a beard!

**小贩Ⅰ**：你是从哪来的？克罗地亚？摩拉维亚？加里西亚？\
**Vendor I**: Where are you from? Croatia? Moravia? Galicia?

**马库斯**：我在罗马尼亚长大……\
**Marcus**: I grew up in Romania ...

**小贩Ⅰ**：噢，我来自波斯尼亚和黑塞哥维那——反正咱们就是“同乡”了！\
**Vendor I**: Oh, I'm from Bosnia and Herzegovina ... That makes us friends, since we're both from somewhere-nia! Gahaha!

**卡卡尼亚**：你也要注意安全，伊里奇。要是遇到了卫兵可就麻烦了！你的许可证一定还没签发。\
**Kakania**: Be careful on the streets these days, Illich. You could be in trouble too if the guards catch you! After all, you haven't got a license.

**马库斯**：咦？你们没有许可证吗？\
**Marcus**: Eh? You don't?

**小贩Ⅰ**：嚯，我们当然没有了！听听它的条件，“三代以上的神秘术安全使用担保……”——我一出生就在卖货了，连妈妈的妈妈都没见过哩。\
**Vendor I**: Oh, of course not! Have you read the requirements? "Records of the safe use of arcane skills within three generations" ... I was born in the streets, I don't even know who my grandmother was.

**小贩Ⅰ**：这都算了，担保历来是最好造假的。可现在你要是在维也纳申请许可证，就得经过中央政府签发。\
**Vendor I**: And the records aren't the hard part to get around. If you're applying in Vienna, the license has to be issued by the central government.

**小贩Ⅰ**：不是奥地利政府，也不是匈牙利政府——是那个夹在它们中间的中央政府。\
**Vendor I**: It's not an Austrian problem, nor a Hungarian problem. The central government sits in the middle ...

**小贩Ⅰ**：而这就是最难的一步，从没人能稳妥地理清这里的区别。哪里是皇帝的，哪里是国王的，哪里是皇帝-国王的……\
**Vendor I**: ... and no official has any idea of what's what—should this be the Kaiser's concern? Or the König's? Or both?

**小贩Ⅰ**：你要是照章办事，就会发现自己上了大当啦！回过神来，就会被未知的咒术困在这里，束手束脚，动弹不得。除非拿出点闪闪发光的克朗润滑一下……\
**Vendor I**: You'd be the biggest fool to listen and follow these broken rules! Stuck in the system, nowhere to go ... unless you work the magic of krones ...

**马库斯**：……如果没有神秘术许可证，会怎么办？\
**Marcus**: ... What happens if we don't have an arcanum license?

**小贩Ⅰ**：噢，那就刺激了。\
**Vendor I**: Oh, you'll love this.

**小贩Ⅰ**：你可能被拘留三天，也可能被判刑十年。也可能你被判了十年，法院却忘了通知你。\
**Vendor I**: Who knows. You could get 3 days in detention, or maybe 10 years in prison. Even if you are sentenced to prison, they might forget to bring you in.

**小贩Ⅰ**：又或者你实在技艺高超，正适合通过一场先进的外科切除手术，来验证理性对神秘学的压倒性胜利……\
**Vendor I**: Or, if you're an outstanding citizen who can shed your arcanum during your human re-education, you might get to have a nice life—without a license that is.

**小贩Ⅰ**：这里的制度可比神秘术随机多了，咱们的机会还是相当大的！\
**Vendor I**: Our justice system is much more unpredictable than the arcanists'. We still have a fair chance of getting away!

**卡卡尼亚**：可以了，伊里奇。\
**Kakania**: Very informative, Illich.

卡卡尼亚清了清嗓子，仍有些戒备地使了个眼色。\
Kakania clears her throat, still somewhat guarded, and flashes out a meaningful glance.

**小贩Ⅰ**：哦，好的，好的……再见了，卡卡尼亚和——政府的小姐，就当我什么都没说过！\
**Vendor I**: Oh, well then ... See you, Kakania and Ms. Foundation. Forget I said anything!

**马库斯**：他们是……？\
**Marcus**: They are ...?

**卡卡尼亚**：一些神秘学家孩子，我很惊讶您竟然不清楚这些。这个国家就是有这样的处境。维也纳可不是所有事物都像环城大道的建筑和绅士街【Herrengasse】那样辉煌。\
**Kakania**: Some arcanist kids on the streets. I'm surprised you know nothing about them. The country has changed, lady, and not everything in Vienna is as decent and sumptuous as the buildings on the Ring Road and Herrengasse.

她语气里带了一点点讥讽。\
Her tone belies a hint of sarcasm.

**卡卡尼亚**：我很感谢您的帮助，政府小姐，不过目前我也同样帮助了您——被卫兵发现对你们来说也不是那么好摆平的，不是吗？咱们扯平了！\
**Kakania**: I'm thankful for your help, Ms. Foundation, but so far I have returned the favor—you don't want the guards either, do you? We're even.

**卡卡尼亚**：所以您来找我究竟是为了什么？\
**Kakania**: So can you tell me why you're here?

**卡卡尼亚**：噢，我知道了。是卡尔先生叫你们来找我要行医许可证的，可您好歹也休息两天吧！\
**Kakania**: Oh, I see. Mr. Karl sent you, didn't he? Because I don't have a psychiatrist's license. Can't you people give me a break?

**卡卡尼亚**：以先祖的名义发誓，我做的是百分之百的神秘学营生，绝没有一丁点和科学以及医学沾边的成分！\
**Kakania**: I swear on my ancestors, I'm doing this entirely the arcanist way. It has nothing to do with human science!

她提出了疑问，却并没给回答的空隙。卡卡尼亚凑近了马库斯，怀疑地推了推眼镜。\
She poses a question but leaves no room for an answer. Leaning closer to Marcus, she pushes her glasses up with suspicion.

**卡卡尼亚**：难道你们不睡觉的吗？难道你们没有个人生活的吗？这个月已经是第十次了，上帝在工作六天后还会休息一天哩！\
**Kakania**: Don't you people ever sleep? Do you not have a life? This is the tenth time this month, even God rests after working six days in a row!

**卡卡尼亚**：我有世袭的神秘术使用许可，这没什么不光彩的，收费也很公道，从没有哪位顾客来投诉我……\
**Kakania**: I have an arcanum license inherited from my family, it's nothing to be ashamed of. My fees are reasonable, no one's ever complained ...

**马库斯**：不，呃，卡卡尼亚小姐，这是巧合……我……呃……我只是听说您是一位心理医生……\
**Marcus**: No, um, Ms. Kakania, this is really coincidental ... I ... Err ... I just happened to know that you are a psychiatrist ...

**卡卡尼亚**：啊？！那又怎样，难道心理学如今被承认为医学了吗？\
**Kakania**: Hm? So? Are psychiatrists considered doctors now?

要在如此快速的跑题节奏中进行体面的敷衍实在是难如登天。\
Maintaining her barriers of politeness against the rapid topic changes feels like holding a smile in a hailstorm.

马库斯欲哭无泪，只得拼命在心里背诵《外勤派遣手册》。\
On the verge of tears, Marcus desperately falls back to the Field Mission Manual.

**马库斯**：我想这里好像有一些误会……我们——我不是来检查您许可证的。\
**Marcus**: I think there's been a misunderstanding. We-I'm not here to check your credentials.

**卡卡尼亚**：那你们是想……？\
**Kakania**: Then what?

**马库斯**：唔，是这样的……您自称卡卡尼亚，可是，我知道您的本名叫克拉拉……\
**Marcus**: So, you call yourself Kakania, but I know your first name is Klara ...

**卡卡尼亚**：噢，没想到基金会也有我的读者——这真叫人快活！\
**Kakania**: Oh, I didn't know the Foundation staff reads my work. How very flattering!

**卡卡尼亚**：是的，我是克拉拉！但是政府小姐，您不觉得这个名字很风趣吗？海因里希——噢，他是我的一位朋友，他给了我一本书，使我受益匪浅。\
**Kakania**: Yes, I'm Klara. But Ms. Foundation, don't you think Kakania is an intriguing name? Heinrich—who is a friend of mine—gave me a book which greatly inspired me.

**马库斯**：……！\
**Marcus**: ...!

**卡卡尼亚**：我们所在的国家正如这个名字一样——既是又是，既有又有，无处可寻，又无处不在！\
**Kakania**: Our country is just like that name. It both is, and isn't; it both has, and has not. If you look for it, it can't be found. Yet if you stop looking, it's everywhere.

**卡卡尼亚**：瞧瞧这片土地吧！\
**Kakania**: Look at this country, my friend!

**卡卡尼亚**：鳞次栉比的金色方块，上面缀满了漂亮的卷草纹，摞得这样高、这样巧妙……\
**Kakania**: The sumptuous buildings rise so high ...

**卡卡尼亚**：——掩盖了波西米亚黑麦田，遮住了亚得里亚海东岸的浪花，又将神秘术制造的焰火挡得严严实实！\
**Kakania**: that the people in power never have to lay eyes on the rye farmers of Bohemia, the immigrants from the east coast of Adriatic Sea, or on the arcanists!

**卡卡尼亚**：怎么会有浓烟在工业区遮天蔽日呢？怎么会有不温暖的房屋呢？咖啡馆里的人一定都是热爱舞步，而非交不起供暖的钱。\
**Kakania**: How could there possibly be smog choking the industrial area? How could there possibly be cold houses in the winter? The coffee house is definitely filled with people who love to dance, and not with those who can't afford the heat, oh no.

**卡卡尼亚**：这里没有官僚，没有歧视，没有贫穷！只有人文的、自由的一切。\
**Kakania**: Surely there's no bureaucracy, no discrimination, no poverty here. This is a city of humanism and freedom, oh yes.

**卡卡尼亚**：“卡卡尼亚”——是K.K.【帝国-皇室的】，又是K.U.K.【帝国及皇室的】，还是——“Shitland”！哈哈哈，再没有比这更精准的概括了。\
**Kakania**: Kakania ... "kaiserlich-königlich," or "kaiserlich und königlich," and ... "Caca-nia," the s**tland! Hahaha, there's no better name for this country.

**马库斯**：这么说，您确实拿到了那本书，从朋友那里……\
**Marcus**: So then, you did get that book, from a friend ...

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**马库斯**：这是个好机会……！我身上还有一根霍夫曼女士留下的“蛛尾巴”。\
**Marcus**: Now's my chance. I still have one "Spider Tail" Madam Hofmann left me.

**马库斯**：如果能趁机留在卡卡尼亚小姐身上——或者她的居所的话……！\
**Marcus**: If I can find a chance to leave the Spider Tail on her ... Or in her place ...

年轻助手缓慢地深呼了一口气。\
The young assistant takes a deep breath.

**马库斯**：我……很感兴趣，您可以带我去看看它吗？\
**Marcus**: I ... I'm intrigued by the book. Can I see it?

**？？？**：——以上就是来自委外合约人才管理组织塞梅尔维斯分队的交接汇报。请知悉，霍夫曼女士。\
**???**: This concludes the report by Semmelweis of the Field Agent Administration. Please confirm, Madam Hofmann.

一处静谧的角落。霍夫曼握着通讯器，眉头微微皱紧。\
In the corner, Hofmann holds her communicator out with brow furrowed.

**霍夫曼**：……好的，我这边已经收到。\
**Hofmann**: Yes, report received.

**？？？**：哈哈，这句话只是例行公事，格蕾塔。你怎么还是这样严肃？\
**???**: Haha, why so serious, Greta? That was just routine.

**霍夫曼**：……真羡慕你还能笑得如此轻松。这么紧急地将你们调离维也纳，想必那里的情况也不容乐观。\
**Hofmann**: And I envy your lightheartedness and optimism. They got you out of Vienna on such short notice, I can only imagine that it must have been difficult for you as well.

**霍夫曼**：而且，据你发来的信息……帝国在这样短的时间内发生了这么多桩刺杀案。这对临界点来说不是个好消息，塞梅尔维斯。\
**Hofmann**: According to your intel, the Empire's had too many assassinations in a short period of time. This is not good for the Critical Point, Semmelweis.

**塞梅尔维斯**：总是要保持一个好心态的——除此之外，我们又能怎么办呢？\
**Semmelweis**: At least try to stay in a good mood. What else can we do?

**塞梅尔维斯**：除此之外，格蕾塔，我这边还有一些消息要向你汇报——我们的交接太匆忙，新抵达的成员还没有获得这些一手信息。\
**Semmelweis**: Aside from that, Greta, I have more to tell you. I was pulled out of Vienna overnight and I didn't have time to brief the new squad there.

**塞梅尔维斯**：你也知道，流程太过冗长，我暂时只能以个人名义告知你。\
**Semmelweis**: You know, it takes ages to get through the briefing process. I might as well just tell you now, personally.

**塞梅尔维斯**：维也纳很可能有一位曾经跨越过“暴雨”的神秘学家。\
**Semmelweis**: There could be an arcanist who has crossed the "Storm," and is now in Vienna.

**霍夫曼**：……你说什么？有这个人的具体信息吗？\
**Hofmann**: What did you say? Do we know more about this arcanist?

**塞梅尔维斯**：目前已知他的名字是“海因里希”。我们和原驻柏林小组汇合时发现了这件事，但时间不允许我们核实。\
**Semmelweis**: We only know his name is Heinrich. We learned about this from the Berlin squad when we met up here, but had no time to verify.

**霍夫曼**：……明白了，后续就交给我们吧。\
**Hofmann**: I see. Leave the rest to us.

**塞梅尔维斯**：如果消息确凿，他应该是在第六次“暴雨”时前往柏林，并在那里躲过了1913年的“暴雨”。然后在66年、29年的“暴雨”后……\
**Semmelweis**: If true, he traveled to Berlin during the sixth "Storm" and survived the 1913 "Storm" there. And after the 1966 "Storm," and the one in 1929 ...

**霍夫曼**：时代又回到了1913年。对所有越过了第六次“暴雨”的神秘学家来说，这都是无比令人振奋的消息。\
**Hofmann**: And now it's 1913 for the second time. For all the arcanists who crossed the sixth "Storm," this is exciting news.

**塞梅尔维斯**：——嗯哼，他们的时代又回来了。\
**Semmelweis**: Mmhmm. Their time has returned.

**霍夫曼**：我很熟知这种心态，但这很可能只是时间在乱序运动中随机到了两个相同的年份。\
**Hofmann**: I understand the excitement, but perhaps time, in its chaotic fashion, has inadvertently returned to the same year.

**霍夫曼**：我明白了，塞梅尔维斯，这条消息价值极高，我会尽快——\
**Hofmann**: I hear you, Semmelweis. This is valuable information, I'll let the ...

**霍夫曼**：……！\
**Hofmann**: ...!

**塞梅尔维斯**：格蕾塔？你那边怎么了？\
**Semmelweis**: Greta? Are you still there?

**霍夫曼**：抱歉，我要中断通话了……\
**Hofmann**: Sorry, I have to go ...

**霍夫曼**：我留在马库斯身上的“蛛尾巴”有异常的神秘术反应，那不是她使用的术式……她那边出事了。\
**Hofmann**: Something's wrong with the "Spider Tail" I left on Marcus. This is not her ritual ... Something's happened.

音效-二人走路声，钥匙开锁声

**卡卡尼亚**：真叫我意外，马库斯小姐，您对我们这个时代的文化流行竟然如此了解！\
**Kakania**: I'm surprised, Ms. Marcus, you know so much about this era!

**卡卡尼亚**：我以为基金会里要么是腐朽的官僚，要么是冰冷的呆子……噢，您去过分离派之家了？您喜欢那儿吗？遗憾的是那本书没在那里……\
**Kakania**: I thought the Foundation was nothing but bureaucrats and bookworms. Oh, have you been to the Secession Building? Did you like it? Shame that book isn't there.

卡卡尼亚终于摸到了钥匙。\
Kakania finally finds the key.

**卡卡尼亚**：请进！希望您不介意这里的混乱。相比帝国的行政系统，它还是很整洁的……\
**Kakania**: Please, come in! Forgive the mess. I must say that it is at least more orderly than the administration of the Empire.

**马库斯**：好，好的。\
**Marcus**: Than-thank you.

比起诊所，这里更像是一个工作室。\
The room resembles a studio more so than a clinic.

房间里四处散落着未完成的画作、颜料、舞台布景道具和海报。\
The scene is scattered about with unfinished paintings, dried paints, stage props, and posters.

以及镜子，很多面镜子。\
And mirrors. Many, many mirrors.

**卡卡尼亚**：噢！这些舞台道具是海因里希放在这的，他在柏林真是学了不少好东西回来！\
**Kakania**: These are stage props, Heinrich left them here. He certainly learned some useful things in Berlin.

**卡卡尼亚**：您随便坐。我去给您倒杯茶，再帮您找找那本书……\
**Kakania**: Make yourself comfortable. I'll get you some tea, and look for the book.

**马库斯**：不了，卡卡尼亚小姐，我还需要回分部报到。\
**Marcus**: Please don't bother, Ms. Kakania! I won't stay long, I have to go back to the branch soon.

**马库斯**：我只需要确认您拥有那本书就好了，不是从他人口中复述，而是亲手……\
**Marcus**: I just need to confirm that you have that book with you ...

**马库斯**：唔！\
**Marcus**: Ooh!

诊所里窗帘紧闭，镜子却强烈闪烁了一秒。\
The clinic's curtains are tightly drawn, blocking out the day, yet her mirrors flash with light for a second.

**马库斯**：是卡卡尼亚的神秘术？\
**Marcus**: Is this ... Kakania's arcane skill?

马库斯连忙抬手捂住眼睛，向门外退了一步。\
Marcus quickly covers her eyes with her hands, stepping back toward the door.

卡卡尼亚快活的声音从一边传来。\
Kakania's cheerful voice rings from the other side.

**卡卡尼亚**：……噢，瞧您！政府小姐，别太紧张，这只是个无伤大雅的安保措施，平时我还会收钱哩！\
**Kakania**: Ms. Foundation, it's okay! Just a little trick I use to ensure my personal safety. I usually even charge for this!

**卡卡尼亚**：“请看看这面镜子，它会映出您内心的光景”……神秘学家千年不变的小把戏，从罗马帝国时代传承至今。\
**Kakania**: "Look into the mirror, which reflects your inner world" ... This trick has been used by arcanists for thousands of years. When it was first used, the Roman Emperors still ruled this land.

**卡卡尼亚**：说到这个，政府小姐——\
**Kakania**: Speaking of which, Ms. Foundation ...

**卡卡尼亚**：您是怎么发现那把手枪被做了手脚的？是您的神秘术吗？\
**Kakania**: How did you know that the pistol was tampered with? Your arcane skill?

也许是心理暗示——镜子的闪光愈发晃眼。\
Though it might only be some sort of trick of psychology—the mirror's glare becomes increasingly blinding.

**马库斯**：……唔，不能看向镜子！\
**Marcus**: ... Um, don't look at the mirror!

调查员戒备起来，她握紧提灯，在第一时间做好了战斗准备。\
The investigator braces herself as she grips the lamp, ready for combat at a moment's notice.

卡卡尼亚的语气依然和缓，仿佛是在抚慰自己的有应激创伤的病人。\
Kakania's tone remains gentle, as if soothing one of her patients.

**卡卡尼亚**：我对此非常感兴趣，请放心——我会控制好力道的。\
**Kakania**: I am curious. No need to be alarmed—I'll treat you gently.

## 6TH-09 门与门之间 / Between the Doors

**马库斯**：呼……她制造的光学影像很逼真，但不是完美的。\
**Marcus**: Phew. The reflections she created were real enough, but not perfect.

**马库斯**：镜中的虚影没有影子，没有呼吸的颤动，最重要的是，没有她吵闹的热情和过剩的小动作。\
**Marcus**: The reflections had neither shadows nor breath. Most importantly, they didn't have her passion and subtle movements.

**马库斯**：这些细节让我读到了真实——她确实并不想伤害我。也许这的确只是个神秘学小把戏……\
**Marcus**: I "read" the truth from these details ... She meant me no harm. Maybe it was just a little trick she was playing.

**马库斯**：呃，不过我——\
**Marcus**: But, I ...

助手平复了呼吸，望向地上的人影。\
She steadies her breath, looking down at the figure on the ground.

她不小心用了太大力道，卡卡尼亚仍躺在地上，用手扶着帽子。\
She inadvertently used too much force. Kakania is still on the ground, supporting her hat with one hand.

她的嘴唇难以置信地颤抖着，像是震惊于自己的失败。\
Her lips tremble incredulously, shocked by her own failure.

**卡卡尼亚**：……这真是，这真是……\
**Kakania**: This is ... That was ...

她扑向马库斯，后者再次条件反射地缩回了手。\
She lunges toward Marcus, who reflexively withdraws her hand.

**卡卡尼亚**：果然同我猜得一样，您的神秘术如此特殊，仅是观察表象就能发现内在……\
**Kakania**: I knew it! Your arcane skill is incredibly unique, you can discover what's on the inside by observing what's on the outside.

**卡卡尼亚**：——您一定是生来就要成为心理医生的！\
**Kakania**: You are born to be a psychiatrist!

**马库斯**：——啊？\
**Marcus**: Huh?

她紧紧地攥住了马库斯的手，那模样像是见到了失散多年的亲人。\
She clings tightly to Marcus's hand, as if she's found a long-lost relative.

**卡卡尼亚**：天啊，您看起来这么小，还这么瘦……连外套都不合身，他们怎么能虐待儿童呢？\
**Kakania**: Look at you, you are so tiny, and they gave you this big coat. How can they do this to a child?!

**卡卡尼亚**：不如这样，您辞了这份工作，来我的诊所当助手如何？您的观察力和洞悉力，是我们这一行很需要的，因为我们的职责正是从只言片语和模糊不清中发掘事实……\
**Kakania**: How about you quit the Foundation and be my assistant? Your perception would be invaluable in this line of work. After all, we search for truth from foggy memories and vague descriptions for a living ...

**马库斯**：那，那个……书……\
**Marcus**: Ah, Miss ... The book ...

马库斯礼貌而僵硬地试图抽回手。\
Marcus attempts to withdraw her hand, politely but stiffly.

但卡卡尼亚热情不改。\
Kakania's enthusiasm remains unchanged.

**卡卡尼亚**：先不要去管那本书了！这是一门富有生命力的新兴学科，您这样的年轻人一定会感兴趣的！……要不我们去里面坐下，瞧我，都忘了给您倒杯茶！\
**Kakania**: Forget the book! A new academic field is opening its doors to you! Let's go inside. Oh dear, I forgot your tea!

**马库斯**：天啊，她就像一只喋喋不休的绿色鹦鹉……\
**Marcus**: Gosh, she's babbling like a parrot.

音效-联络器

**马库斯**：啊……！是霍夫曼女士……！\
**Marcus**: Ah ...! It's Madam Hofmann!

**马库斯**：您——\
**Marcus**: Ma'am.

**霍夫曼**：马库斯，“蛛尾巴”告诉我你的方向了——怎么这么远，你在哪里，为什么会有神秘术波动？！\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, the "Spider Tail" has shown me your direction. How did you get that far? What is that place? An arcane fluctuation?!

**马库斯**：我在和目标……我和卡卡尼亚小姐在一起，在她的诊所——我没事，调查很顺利！您——\
**Marcus**: I'm with the targe- ... Ms. Kakania. In her clinic. I'm safe, the investigation's going well! Ma'am!

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

**霍夫曼**：——在那里等着我！保护好自己，听到了吗？\
**Hofmann**: Stay where you are, I'm on my way! And take care of yourself, you hear me?

**马库斯**：呃，好……\
**Marcus**: Erm, yes, ma'am ...

音效-挂断

**卡卡尼亚**：那是您的上司吗？她可真严厉，我合理质疑基金会在非法雇佣未成年人——\
**Kakania**: Was that your supervisor? She sounds rather harsh. I do have to question the Foundation, hiring underage children and all ...

**马库斯**：……时间刚刚好！\
**Marcus**: ... Just in time!

马库斯用余光瞄着正在感慨的绿色女士，轻轻扑了下裙摆。几乎不可见的隐线落在了绿色织物上。\
Marcus glances at the doctor, who is now lost in thought, lightly flicking her skirt. An almost invisible thread lands on the green fabric.

**马库斯**：不，霍夫曼女士她……其实很温柔。\
**Marcus**: Well, actually, Madam Hofmann is ... very kind to me.

她抬起头，试图进一步转移医生的注意力。\
She lifts her head, trying to further divert the doctor's attention.

卡卡尼亚不置可否。\
Kakania remains unimpressed by her answer.

**卡卡尼亚**：总之，你也看到了——我、我的诊所、我的神秘术——我的一切已经向您展露无遗。或许这可以打消您的疑虑了，马库斯小姐！\
**Kakania**: Well, you have seen it all for yourself. Me, my clinic, my arcane skill—I showed you everything. Have they cleared up your doubts, Ms. Marcus?

**马库斯**：……我还有一个问题。\
**Marcus**: Just one more question.

**卡卡尼亚**：请说。\
**Kakania**: Please go ahead.

**马库斯**：关于……“魔圈”。\
**Marcus**: About ... "The Circle."

**卡卡尼亚**：噢？难道您煞有介事跑来，就是为了这个吗？\
**Kakania**: Eh? Did you go through all this trouble just for that?

卡卡尼亚夸张地抬起手，在软椅上坐下。\
Kakania dramatically raises her hand, settling down into her soft chair.

**卡卡尼亚**：那您真是问对人了——我就是“魔圈”的创始人！\
**Kakania**: You could have asked me earlier. I am the founder of "The Circle."

**马库斯**：什——什么？！\
**Marcus**: Wh-what?!

马库斯刚把热茶放在嘴边，就险些被烫了个满怀。\
Marcus nearly scalds herself with the hot tea as she brings it up to her lips.

**卡卡尼亚**：您为什么这样激动？您也是我们的仰慕者不成？\
**Kakania**: You're awfully excited. Are you an admirer?

**卡卡尼亚**：开玩笑的——它只是我们几个常在一起喝咖啡的朋友，出于兴趣创立的小团体，完全合理合法，没有任何邪恶！\
**Kakania**: Joking. It's just a little group a couple of friends started out of interest. Completely legal, nothing nefarious.

**卡卡尼亚**：我们致力于改善维也纳神秘学家的处境——比基金会更关心。\
**Kakania**: We're committed to changing the arcanists' current situation ... more committed than the Foundation.

**卡卡尼亚**：我们马上会开展一场公益性质的画展，将所有募捐所得用于帮助下层神秘学家取得许可证——这本该是你们的工作！\
**Kakania**: There will be a non-profit exhibit soon, and all donations will help lower class arcanists get their license, which should have been your responsibility!

她的话语骤然尖锐，又在意识到谈话对象后止住话头。\
Her words are sharply pointed, only to stop abruptly as she recalls the identity of their target.

**卡卡尼亚**：噢，抱歉，职业病犯了。我应该招揽您，而不是攻击您的背景。\
**Kakania**: Oh, sorry, I get carried away. I should persuade you to join us, not attack your current job.

马库斯摇了摇头，所幸她并不介意这个时代的纠纷。\
Marcus shakes her head, feeling all-together fortunate now to not be involved in the disputes of this era.

**马库斯**：那幅要展出的画……是《拯救》吗？\
**Marcus**: And the painting in this exhibit ... will be The Salvation?

**卡卡尼亚**：对了，您去过分离派之家——那的确，谁都会注意到它！\
**Kakania**: That's right, you've been to the Secession Building, and that's a masterpiece which will be hard to miss.

**卡卡尼亚**：那是西奥菲尔生前所绘的最后一幅画——以黄金岛为主题绘制的。\
**Kakania**: That was Theophil's final piece of work, the Golden Isle being its subject.

她垂下头，给茶杯添上新的茶水。\
She lowers her head a little while refilling her cup with fresh tea.

**卡卡尼亚**：那可真是个不得了的大新闻……\
**Kakania**: It was big news at the time ...

**卡卡尼亚**：爱琴海上的隐秘岛屿，古老而独立的神秘学家聚落，奇特的洋流和磁场，只存在于传说里的神秘动物，以及现代的阴影对它的迫近……\
**Kakania**: The island hidden from all people in the Aegean Sea, the ancient arcanist settlement, the strange current and magnetic field around it, the animals only heard in stories, and the shadow of modern society cast upon it ...

**卡卡尼亚**：当然了，我也是道听途说。人们说什么的都有……军事基地，神话王国，天启神迹……\
**Kakania**: Well, those are just hearsay. People have all kinds of speculations about it ... A military base, a mythical kingdom, the apocalypse ...

**卡卡尼亚**：您们——才是对它最了解的人。\
**Kakania**: The Foundation knows it better than any of us.

“——嗒。”\
*clink*

卡卡尼亚放下茶杯，她的目光空前冷静。\
Kakania sets down the teacup, her focus calm but impassioned.

**卡卡尼亚**：马库斯小姐，我已经把我知道的都告诉了您。如果您信任我，我希望您也告诉我一件事。\
**Kakania**: Ms. Marcus, I've told you everything I know. If you trust me, please tell me one thing.

**马库斯**：……抱歉，卡卡尼亚小姐，我不能……\
**Marcus**: I'm sorry, Ms. Kakania, I can't ...

**卡卡尼亚**：——那座岛上是否真的有我们的同胞？如果有，他们又如何在时代的洪流中保全自己？\
**Kakania**: Are there really our people on that island? If so, how did they protect themselves in these changing times?

**卡卡尼亚**：我只是想问这个问题！作为一个幸存的神秘学家！作为一个人！\
**Kakania**: This is my only question. As an arcanist, and as a human being.

**马库斯**：……！\
**Marcus**: ...!

**卡卡尼亚**：如今欧洲的军火公司将巴尔干半岛当成试验场，在上面试验他们的新式武器——那座岛也是因此被发现的。\
**Kakania**: The arms companies are turning the Balkan Peninsula into a proving ground for their new weapons—that was how they discovered this island.

**卡卡尼亚**：您隶属于官方机构，您一定知道些什么。拜托了，我只是想知道——\
**Kakania**: You work for the authorities. You must know something. Please, I just want to know if ...

**卡卡尼亚**：在世界上的这个角落，是否还有我们的同胞在默默经受着苦难，无法发声，也无法得到任何帮助。\
**Kakania**: If there's any more of us in this world, suffering, silenced, and helpless.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

卡卡尼亚的激情在对方漫长的沉默中渐渐熄灭。\
Kakania's passion dims over the prolonged silence.

**卡卡尼亚**：好吧，当然，您毕竟还是基金会的职员——我不该问的，抱歉。\
**Kakania**: Fine. You work for the Foundation, after all. I shouldn't have asked.

**卡卡尼亚**：只是我希望，至少，至少在这样无药可救的官僚体系中，仍能有一位清醒的人。不要认为那里只有一群精神失常的疯子……\
**Kakania**: It's just that I'm hoping for at least one rational person in such an irredeemable bureaucracy. Someone who doesn't think it's just a bunch of deranged lunatics over there.

**卡卡尼亚**：一如神秘学家这个群体千百年来承受的污名。\
**Kakania**: ... Which is a stigma the arcanists have carried around for centuries.

**马库斯**：——不是的，我们不是疯子！\
**Marcus**: … No, we are not crazy!

**卡卡尼亚**：……！\
**Kakania**: ...!

她攒紧了衣角，颤抖地抬起头来。\
She clenches the fabric of her dress, lifting her head in a trembling outburst.

**马库斯**：我，我个人也认为岛上的神秘学家并非疯子！\
**Marcus**: I, I don't think the arcanists on the island are crazy either!

**卡卡尼亚**：马库斯小姐？！\
**Kakania**: Ms. Marcus?

**马库斯**：……卡卡尼亚医生，我知道既定的不愉快难以消除，但并非所有人都同意卡尔先生的做法。\
**Marcus**: Dr. Kakania, I know there has been discord and resentment between humans and arcanists, but not everyone is like Mr. Karl.

**马库斯**：我们来自基金会总部。那里有很多人和你们一样，正在为神秘学家的合法权益奔走。\
**Marcus**: We're from the headquarters, where many like you are fighting for the rights of arcanists.

**马库斯**：在关心同胞这一点上，我们没有根本的分歧。\
**Marcus**: When it comes to caring for our people, we're not so different there.

**马库斯**：维护神秘学家的权益，以及世界的和平和秩序……这正是基金会成立的初衷。现在，我们也在为此努力着。\
**Marcus**: That was what the Foundation was for. To defend the interests of the arcanists, and to keep the world safe and orderly. Till this day, we continue to strive for this goal.

心跳得很快。\
Her heart thumps hard in her chest.

她不该这么做的……可是，可是，她也做不到对这个问题视而不见。\
She shouldn't do this ... but, but, she can't ignore the question any longer either.

这或许也是值得的！她的“阅读”告诉她，这个盟友是值得的。她们没有根本上的分歧。\
Perhaps it's worth it! Her "reading" tells her that this is a worthwhile ally. They have had no fundamental disagreements between one another.

只是透露这一点无关紧要的信息的话……如果这样就能弥合立场上的鸿沟的话——\
Just this one insignificant piece of information ... if it might bridge the gap in their positions ...

时间变得漫长。\
Time stretches on.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：我真为这一切感到遗憾。\
**Kakania**: My sympathies for all that is happening.

**马库斯**：唔……？！\
**Marcus**: Erm?!

马库斯得到了一个拥抱。\
Marcus receives another embrace.

**卡卡尼亚**：如果您不是在基金会的话，我想我们能成为很好的朋友。\
**Kakania**: We could've been very good friends, if you weren't working for the Foundation.

**卡卡尼亚**：我知道您没有说谎——我不会错看年轻人心里燃烧的火焰。“魔圈”也是因此聚集在了一起。\
**Kakania**: I know you meant every word you said, I can see how you burned with passion. "The Circle" was founded for the same reason.

**卡卡尼亚**：但我也不会改变对既定机构的看法。\
**Kakania**: But I will not change my view on certain things.

**马库斯**：啊，那……\
**Marcus**: Ah ...

**卡卡尼亚**：不过我又想了想，朋友嘛，总是在哪里任职的都有……\
**Kakania**: But on second thought, I have friends working in all kinds of places ...

**卡卡尼亚**：我们的场地很开阔，酒水和点心也很充足，完全足够再站下一个新朋友。\
**Kakania**: We have a big house, plenty of wine and refreshments, there is more than enough room for a new friend.

**卡卡尼亚**：——我想邀请您明天来分离派之家，参加我们的开展仪式，马库斯小姐。\
**Kakania**: I would like to invite you to the Secession Building and to be present at the opening of the exhibit, Ms. Marcus.

**卡卡尼亚**：至于您说的话，我们可以之后再聊聊。\
**Kakania**: And we can talk more about what you said afterwards.

**马库斯**：……那太好了！\
**Marcus**: That'd be great!

**马库斯**：但是……我的导——我的“上司”——\
**Marcus**: But ... my ment- ... um, my supervisor ...

**卡卡尼亚**：唔，这确实不好处理。鉴于您的年纪确实需要一名监护人，在此之前又向我说了“她很温柔”……\
**Kakania**: Hmm, that is tricky. But a minor like you requires the presence of a guardian, and you told me that she's "kind" to you ...

**卡卡尼亚**：——好吧，如果您要带上她，我也不介意。毕竟这是法律。\
**Kakania**: Well, she can come with you. We must abide by the law, after all.

**卡卡尼亚**：亲眼目睹我们究竟是在做怎样的事业……也有助于消除你们对我们的误会。\
**Kakania**: It might help to clear up misunderstandings if she's there.

卡卡尼亚又给了马库斯一个拥抱。\
A hug comes once again.

**卡卡尼亚**：……好了，接下来我就得通知海因里希，告诉他我为何又发出去两张邀请函……\
**Kakania**: Alright, I have to inform Heinrich that we have two more guests coming ...

**卡卡尼亚**：啊，糟糕！\
**Kakania**: Oh, shoot!

**卡卡尼亚**：我接下来还有一场诊疗！我差点忘记了时间，很抱歉不能再和您多说几句——不，我知道您想问什么，关于患者的信息我是不会透露的！\
**Kakania**: I have an appointment today! I almost forgot the time. I have to go. I know what you're going to ask, but patient information is confidential!

卡卡尼亚自顾自地摇了摇手指，她的思维显然已经飘到了未来的诊疗上。\
Kakania idly wags her finger. Her thoughts seem to have drifted on to future treatments.

她匆匆盖上钢笔盖，将邀请函递给马库斯。\
She hastily caps her pen, handing the invitation to Marcus.

**卡卡尼亚**：那我便不留您了。再见了，可爱的政府小姐！\
**Kakania**: I shouldn't keep you any longer. See you soon, Ms. Foundation!

**卡卡尼亚**：——“魔圈”欢迎您的到来！\
**Kakania**: Welcome to "The Circle!"

敲门声轻轻响起。\
A gentle knock sounds at the door.

**马库斯**：噢！我，我这就走……谢谢您，卡卡尼亚小姐。\
**Marcus**: Oh, I, I should go ... Thank you, Ms. Kakania.

她转身匆匆离去，门适时地开启了。\
She turns and hurries away, the door opening just in time.

**伊索尔德**：……？\
**Isolde**: ...?

马库斯没有停下脚步，向着来人轻轻颔首。\
Marcus doesn't stop, nodding and gliding around the newcomer in a fast, fluid motion.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

## 6TH-10 内窥镜 / The Mind's Endoscope

两张邀请函，来自“魔圈”的发起人。\
Two invitations, from the founder of "The Circle," no less.

宝贵的机会，来之不易的线索。\
A precious opportunity—a rare and precious clue to the goings-on here.

霍夫曼女士摩挲着它的边缘，久久沉默。\
Hofmann caresses the edges, sinking into a long silence.

眼前的乖巧助手低着头，等待着一场雷暴。\
The obedient assistant looks off into the far distance, awaiting the impending storm.

**霍夫曼**：……你也知晓了信息。但根据基金会的章程，我需要再次告知：此次调查任务的主要目标更换为海因里希。\
**Hofmann**: ... You know what happened. But under the Foundation's regulations, I must reiterate that the primary subject of this investigation has been changed to Heinrich.

**霍夫曼**：这两张邀请函确实很有帮助，我会与委外合约小队联系，在明晚的沙龙上展开行动。一旦他的身份核实，就进行控制。\
**Hofmann**: These two invitations are very useful. I'll tell the Field Agent Squad to act tomorrow night. Once Heinrich's identity is verified, we will detain him in the exhibit.

**霍夫曼**：——但我必须提醒你，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: But I must remind you, Marcus.

**霍夫曼**：你今天的行为，严重违反了《外勤派遣手册》。我会把你的行为上报给总部。\
**Hofmann**: What you did today was a serious violation of the Field Mission Manual. And I have to report this to the headquarters.

**霍夫曼**：那座岛不属于这个时代，关于它的一切都是严格的机密，你越界了。\
**Hofmann**: That island is not of this era. Everything about it is strictly confidential. You have crossed a line.

导师语气严厉。\
The mentor's tone was of a stern reproach. Not so inconsequential anymore.

**马库斯**：……我明白……\
**Marcus**: ... Understood ...

马库斯脸色极度苍白，她尝试开了好几次口，都没能发出任何声音。\
Marcus's complexion turns deathly pale. Her mouth hangs open to speak several times but fails to make a sound.

如果不是靠着墙，她也许已经跌倒了。\
If not for the wall, she might well have fallen over.

**霍夫曼**：……我理解你的想法，我们确实非常需要接触这个青年团体。\
**Hofmann**: I know what you're thinking. We need to get closer to this group.

**霍夫曼**：你也许会觉得，比起维也纳分部的官僚，他们更接近我们总部的立场，可以友好地互相建立信任。\
**Hofmann**: You might think that their ideas are closer to those of the headquarters, and therefore easier to work with compared to the Vienna branch.

**马库斯**：嗯……？！\
**Marcus**: Umm ...?!

马库斯猛地抬起头，惊讶于自己得到了死刑缓期执行。\
Marcus finds herself surprised by her stay of execution.

**霍夫曼**：……但首先，我们并非只有卡卡尼亚一个情报获取来源。\
**Hofmann**: You must know that Kakania is not our only source of information.

霍夫曼别过脸，不去看向学徒过于高兴的眼神。\
Hofmann turns away, intentionally avoiding the overeager eyes of her apprentice.

**霍夫曼**：卡尔提供了名单。原则上，上面的每个人我们都可以接触。此外，基金会分部的人脉资源也能为我们所用。\
**Hofmann**: On the one hand, Karl has given us a list. In principle, everyone on this list is useful. On the other hand, the branch has its own connections too.

**霍夫曼**：更重要的是，人们并非如此简单地就能结为同党。\
**Hofmann**: More importantly, it takes more than a conversation over tea to get people on the same side of a conflict.

经验更丰富些的调查员叹了一口气，揉搓着自己的眉心。\
The experienced investigator sighs, rubbing her forehead.

**霍夫曼**：我担心的是你是否太过天真，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: I'm worried you are not ready for this, Marcus.

**霍夫曼**：因为有太多卑劣的罪恶打着崇高的名义进行，最残酷的暴行以最伟大的名号发生。\
**Hofmann**: There is too much wickedness out there dressed in the skin of kindness. The most horrible atrocities are always committed for the most seemingly justified reasons.

**霍夫曼**：即使是基金会总部，也存在着大量立场不同的人们的利益妥协和相互协商。\
**Hofmann**: Even at the headquarters, people are mired in power struggles and compromises.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**马库斯**：抱歉，是我想得太单纯了……\
**Marcus**: Sorry, ma'am, I was naive ...

**霍夫曼**：……决断你的行为是总部的事。如果你付出的风险切实取得了收获，也许他们会重新评估。\
**Hofmann**: It'll be the Foundation's judgment call. If the information you've gathered outweighs the risks, you may be treated leniently.

**霍夫曼**：马库斯，看看这条街道。\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, look at the street.

环城大道开阔，宁静，人来人往。\
The Ring Road has a feeling of tranquility despite the evening bustle.

**霍夫曼**：……你不是唯一一个想要“帮助”这份美好的人。我们为和平的志向而来，曾有过太多人想要避免一些必然的悲剧，然后目睹更大的悲剧在眼前诞生。\
**Hofmann**: You're not the only one who wants to contribute to this place and its people. We come for peace, and many before us have tried to prevent foreseeable tragedies, only to cause greater tragedies.

**霍夫曼**：条例不会凭空而生。尤其是《外勤派遣手册》里的条例——它们每一条的诞生都伴随着血或泪。\
**Hofmann**: The rules are there for a reason. Nothing in the manual was written out of imagination. Every one of them came from a mistake of the past.

**霍夫曼**：我们所处的位置只能是“旁观者”。\
**Hofmann**: We are only here to observe.

衣着端庄的公民们享受着自己黄昏的散步时光。\
Many well-dressed citizens pass by, enjoying their sunset strolls.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**霍夫曼**：而这里是1914年的维也纳，是火药桶的引信，是混乱时代的临界点。\
**Hofmann**: This is Vienna in 1914. The birthplace of an enduring war and chaos, the Critical Point.

**霍夫曼**：它就像一个高压泵，只要烟卷末端的一丝火星就可能炸开，我们无法估计自己的行为会产生怎样的结果。\
**Hofmann**: It is a powder keg, and the slightest spark will set it off. Any action we take could have unfathomable consequences.

**霍夫曼**：因此，我们能做的就是尽可能地谨小慎微。\
**Hofmann**: That's why we advise extreme caution.

**霍夫曼**：这是我们唯一对时代负责的方式。\
**Hofmann**: This is our responsibility to this era.

马库斯顺着导师的手望向远方。\
Marcus follows her mentor's hand, gazing into the distance.

这是她第一次如此仔细地端详这座城市。\
For the first time, she scrutinizes the city ahead of her in detail.

这里有无数种生活、无数种可能、无数新思想和旧思想的碰撞……\
Here, countless lives, possibilities, and thoughts new and old collide ...

难道这一切都会在瞬间终结于雨幕吗？\
Would all this end in an instant beneath a curtain of rain?

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

马库斯沉默地低下头去。\
Marcus nods, searching out a word of affirmation.

**马库斯**：……我明白了，霍夫曼女士。\
**Marcus**: ... I understand completely, Madam Hofmann.

**马库斯**：我不会再犯下这样的过错。\
**Marcus**: I won't make the same mistake again.

人们仍在履行自己的生活轨迹。\
Away from the Ring Road, others continue on their life's trajectory.

卡卡尼亚的诊所里，一场稍有不同的诊疗正要开始。\
In Kakania's clinic, a slightly unorthodox treatment is about to begin.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德小姐？怎么了，为何您的眉头皱得这样的紧？\
**Kakania**: Isolde? You look sad and pale, what happened?

**卡卡尼亚**：是剧团的事又让您烦心了吗？还是那些可憎的官僚又来骚扰您？\
**Kakania**: Did something happen in the troupe? Or did those dreadful officials come back?

**伊索尔德**：不，让您见笑了，我只是……有些担心。\
**Isolde**: No. I'm just ... a bit worried.

**伊索尔德**：倒是您……您竟然为了我的诊疗，去和施瓦茨医生决斗。天呐，还好您没有什么大碍，不然我非得心碎终生不可……\
**Isolde**: You ... you entered a duel for my sake. Dear lord, the thought of you getting hurt breaks my heart.

**卡卡尼亚**：噢不！是海因里希告诉了您吗？他可真是多嘴！\
**Kakania**: Did Heinrich tell you that? He needs to keep his mouth shut.

**卡卡尼亚**：千万别感到负担，伊索尔德小姐。我是为了自己的职业伦理去和施瓦茨发起决斗的，我后果自负。\
**Kakania**: Don't worry about me, Isolde. I fought for the ethics of the profession, and I'm ready to bear the consequences of my actions.

**卡卡尼亚**：他将用于治疗的催眠技术出卖给军方用作审讯，是一个十足的人渣！\
**Kakania**: That scum sold the secrets of hypnosis to the military. It's a treatment, not a means of interrogation!

**卡卡尼亚**：可结果而言，决斗并未开始，我也好端端站在这！这多亏了基金会的那位小姐。\
**Kakania**: In the end, all is well! The duel didn't happen, and I'm here, unharmed. All thanks to that young missy from the Foundation.

**伊索尔德**：……基金会的那位小姐……\
**Isolde**: That young missy from the Foundation ...

**伊索尔德**：是刚刚离开这儿的那位吗？我来时，在门口遇到了她。\
**Isolde**: The lady who just left? I bumped into her at the door.

**卡卡尼亚**：哦？您见到她了？\
**Kakania**: So you've seen her.

**伊索尔德**：我在分离派之家见过她，当时您不在那儿。\
**Isolde**: She was at the Secession Building. You weren't there.

**伊索尔德**：她给您制造麻烦了吗？您曾说，基金会那边因医疗许可的问题纠缠您过一段时间……\
**Isolde**: Did she give you any trouble? You told me that the Foundation was after you for a while because you didn't have a license.

**伊索尔德**：我可以帮助您，医生。我可以拜托卡尔先生……\
**Isolde**: I can help you, doctor. I can ask Mr. Karl to ...

**卡卡尼亚**：嗯？不用，完全不用！她——她是我刚刚结识的朋友！\
**Kakania**: Eh? No need for that. We only just became friends.

**伊索尔德**：……朋友？\
**Isolde**: Friends?

**伊索尔德**：……您总是不愿让我为您与基金会的官员交谈，可您如今却又结识了基金会的朋友？\
**Isolde**: You told me to stay away from the Foundation staff, but now you're making friends with them ...

**卡卡尼亚**：噢，她是不一样的，伊索尔德！而且我与她的结识完全是巧合。我给了她沙龙邀请函，之后你也会见到她的，我觉得你们也能成为不错的朋友。\
**Kakania**: Oh, she's different, dear Isolde! We met by chance. I gave her an invitation to the exhibit, so you'll see her there. I think you two will become best friends.

**卡卡尼亚**：要解释那就说来话长了，当务之急还是您的诊疗。这都是些不重要的小事！\
**Kakania**: It would take all day to tell you everything. You're here for treatment. Let's not waste time on unimportant things.

**伊索尔德**：……不重要的？好……\
**Isolde**: Unimportant? Alright ...

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

卡卡尼亚咳嗽了一声，试图让自己显得更加职业化一点。\
Kakania coughs, trying to revert to her more professional guise.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德小姐，您是我的朋友，照理来说，我本不想给您看诊……\
**Kakania**: You're a personal friend, Isolde, so I didn't want to give you therapy in the first place ...

**伊索尔德**：……是……我没有资格吗？\
**Isolde**: Be-because I'm not good enough, or sick enough, to be your patient?

**卡卡尼亚**：不，不，是我没有资格！我半路出家，没有行医执照，未能从医学院毕业，这都是客观事实，而您对我又如此重要。\
**Kakania**: No no no, because I'm not good enough. I wasn't properly trained, I don't have a medical license, or a degree! This is the cold, hard truth, and you're too important a friend to me.

**卡卡尼亚**：可是我实在看不下去您再去求助那些庸医了……\
**Kakania**: But I can no longer watch you suffer from the horrible treatments those quacks gave you.

**卡卡尼亚**：至少我能为自己的职业道德担保，不漫天要价，不在问诊中兜售小商品，也绝不打着手术的名义进行人体实验！\
**Kakania**: I may not have a license, but I have the knowledge and ethics that they don't. I never overcharge my treatment, nor sell unnecessary things to the patient, and I will never experiment on my patients!

**伊索尔德**：……呵呵。\
**Isolde**: Heh heh.

**卡卡尼亚**：您笑了？很好，看来您也认为，我对他们的抨击是中肯的！\
**Kakania**: Your smile. So you agree with what I said about those psychiatrists and doctors!

**卡卡尼亚**：——那让我们开始吧！\
**Kakania**: Okay, then let's get to it!

卡卡尼亚高兴地旋转着钢笔，翻开诊疗本的一页。\
Kakania spins her pen in an excited twirl, flipping open her treatment book.

**卡卡尼亚**：西格蒙德·弗洛伊德医生曾经写过，是我们内心对本能的遏制导致了歇斯底里症。\
**Kakania**: Dr. Sigmund Freud wrote that repression of desires is one of the primary causes of hysteria.

**卡卡尼亚**：您需要一次解放。我将通过话语去引导您进行回忆，您只需信任我，将其倾诉出来。\
**Kakania**: You need to release these desires. I'll guide your memory to find the deeply hidden thoughts. Trust me and tell me everything during the session.

**卡卡尼亚**：这可以一定程度上使压抑的欲望得到缓和，这样一来，您躯体上的昏厥与痉挛症状也能得到一些改善。\
**Kakania**: You'll suffer less from the repression, and your physical ailments, fainting and convulsions, will become less severe.

**卡卡尼亚**：忘记所有束缚，并信任我——这便是治疗的第一步。\
**Kakania**: Cast off your shackles and trust in me. This first step is crucial.

**卡卡尼亚**：我知道，家族内接连不断的悲剧让您深感痛苦。但请相信我，心理医生就是为了解决这些问题的。\
**Kakania**: I know tragedies in your family have affected you deeply. But I'm here to help you now.

**卡卡尼亚**：如果您对开口述说感到困难，可以看着这面镜子。\
**Kakania**: If you have trouble putting thoughts into words, use this mirror.

**卡卡尼亚**：它能映出您“内心的图景”。您可以把它当作一个心理手术用的“内视镜”。我使用了一点神秘术来便于自由联想……\
**Kakania**: It reflects your inner thoughts, like a mind's endoscope. I cast an arcane skill on it to help your thoughts surface.

**卡卡尼亚**：您只需要看一下它，然后告诉我眼前所见。\
**Kakania**: Look at it, and tell me what you see.

**伊索尔德**：……内心的图景……\
**Isolde**: My inner thoughts ...

**卡卡尼亚**：是的，我不会对您使用催眠，也不会转过头来，窥探您内心的隐秘。在这里会发生的仅仅是一场谈话。\
**Kakania**: Yes, I won't hypnotize you, nor will I turn around and peek at the mirror. What's in there belongs to only you, we're just going to talk.

**卡卡尼亚**：实际上，催眠正是我最厌恶的手段——它无助于您认清自己。\
**Kakania**: Hypnosis is a therapy I most detest. It doesn't help you understand and rediscover yourself.

**卡卡尼亚**：如果不是在理智完全清醒，双方完全同意的基础下，对话就没有任何意义。\
**Kakania**: And if the dialogue isn't based on the full awareness and consent of both parties, it's pointless.

**伊索尔德**：我明白，请放心，我会好好表现……\
**Isolde**: I see. I will do my best.

**卡卡尼亚**：哈哈，表现！您的担子太重啦，怎么能在需要敞开心扉的时刻还记着表演呢？这里又不是舞台……现在，您只需要瞧着镜子里，然后告诉我……\
**Kakania**: Do your best? Hah, relax, you're not on the job. Just turn around, look in the mirror, and tell me ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……您看到了什么？\
**Kakania**: What do you see?

**伊索尔德**：唔……\
**Isolde**: Uhm ...

**伊索尔德**：我看见……黄金一般的圆圈……\
**Isolde**: I see ... golden circles ...

**伊索尔德**：西奥菲尔站在书房，手激烈地在空中比划……\
**Isolde**: Theophil in his study, on his feet, his hand gesturing intensely in the air ...

**伊索尔德**：……啊，是的，我也在那儿。我在——\
**Isolde**: Ah, yes, I'm there too. I'm ...

**伊索尔德**：——？\
**Isolde**: ...?

她的声音变得古怪而尖锐。\
Her voice becomes strange and sharp.

**伊索尔德**：奇怪，这里为什么没有我呢？\
**Isolde**: Odd. Why am I not here?

**伊索尔德**：医生，您的镜子是坏了吗？它没有映出我自己来。这可不行，我答应了您，一定要好好表现……\
**Isolde**: Doctor, is your mirror not working? It's not showing my reflection. No, no, this isn't right, I promised to do my best ...

**伊索尔德**：我当时肯定在那里，我得清晰地想起来，才对得起您这场悉心设置的诊疗……\
**Isolde**: I was there, I must have been. I have to remember it. You prepared all of this for my sake, I mustn't disappoint you ...

**卡卡尼亚**：糟糕，她的强迫行为发作了——！\
**Kakania**: Oh no, she's stuck in her obsessive thoughts!

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德，请您先坐，听我说——\
**Kakania**: Isolde, please sit down and listen to my voice.

歌剧女演员罔顾医生的劝阻，只是用力地用手掰住镜子的边缘。\
The actress, ignoring her doctor's warnings, forcefully grips the edge of the mirror.

**伊索尔德**：——我在哪里？我又是谁？\
**Isolde**: Who am I? Where am I?

**伊索尔德**：您好，有人在那里吗？谁是我？我是谁？您好，您好？\
**Isolde**: Hello, is anybody there? Who is me? I am who? Greetings. Hello?

蜡烛熄灭了，房间里无端多了许多风声。\
The candles go out, and the room fills with an inexplicable breeze.

并无实体的“人”回应了她的问询，从虚空中应邀而来。\
An incorporeal voice responds to her inquiry, invited in from the void.

**卡卡尼亚**：游灵现象……上次在分离派之家……天啊，原来是这么回事。\
**Kakania**: The lost ghosts. The last time in the Secession Building ... Now I understand.

**卡卡尼亚**：得先帮伊索尔德解决她过度依赖神秘术的倾向……万幸，正因为没完成专业化教育，我什么都会一点。\
**Kakania**: I have to get her to stop relying so much on her arcane power. Luckily, not completing my education is why I know a little bit of everything.

医生冲到工坊里等身高的镜子旁边，逐个揭开上面罩着的灰布。\
The doctor rushes to the full-sized mirror in the workshop, removing the gray cloths one by one.

**伊索尔德**：唔……！医生，您在做什么？治疗中断了吗？\
**Isolde**: What are you doing, doctor? Is the session over?

**伊索尔德**：是因为我做错了什么吗？我做得不够好吗？\
**Isolde**: Was it because I did something wrong? Did I mess up?

**卡卡尼亚**：不，您很好，非常好！只是我要给这个地方来场突发的大扫除。\
**Kakania**: Nonsense, you were doing great! I just have to clean the room a bit.

更强烈的闪光充斥了诊所，驱散了那片潮湿而幽怨的黑暗。\
A more intense flash fills the clinic, dispelling the damp and resentful darkness.

**卡卡尼亚**：走吧，都走吧！幽灵无法在真实之镜里成像！\
**Kakania**: Shoo, go away! Mirrors are useless to ghosts!

**卡卡尼亚**：——别再缠着我的病人，你们该给自己也找个医生了！\
**Kakania**: Leave my patient alone, and never come back!

## 6TH-11 独幕剧 / One-Act Play

**卡卡尼亚**：……您现在好些了吗？还有东西缠着您，要同您说话吗？\
**Kakania**: Feeling better now? Is anything still haunting you, talking to you?

**卡卡尼亚**：现在您想起来自己是谁了吗，伊索尔德小姐？\
**Kakania**: Do you remember who you are, Isolde?

诊所重归寂静，卡卡尼亚握着伊索尔德的手，担忧地望着面前苍白的女演员。\
The clinic returns to silence as Kakania holds Isolde's hand, observing with concern the pale actress before her.

她望着前方的桌面镜，目光空洞地任由泪水从眼中滑落。\
She looks toward the tabletop mirror, allowing tears to fall from her hollow eyes.

**伊索尔德**：呀，是的，医生，现在我都看见了。\
**Isolde**: Oh, yes, doctor. I see it now.

**伊索尔德**：那场火——那场焚尽了一切的火！我怎么会忘记呢？\
**Isolde**: That fire, the fire that devoured everything! How could I ever forget?

**伊索尔德**：火焰吞噬着一切，西奥菲尔站在火中，尖叫着——他在点燃之前没有考虑任何事情！\
**Isolde**: The raging fire consumed everything, including Theophil. He was screaming—his mind was already gone before he ignited it all.

**伊索尔德**：他怎么可以就这样忘却一切呢——他凭什么能就这样忘却一切呢？\
**Isolde**: How could he ignore everything with such disregard? Who allowed him to forget with such disregard?

**伊索尔德**：而我都记得，都记得……我要是一名优雅的贵族，要是一名出色的神秘学家，要是一名优秀的歌剧演员，一名合格的迪塔斯多夫，一个好妹妹、好女儿……\
**Isolde**: While I remember, I remember it all. I'm from a noble family, I need to be a qualified Dittarsdorf, an outstanding arcanist, a first-rate opera singer, a good sister, and a good daughter ...

**伊索尔德**：绝不能僭越，绝不可出格，更罔论出丑！\
**Isolde**: Never forget my manners, never forget the family!

**伊索尔德**：而他，他却可以、可以！……西奥菲尔若是一个真正有勇气的人，他就应该去参军，或是痛痛快快地跟人决斗——这总要光荣些！\
**Isolde**: But he—he got away with it! If Theophil was truly a man of courage, he should've joined the army, or fought a duel with someone—that would've made his death more honorable!

**伊索尔德**：而他只是选择带着一身风流债，以这样的形式死去……\
**Isolde**: Yet, he chose to die this way, after a life of debauchery.

她剧烈呼吸着，苍白的脸上也终于有了血色。\
She breathes a heavy and bitter sigh, and finally, color returns to her face.

**伊索尔德**：呜，对不起，我不该说这些……\
**Isolde**: *sobs* I'm sorry ... I shouldn't have told you that.

**卡卡尼亚**：不，伊索尔德小姐，您这样是正确的——！这正是这次诊疗的目的。\
**Kakania**: It's okay, Isolde, you're doing it right. That's what therapy is for.

**卡卡尼亚**：这些正是我们需要知道的东西，那些被遏制、被刻意忽略的记忆……它将变为表象、变为语言来重新连结情感，再进一步，便可减轻躯体上体现的癔症症状！\
**Kakania**: These memories are exactly what we need. What's been deliberately repressed and ignored in the depths of your heart will manifest into words, and help you reconnect with your emotions. Soon your symptoms of hysteria will diminish!

**卡卡尼亚**：别担心，无论什么，您都可以向我倾诉——以家族与以希波克拉底的名义起誓！我绝不会将任何信息透露给第三个人。\
**Kakania**: Don't be afraid. You can talk to me about anything. In the name of my family and the Hippocratic Oath, I will keep things between you and me.

**卡卡尼亚**：……知道的人只会有你和我，它们将变成我们共同的秘密。\
**Kakania**: Everything will be a secret, our secret.

**伊索尔德**：共同的秘密……\
**Isolde**: Our secret ...

女人的面颊仍挂着泪珠，却又露出一个笑容，就像玫瑰花瓣上缀着露水。\
The woman's cheeks, still wet with tears, reveal a tragic smile, like dew on rose petals.

**伊索尔德**：这听起来真美好。\
**Isolde**: Sounds wonderful.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

她闭上了眼睛，似乎正极力拨开往事的迷雾。\
She closes her eyes, striving in that moment to open them without being free from the fog of the past.

**伊索尔德**：我还记得那间屋子……\
**Isolde**: I remember that room.

**伊索尔德**：那间屋子里亮得惊人。我总是没法习惯灯光……烛光总是要柔和些，那样小小的、惹人怜爱的一簇。从前，妈妈在睡前看望我时总是秉着一根白色的蜡烛。\
**Isolde**: The room was excessively bright. I never got used to light bulbs, preferring the softer light of candles. My mother always had a white candle burning when she saw me at bedtime.

**卡卡尼亚**：那根蜡烛后来去哪了？\
**Kakania**: What happened to that candle?

**伊索尔德**：它被人碰倒了。哈，呵！那个顽皮的男孩，我黑色头发的哥哥！\
**Isolde**: Someone knocked it over. Ha! That naughty brat, my dark-haired brother!

**伊索尔德**：他点燃了蜡烛！点燃了屋子！点燃了自己所有的画！\
**Isolde**: He lit the candle, set the room on fire, and burned all his paintings!

**伊索尔德**：他燃烧着朝我冲过来，手里拿着……！\
**Isolde**: He ran to me, his body burning! In his hand was ...

**伊索尔德**：一把枪。\
**Isolde**: A gun.

**伊索尔德**：我告诉过西奥菲尔，他并不是魏宁格那样的天才，饮弹自尽不会让他名声大噪的。人们只会记住首演，之后都是无趣的重复。\
**Isolde**: I once told Theophil, he's not a genius like Weininger. Biting the bullet won't make him famous. Only a debut leaves an impression, the shows that follow are boring repetitions.

**伊索尔德**：他大笑着说，如今在维也纳开枪自杀的人已经太多，要让世人都记住，还得再添上一把火才行。\
**Isolde**: He laughed. "Indeed. Too many have shot themselves for fame. Only through passionate fire would the world remember me."

**伊索尔德**：我告别他，去楼下与其他小姐交流。血液透过木地板，一滴、一滴地落入我的茶杯中。我走上楼，看见西奥菲尔躺在血泊里。\
**Isolde**: I bid him farewell, and went downstairs to talk to the ladies. Blood soaked the wooden floor and dripped into my cup. Plop, plop, plop. I went upstairs and found Theophil lying in a pool of blood.

**伊索尔德**：一支手枪躺在他的手上——漂亮的左轮，哈哈，在拨动时能发出悦耳的响声。\
**Isolde**: A revolver was in his hand. Ah, how its cylinder clicked like music.

**伊索尔德**：我提着裙子，好叫火从裙摆上流下去。我俯下身，在他左脑太阳穴的空洞上问：“西奥菲尔，您的火呢？”\
**Isolde**: I lifted my dress so the fire could roll down like water. I leaned over to the hole on his left temple and said, "Theophil, where is your fire?"

**伊索尔德**：西奥菲尔从地上坐了起来。他对我说：“伊索尔德，您的枪呢？”\
**Isolde**: Theophil sat up, and said, "Isolde, where's your gun?"

**卡卡尼亚**：……您的枪？\
**Kakania**: "Your gun?"

**伊索尔德**：……我的枪？\
**Isolde**: ... My gun?

她的嘴里突然发出“嗬、嗬”的声音。\
Her voice trailed out into a low sinister growl.

伊索尔德的双眸望向镜中的自己，她高高抬起手，像是演员在舞台上发表独白。\
Isolde swoons toward her reflection in the mirror, her hand raised high as if delivering a monologue on stage.

**伊索尔德**：啊，是我的枪！我想起来了，这支枪一直在我手上！！！\
**Isolde**: My gun! I remember now, I was holding the gun all along!

**伊索尔德**：西奥菲尔站在书房里，火光吞没了房梁，一切都在燃烧！他朝我冲过来，他朝我伸出手，要把我拉入火海之中——\
**Isolde**: Theophil stood in the study. The flames engulfed the beam, the ceiling, everything.

**卡卡尼亚**：什么？！\
**Kakania**: What?!

卡卡尼亚尽可能地放轻声音，不去惊扰女人的自白。\
Kakania speaks as softly as possible despite her shock, with the intent not to disturb the woman's soliloquy.

**伊索尔德**：他冲向我，哀嚎着，他很痛苦，又那么炙热，将我的眼球烤干——\
**Isolde**: He ran toward me, screaming, in pain. He was burning, the heat drying up my eyes ...

女人开始发抖。\
The woman begins to shake under the weight of revelation.

**伊索尔德**：他燃着火，他冲向我，医生，他冲向我！\
**Isolde**: He was on fire, and running towards me. Doctor, he ran at me!

她咬紧牙关，试图从那些白贝似的小骨头里挤出字眼来，挤出内脏来——要将自己像个精美木盒儿一般敞开，奉献给眼前的救世主。\
She clenches her teeth, trying to squeeze out words, gripping her chest as if to squeeze out her insides—to open herself like a finely crafted wooden box, offering herself to her rescuer.

**卡卡尼亚**：深呼吸，伊索尔德，深呼吸……没事的，没事的。我在这里，我还在你身边，你很安全。\
**Kakania**: Breathe in, breathe out ... It's okay, Isolde. I'm here by your side. You're safe.

卡卡尼亚伸出双臂，轻轻环住身边的女人。\
Kakania extends her arms, gently encircling the woman into her embrace.

她大口呼吸着，在绿色的怀抱中逐渐平静下来。\
She breathes deeply, calming down inside the green warmth.

**伊索尔德**：……然后，我听见一声枪响。\
**Isolde**: And then, I heard a shot.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

怀抱微微收紧了些。\
Their embrace tightens slightly.

**伊索尔德**：我记不清了，扳机很硬，枪响之后，它就从我的虎口滑了出去……\
**Isolde**: I-I can't remember ... The trigger was hard to pull. After the shot, it slipped out of my hand ...

她从怀抱中抬起头来，泪水涟涟。\
She lifts her head up towards the good doctor, tears flowing from her eyes.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

**伊索尔德**：是我杀了西奥菲尔！是我……！\
**Isolde**: I killed Theophil! It was me!

**伊索尔德**：我没有资格参加他的葬礼，没有资格举办他的纪念画展，没有资格承受这些同情和善意……\
**Isolde**: I don't deserve the right to attend his funeral, or to hold his memorial art exhibit. I don't deserve any of the sympathy and kindness ...

**伊索尔德**：我也应该走进那场火里，我也应该痛痛快快地去死，我……！呜呜呜呜………………\
**Isolde**: I should have burned in that fire, I should have died! *sobbing*

**卡卡尼亚**：没关系的。\
**Kakania**: It's fine.

**伊索尔德**：……？\
**Isolde**: ...?

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德小姐，我不是法官，不是警察，只是您的医生——无论您自认是一个怎样的人，我只对您负责。\
**Kakania**: I'm neither judge nor police, Isolde. I'm just your doctor. I'll remain faithful to you, no matter what you think you are.

**卡卡尼亚**：您的生命在当时受到了严重的威胁。换作他人，情急之下也很可能会做出同样的抉择。\
**Kakania**: Your life was in danger. Anyone would've done the same.

**卡卡尼亚**：这不是您的错，伊索尔德小姐，您只是……被吓坏了。\
**Kakania**: It was not your fault, Isolde. You were just ... terrified.

**卡卡尼亚**：您完全无需为本能感到羞耻。请您放心，我会为您保守这个秘密。\
**Kakania**: Don't be ashamed of your instinctive behavior. Rest assured, your secret is safe with me.

**卡卡尼亚**：按照弗洛伊德医生的说法，接受阴暗是解除压抑的第一步。\
**Kakania**: According to Dr. Freud, embracing your darkness is the first step to liberation.

**卡卡尼亚**：您已经迈出了这一步，这是非常有勇气、非常困难的一步。绝大多数的人都无法做到，可您做得很好。\
**Kakania**: It takes courage, and is not easy to do. Most people can't do it, but you've done a very good job.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**伊索尔德**：我，做得好吗？\
**Isolde**: I did a good job?

**卡卡尼亚**：是的，您做得非常棒。\
**Kakania**: Yes. An excellent job.

**伊索尔德**：医生……\
**Isolde**: Doctor ...

她终于如释负重地失声痛哭。\
Her tears now are like a broken dam, relieved of the burden that it had too long held.

卡卡尼亚轻轻抱着她，静待这场久违的释放结束。\
Kakania holds her gently, waiting for her long-overdue catharsis to come to an end.

**卡卡尼亚**：好了，我就送您到这儿——明天您要主持开展仪式，下周还有《托斯卡》的演出。如果我夺走您宝贵的排练时间，整个维也纳都会恨我的。\
**Kakania**: Alright, this is as far as I can walk you. You have to host a ceremony tomorrow, and Tosca's next week. Vienna won't forgive me if I take up too much of your time.

**伊索尔德**：没关系，如您所说，吹吹夜风更有助于我的健康。\
**Isolde**: Don't worry about it. Like you said, the night breeze will do me some good.

她挽着卡卡尼亚的胳膊，几不可微地摇了摇头。\
She still cleaves hard to Kakania's arm, imperceptibly shaking her head.

天光已暗，没有多少散步的行人注意到这位杰出的歌剧女演员就在自己身边。\
As twilight falls, few passersby notice the distinguished opera singer among them.

**卡卡尼亚**：我听海因里希说，你们要做一些新的尝试？\
**Kakania**: I heard from Heinrich that you're trying new things?

**卡卡尼亚**：我看了他的舞台设计稿，他吸收了柏林那边的表现主义风格，真是叫人耳目一新……\
**Kakania**: I read his stage design. The style of Berlin expressionism he adopted is quite refreshing.

**卡卡尼亚**：我承认，他从柏林回来之后就变得有些古怪。但他还是一样对艺术如此热忱，对同胞也爱得真心实意。\
**Kakania**: I have to admit, he became a little strange after his trip to Berlin. But his passion for art didn't change, nor did his love for his fellow Viennese.

**伊索尔德**：是的，我也非常感激他。只可惜，皇家宫廷剧院没有通过申请，我们最终还是在维也纳人民歌剧院上演。\
**Isolde**: I appreciate his hard work as well. But sadly, the Vienna Court Opera didn't approve our performance application, so we turned to the Vienna People's Opera.

**卡卡尼亚**：嚯，我一点也不意外。当初马勒先生努力了那么久，也无法拿到《莎乐美》的演出许可，要知道他自己就是皇家宫廷剧院的艺术总监……\
**Kakania**: Well, I'm not surprised. Understand that Mr. Mahler is the artistic director of the Vienna Court Opera, and even he could not bring Salome to the stage.

**卡卡尼亚**：这些老古板是不会让新的艺术形式通过的，他们只是希望陈旧的曲调和布景像天国一样永恒。\
**Kakania**: Those boring, stale old-timers will never approve of new forms of art. They always expect something predictable and unvarying, the same old pieces and settings.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

她的脸色突然黯淡下去。\
Her complexion darkens again as she turns her head.

**伊索尔德**：《托斯卡》无法通过皇家宫廷剧院的申请，是因为我。\
**Isolde**: I'm the reason Tosca can't get the permission.

**伊索尔德**：因为他们请了一个灵媒，一个疯疯癫癫的“神秘学家”来做主演。\
**Isolde**: Because I, the star, am a medium, a maniacal "arcanist."

**卡卡尼亚**：哦不，这绝对与此无关。维也纳优秀的作曲家、演奏家、指挥家，几乎全都是神秘学家。\
**Kakania**: Oh, no, that's not it. In Vienna, the great composers, conductors, and performers ... almost all of them have been arcanists.

**卡卡尼亚**：在维也纳，谁要抹除神秘学家独一无二的天赋感知和艺术贡献，谁就把整个维也纳的文化生活都一把火烧光吧！\
**Kakania**: Wiping out the unique talents of arcanists and their artistic contributions would be like setting fire to the cultural tapestry of Viennese society!

**卡卡尼亚**：噢，真对不起……一场洪水！洪水要更好……\
**Kakania**: Oh, sorry. A flood! A flood is better ...

女演员没注意到这个小小的口误。\
The actress is, or at least acts, oblivious to this minor slip.

**伊索尔德**：可许多人并不承认“灵媒表演”。他们认为这是对舞台的玷污……演唱者在舞台上使用降灵术，请灵附身于自己，让自己“成为”歌剧里的角色。\
**Isolde**: They consider it a desecration of the stage. When a singer is channeling, she's essentially asking a spirit to possess her and speak directly through her, thus she "becomes" the character in the opera ...

**伊索尔德**：人们会质疑，那还是“演唱者”自己的歌喉吗？这不是一种欺诈吗？\
**Isolde**: People will question the authenticity of the voice—is this still the singer's own voice? Or is it fraud?

**卡卡尼亚**：不，伊索尔德，他们这样说，是因为他们完全不懂戏剧，一丁点也不懂……\
**Kakania**: No, Isolde. They think that, because they know nothing about performance, not even the slightest thing.

**卡卡尼亚**：戏剧的本质就是欺诈。我们走进剧院，不是为了直面自己，是为了成为他人！你想，他们如果这么追求实际的话，干嘛不上我的诊所来照照镜子呢？\
