**Kakania**: The nature of the stage is to be someone else. If they're so intent on the presentation of the true self, the mirrors in my clinic would like a word with them.

**卡卡尼亚**：演员的职责，正是在舞台那个虚幻的空间里，在那短暂的时间中，全然地成为他人，并把这种幻觉尽可能逼真地带到我们眼前。\
**Kakania**: It is an actor's job to become another person. On stage, in a fictional world, they briefly trick our eyes into thinking it's real.

**卡卡尼亚**：为此，我们艰苦卓绝地排练，精心设计曲目、服装、布景、光照……\
**Kakania**: And to achieve that, we rehearse rigorously, through sweat and pain. We take care of the music, the costumes, the settings, the lights ...

**卡卡尼亚**：而您的天赋能帮助您更好地达成这一点，仅此而已。\
**Kakania**: Your gift helps you do this better than others. That's all.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**伊索尔德**：可是，我的确是运用了迪塔斯多夫家族的神秘术。没有它，我无法取得这样的成就。\
**Isolde**: But I used the arcane skills of the Dittarsdorf family. I couldn't have done these things without them.

**伊索尔德**：神秘学家卓越的艺术天赋，也是一种疯癫的诅咒。\
**Isolde**: What if an arcanist's talent for art is also a curse?

**伊索尔德**：医生，或许我只是一个借助疾病的冒充者。一旦病症好转，艺术天赋便荡然无存……\
**Isolde**: Maybe I'm just a fraud, doctor. I'm propped up by my illness, and once it's cured, my talent will be gone with it ...

卡卡尼亚突然顿住了。\
Kakania pauses abruptly.

她回过头来，望向这位为自己的天赋而饱受困扰的歌剧天才。\
She turns back, looking at an operatic genius tormented by her own talents.

**卡卡尼亚**：不是这样的，伊索尔德小姐。\
**Kakania**: It's not like that, Isolde.

**卡卡尼亚**：我从没听说过，任何人运用自己的天赋，会被称为舞弊。\
**Kakania**: Using your talents is not cheating.

**卡卡尼亚**：我们是神秘学家。可在我们被这个模糊不清的词语定性前，我们是谁？\
**Kakania**: We're "arcanists." But before we allow ourselves to be defined by that word, who are we really?

**卡卡尼亚**：如果一个“神秘学家”从小就在孤岛上生活……她绝不会称自己为“神秘学家”，只会觉得自己是一个“人”——一个和我们，和所有人都没有区别的人。\
**Kakania**: If an "arcanist" grew up on a lonely island, she wouldn't see herself as an "arcanist," but as a "person" like you, like me, like everyone.

**伊索尔德**：医生……\
**Isolde**: Doctor ...

伊索尔德抬起头，看着卡卡尼亚眼底的闪烁的星点。\
Isolde meets her gaze as the stars twinkle back in Kakania's eyes.

**卡卡尼亚**：可是伊索尔德，你知道吗？当我向人群中望去，我从未见过任何一个“神秘学家”！\
**Kakania**: But you know, the truth is, when I look at a crowd, I don't see any "arcanists"!

**卡卡尼亚**：我只是看到一个一个有天赋的同胞，受限于世俗的困顿之中，磨平自己的棱角，变得面目朦胧、模糊不清。\
**Kakania**: All I see is our people, with different talents, trapped in life, their selfhoods ground smooth until they're indistinguishable from the crowd.

**卡卡尼亚**：人类因他们的缺陷而纯粹，我们却因为非凡而受阻。\
**Kakania**: Humans celebrate their flaws, yet they persecute our gifts.

**卡卡尼亚**：在那个评价体系里，我们的天赋仅仅是一种病症，才华仅仅是一种缺损，血脉则是一种可怖的诅咒。\
**Kakania**: They control the narrative. They define our gifts as diseases, our talents as weaknesses, and our bloodlines as curses.

**卡卡尼亚**：治好了病症，我们便泯然众人。要靠病症生存，我们便反复刨开自己的创口。\
**Kakania**: If we're cured, we're just another face in the crowd. But if we live on with our "diseases," we're forever ill, forever afflicted.

**卡卡尼亚**：神秘学家就像这样贩卖自己呕出的血肉生存。\
**Kakania**: We arcanists have to live in such a world, where we survive through suffering.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：您看看这个地方，我们最开明、最包容的城市。在萨赫蛋糕的甜美巧克力外衣下，埋藏的却是火药和毒酒。\
**Kakania**: Look at this city, this most enlightened, tolerant city. Under the sweet surface of the Sachertorte lies powder and poisonous wine.

**卡卡尼亚**：神秘学家被承认拥有艺术才华，却也仅仅如此，我们没有任何议会席位，难以评上任何职称，也难以获得任何专业证明。\
**Kakania**: Arcanists are recognized for their artistic abilities, nothing more. We hold no parliamentary seats, no professional titles, and no professional credentials.

**卡卡尼亚**：我们被流放到文化的角落，流放到装饰画和花瓶的位置，因为那是唯一一个掀不起波澜的地方。\
**Kakania**: We are exiled and marginalized. Our only voice in the culture is to be decoration, because decoration impacts nothing.

**卡卡尼亚**：而针对神秘学家的管束和歧视每天都在增加，先是登记，然后是居留证明，现在是神秘术许可证……\
**Kakania**: The restrictions and discrimination against arcanists are worsening by day. First we had to register with the government, then we needed residence permits, and now, permission to cast arcane skills.

**卡卡尼亚**：我们必须忍气吞声，必须合乎体面，必须做一个“好”神秘学家，不能出现任何“不稳定”，因为我们应是理性的动物，否则我们就是动物。\
**Kakania**: And we can do nothing but tolerate, stay polite and dignified. Be a "good" arcanist, show no signs of "instability," because we're supposed to stay rational, otherwise, we're animals.

**卡卡尼亚**：可人并不是只有理性的一面——正如弗洛伊德医生揭示的那样，它只是冰山一角。\
**Kakania**: But people are complicated, they can't stay rational forever—as Dr. Freud said, we're just seeing the tip of the iceberg.

街边的路灯亮起了，卡卡尼亚抬起头来，现在她也像一个独幕剧演员了。\
As the streetlights come on, Kakania looks up, now resembling an actress mid-monologue beneath the stark light.

**卡卡尼亚**：……您也许病了，也许我们都病了。但根源是社会病了，仅仅诊断个人是不够的。\
**Kakania**: You might be sick, I might be too. But the truth is, this whole society is sick! You can't just treat the individual and ignore the bigger picture.

**卡卡尼亚**：正是对非理性冲动的压抑，导致了我们时代普遍的疾病。\
**Kakania**: It was the repression of irrational desires that allowed the diseases to spread in our time.

**卡卡尼亚**：在这层意义上，那座岛上的人们倒是比我们要自由得多！\
**Kakania**: In this case, the people on that island are much freer than we are!

**伊索尔德**：您是在说……传言里那座埋着黄金的神秘小岛吗？\
**Isolde**: You mean that mysterious island? I hear gold is in the ground there.

卡卡尼亚用力点了点头。\
Kakania nods with vigor.

**卡卡尼亚**：您还记得刚刚基金会的那位小姐吗？\
**Kakania**: Remember the lady from the Foundation?

**伊索尔德**：……嗯，您为何又突然提起她？\
**Isolde**: Yes. Why?

**卡卡尼亚**：那位刚结识不久的新朋友告诉我，那座岛上的神秘学家不是疯子……他们自由地生存在那里。\
**Kakania**: She said the arcanists on that island are not lunatics, and they're living a life free of restrictions.

**卡卡尼亚**：多么理想啊，如果我们也能建立一个属于自己的团体，就像艺术家结社那样，我们自己种植、生产、劳作、分工。\
**Kakania**: Doesn't that sound great? If we could form our own society, like those artistic associations, and have control over our own production and labor.

**卡卡尼亚**：我想这就是那座小岛对人们的启示……尽管我还未见到，但可以预见的，他们展示了另一种生活，一个没有压抑的自由王国。\
**Kakania**: This must've been some kind of enlightenment. I can almost see it, they'll show us another way of life, a kingdom free of repression.

**卡卡尼亚**：因此帮助他们，就像帮助我们自己。这也是您举办那场画展的意义。\
**Kakania**: To help them is to help ourselves. And that's also what your exhibit is about.

**伊索尔德**：我……？不，我并不是那么伟大的人。\
**Isolde**: Me? No, I'm not as great a person as you.

**卡卡尼亚**：可您也做着伟大的事业。\
**Kakania**: But you are working for a great cause.

那眼底的星点漾开了。卡卡尼亚露出了一个笑容。\
The stars in her eyes begin to spread out. Kakania reveals a deep and tender smile.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德，我的朋友。我对您说我的梦想，我希望它有一天也是您的梦想，所有人的梦想。\
**Kakania**: Isolde, my friend. I've shared my dream with you, and I hope one day it'll become your own, until the day when everyone shares the same dream.

**卡卡尼亚**：我们的社会需要一场彻底的变革，一场大手术。\
**Kakania**: Our society needs a revolution, a radical surgery.

**卡卡尼亚**：在这个属于进步的世纪之初，我们迫切需要一种新的思想，好将我们重新整合起来。\
**Kakania**: We urgently need a new vision to reunite us at the dawn of the new century.

**卡卡尼亚**：就像艺术有它们的分离派，我们也需要有神秘学的分离派。从“歇斯底里的精神病人”、“贩卖小商品的小贩”、“装神弄鬼的街头骗子”中分离出去……\
**Kakania**: Like the secession in art history, we need a secession of arcanum to distinguish us from "hysterical lunatics," "street peddlers," and "con artists."

**卡卡尼亚**：——我们需要有新的梦想，新的神话。我们需重新将自己在世界上发明出来，成为新的人。\
**Kakania**: We need a new dream, a new saga. We need to reinvent ourselves and become a new people.

**卡卡尼亚**：再无压抑，只是拥抱原初的激情。\
**Kakania**: No more repression, only the full embrace of our primal desires.

卡卡尼亚结束了独白，她摘下自己的帽子，理了理上面的羽毛。\
Kakania concludes her monologue, removing her hat to fastidiously straighten the feathers on top.

**卡卡尼亚**：因此，您的工作绝不是徒劳的。无论是承办西奥菲尔的画展，还是推进新的歌剧艺术……\
**Kakania**: That's why your work has not been in vain! From Theophil's art exhibition to the promotion of new art ...

**卡卡尼亚**：不要质疑自己，您所做的事是伟大的。\
**Kakania**: Do not doubt yourself. You're helping a great cause.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**伊索尔德**：谢谢您，医生。这是第一次……有人对我说这些话。\
**Isolde**: Thank you, doctor. This is the first time anyone's said that to me.

**伊索尔德**：我会将它们谨记在心。\
**Isolde**: I will bear that in mind.

**伊索尔德**：……这些夜风和您的话语都让我非常振奋，我感觉呼吸畅快多了。您可以再陪我散一会步吗？\
**Isolde**: ... Your words in the breeze of night have been stirring. Can you walk with me a little longer?

**伊索尔德**：我想再听您谈谈刚刚提到的分离派观念，也好为明天的开展仪式准备讲稿……\
**Isolde**: I'd like to hear more things about the secession you mentioned, so that I can prepare my speech for tomorrow's ceremony ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……当然，这是我的荣幸！\
**Kakania**: Yes. It is my pleasure.

**卡卡尼亚**：您想去人民歌剧院的附近看看吗？他们一定张贴了新的宣传海报……\
**Kakania**: Would you like a walk to the Vienna People's Opera? I think they put up new posters.

## 6TH-12 艺术沙龙 / Art Exhibit

高一点的地方，视野比上次好了许多。\
From a higher vantage, the view is much improved.

**马库斯**：《新自由报》的记者……《潘神》的主编……《火炬》的创刊人……\
**Marcus**: Reporter of New Free Press, editor-in-chief of the Pan ... The founder of The Torch ...

**马库斯**：噢，那是埃贡·埃尔温·基希！报道雷德尔上校事件的《波西米亚报》记者，我做了功课……\
**Marcus**: Oh, that's Egon Erwin Kisch! The reporter who uncovered the scandal surrounding Colonel Alfred Redl ... I had investigated this before ...

**马库斯**：建筑师阿道夫·路斯，啊！我记得斯坦纳住宅【Steiner House】是他的杰作……马克西米利安·荣格少校和他的夫人……没想到这些大人物也会来参观画展。\
**Marcus**: Adolf Loos, the architect! He designed the Steiner House, as I recall. That's Major Maximilian Ronge and his wife ... who knew that celebrities like them would visit this exhibition.

**马库斯**：和我以前在岛上看到的报纸有些差别……之前好像没有那么浑圆和老态，哦。难道是我记错了？摄影也算是一个美化人的艺术啊。\
**Marcus**: But they look different from the pictures in the papers ... They were younger, and less chubby. Has my memory failed me? Or is it because photography is also an art of beautification?

**马库斯**：卡尔先生说得没错，人们没完没了地参观分离派之家，只为一睹新艺术的风采……\
**Marcus**: Mr. Karl was right. People are flocking to the Secession Building to get a glimpse of the new art.

**霍夫曼**：……我一点也看不懂这些艺术品。\
**Hofmann**: … I can't appreciate these things at all.

霍夫曼女士客观地评价道。\
Hofmann comments from her typical cold objectivity.

**霍夫曼**：我已经和委外合约小队的成员布置好了行动安排。海因里希一旦出现，就对他进行控制。\
**Hofmann**: I've informed the Field Agent Squad, as soon as Heinrich shows up, we'll get him under control.

**霍夫曼**：理想是以“非法使用神秘术”的名由把他带离——符合这个时代的法律，风险也最低。但如果他背后的确是重塑之手，可能会出现正面冲突。\
**Hofmann**: Ideally, we will take him away for "illegal use of arcane skills." It is the best reason and the least risk. It also complies with the laws of this time. If Manus Vindictae is behind all this, they'll show themselves for sure.

**霍夫曼**：届时，委外合约小队的成员会在外围给予我们支持。\
**Hofmann**: The squad will assist us from the perimeter by then.

**霍夫曼**：马库斯，你的任务是留心观察，不排除海因里希会伪装在人群中。另外，也要留心重塑之手相关的术式痕迹，这才是我们本来的目的。\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, your mission is to watch everything closely. Heinrich could be disguised and hiding in the crowd. Also keep an eye on the Manus and their rituals—that's what we were originally here for.

**马库斯**：嗯！我一定不会漏看的。\
**Marcus**: Leave it to me! I won't miss a thing.

马库斯深呼吸一口气。\
Marcus takes a deep breath, seeking a clear moment before diving.

场景加载-阅读状态。理想是有一个翻页的特效，然后场景变为线稿。（用PS处理一下？）

无数的信息涌入马库斯的眼中。\
A starburst of information floods into Marcus's eyes, reeling across her mind with a thousand pages at once.

世界对她是一本书，历来如此。\
The world has always been a book to her.

**马库斯**：托马斯议员正在和几位女士谈论表现主义……他的父辈当年在印象派的事上吃尽大亏，谁都没想到这些没人看懂的画以后会价值连城。\
**Marcus**: Mr. Thomas, the representative, is talking to the ladies about expressionism. His parents did not foresee the success of Impressionism—the works that made no sense but became priceless on the market.

**马库斯**：这导致他这一代人在艺术审美上矫枉过正，任何看不懂的艺术都是好艺术……\
**Marcus**: That's why his generation over-corrects their aesthetic standards and pays compliments to any art they don't understand.

**马库斯**：《新自由报》的记者正在和少校讨论近期维也纳接连不断的自杀案……\
**Marcus**: The reporter for the New Free Press and that major are discussing the frequent suicides in Vienna ...

**马库斯**：他们为此写了不少专题报道，不少人将之归因为《少年维特之烦恼》的流行造成的影响……真的吗？\
**Marcus**: They've written articles about it, and many of them attribute it to the publication of The Sorrows of Young Werther.

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚在和《火炬》的编辑高谈“魔圈”创始理念。“这是原始人在自然里画下的第一个魔力圈！”唔，她的字还真是大……\
**Marcus**: Kakania is describing the founding idea of "The Circle." "This is the first magic circle drawn by the primitive man!" Hmm, quite the strong woman ...

**马库斯**：今年春天在波斯尼亚和黑塞哥维那的军事演习……康拉德将军或将失宠……大西洋上空的低压槽……象牙白色的部级用纸……\
**Marcus**: The military exercise in Bosnia and Herzegovina this spring ... General Conrad to lose power ... A low pressure trough on the Atlantic Ocean ... Ivory-colored paper for official use only ...

**马库斯**：将军……内阁议员的夫人……石英砂颜料……神秘学是否是一种病菌感染……精神分析是否是一种全新的心理疾病……\
**Marcus**: The general ... Wife of a cabinet member ... Quartz sand ... Is arcanum a bacterial infection ... Is psychoanalysis a new type of mental illness ...

**马库斯**：海因里希先生不在这里。\
**Marcus**: Mr. Heinrich is not here.

**马库斯**：这一页没有什么实用的信息。\
**Marcus**: Nothing useful on this page.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**马库斯**：……啊，又见到伊索尔德小姐了，她是这次沙龙的主办方。\
**Marcus**: Ah, Ms. Isolde again. She's the host of the exhibition.

**马库斯**：她的状态……看上去竟然比上次见面还要好了许多。\
**Marcus**: She seems ... healthier than the last time we met.

**马库斯**：虽然不清楚原因为何，但真为她感到高兴。\
**Marcus**: I don't know why, but I'm happy for her.

**马库斯**：她要登台致辞了。\
**Marcus**: She's about to make a speech.

特效-翻页

**伊索尔德**：很荣幸能主办这次纪念画展。\
**Isolde**: It is my honor to host this exhibition.

**伊索尔德**：在正式开展之前，我想感谢西奥菲尔的朋友——海因里希先生，他是这次画展的策展人。\
**Isolde**: Before we begin, I'd like to express my gratitude for Mr. Heinrich, who is Theophil's friend and the curator of this exhibition.

**马库斯**：海因里希依然没有出现，难道他提前发现了什么……？\
**Marcus**: Heinrich still hasn't shown up. Did he notice something?

**伊索尔德**：以及我的朋友，同时也是“魔圈”的创始人——克拉拉小姐！\
**Isolde**: And also a friend of mine, the founder of "The Circle"—Ms. Klara!

**伊索尔德**：她在暗处积极地联络，为我们争取了办展的场地。她来自一个新兴的神秘学家中产家庭，是一位尽职的医生，也是一位品位卓越的艺术鉴赏家。\
**Isolde**: Without her tireless work behind the scenes, we wouldn't be here today. Born into a rising arcane family of the middle class, Ms. Klara is a devoted doctor and an art connoisseur with impeccable taste.

伊索尔德盛情介绍着，将手伸向台下。\
Isolde makes for a dramatic introduction, reaching out towards the audience below.

**卡卡尼亚**：呃……！\
**Kakania**: Ugh!

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚医生站了起来，和宾客们打招呼。她笑得十分僵硬，似乎没有想到自己会被提名。\
**Marcus**: Dr. Kakania is standing up, greeting the guests. That's an awkward smile. Looks like she didn't see this coming.

**马库斯**：唔，伊索尔德小姐用鼓励的眼神看着她。——她是想在名流前提携自己的朋友吗？\
**Marcus**: Hmm, Ms. Isolde is giving her an encouraging look. She wants to introduce her friend to the celebrities?

**马库斯**：看来她们的私下关系非常好……\
**Marcus**: So they're actually very close ...

**卡卡尼亚**：唉，我明明告诉她不用提我的名字……\
**Kakania**: *sigh* I told her not to mention my name ...

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚压下帽子，她不习惯出风头吗？……不，她不是这种性格。她在为伊索尔德的目光难为情吗？\
**Marcus**: Ms. Kakania is lowering her hat. Does she not like the spotlight? No, that's not it. Is it because of Ms. Dittarsdorf's gaze?

马库斯全神贯注地观察。\
Marcus observes the woman in green intently.

伊索尔德掀开了纱帘。\
Isolde lifts the curtain.

**伊索尔德**：我们将在此首次展出《拯救》——西奥菲尔生前留下的唯一完整的画。\
**Isolde**: This is the debut of The Salvation—the only painting Theophil left behind.

**马库斯**：……！是它……\
**Marcus**: This is it!

**伊索尔德**：在生前的最后时光，西奥菲尔曾醉心于黄金岛的传言，他畅想那里是一个艺术与人文的美好国度，一个属于神秘学家的乌托邦。\
**Isolde**: In his last moments, Theophil became obsessed with the Golden Isle. He envisioned it as a realm of art and culture, a utopia for arcanists.

**伊索尔德**：他们从未受过世俗沾染，保持着原始的生命力与激情。\
**Isolde**: There, the primal vitality and passion of arcanists would be preserved and never tainted by the outside world.

**伊索尔德**：他曾写下过这样的句子：“那座岛上有着拯救的希望……”\
**Isolde**: He wrote, "That island holds the hope of salvation."

**马库斯**：唔，是这样吗？我的知情权限不够……\
**Marcus**: Hmm, is this so? This is above my clearance ...

**马库斯**：看起来，维也纳的每个人都对那座岛做了自己希望的解读……\
**Marcus**: Sounds like everyone in Vienna has their own interpretation of the island.

**伊索尔德**：……先生们，女士们，我呼吁各位对此事予以关注。我们会成立一个促进委员会，向帝国国会请愿，停止对它的火力打击！\
**Isolde**: Ladies and gentlemen, your attention please! We are forming a committee to petition the Empire to cease its attacks on the island!

**伊索尔德**：那座岛上的神秘学家不是疯子！他们只是自由地生存在那里。\
**Isolde**: The arcanists there are not lunatics, they're simply living free!

**马库斯**：唔……？！\
**Marcus**: Erm?!

熟悉的话语中断了马库斯的思绪，她茫然地瞪大眼睛。\
Familiar words interrupt Marcus's thoughts, her eyes widening in bewilderment.

但在聚光灯下，致辞还在继续。\
But beneath the spotlight, the speech continues.

**伊索尔德**：它的存在对于我们也有巨大的启示。帮助他们，就像是帮助我们自己。\
**Isolde**: Their existence is a revelation to us. To help them is to help ourselves.

**伊索尔德**：……我们的社会生病了，仅仅医治个人是不够的。它需要一场彻底的大手术，一场找回我们饱受压抑的天性，将自己重新在世界上发明出来的大变革……\
**Isolde**: Our society is sick. Treating the individual is only treating a symptom. It needs a radical surgery, a revolution that will let us rediscover our repressed nature, and reinvent ourselves in this world ...

**马库斯**：不好，这些发言，它们……\
**Marcus**: Something's wrong. Her speech is ...

马库斯的直觉在强烈敲着警钟。\
Marcus's intuition hammers out a warning. A loud clear klaxon in her mind.

在她有所动作之前，伊索尔德抬起了手，说出了致辞的高潮。\
Before she can act, Isolde raises her hand as if holding out some drawn sword, reaching the climax of her speech.

**伊索尔德**：我希望，我们神秘学家能够联合起来……\
**Isolde**: I wish for the arcanists to unite ...

**伊索尔德**：——建立一个不再有压抑的，自由的，属于我们自己的独立王国！\
**Isolde**: And establish an independent kingdom of freedom, free from repression and oppression!

**马库斯**：——！\
**Marcus**: —!

**霍夫曼**：……突发事故，封锁出口。增加抓捕目标伊索尔德。\
**Hofmann**: It's an emergency. Seal the exits. Add Isolde to our targets.

霍夫曼没有犹豫，立刻进行了决断。\
Hofmann delivers her orders coldly and without a moment of hesitation.

**霍夫曼**：马库斯，动手。\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, now.

音效-轻轻骚动

**沙龙宾客Ⅰ**：什么……？\
**Guest I**: What?

**沙龙宾客Ⅰ**：是我听错了，还是伊索尔德小姐真的说了……\
**Guest I**: Am I hearing things, or did Ms. Dittarsdorf really say that?

一开始，人群还是小范围地骚动着。\
At first, the crowd stirs like a ripple over a deep and swift current.

**沙龙宾客Ⅰ**：原谅她吧，我想只是迪塔斯多夫小姐她的精神疾病仍未痊愈……\
**Guest I**: Forgive her! Perhaps Ms. Dittarsdorf hasn't fully recovered from her illness ...

**沙龙宾客Ⅲ**：我看也是！\
**Guest III**: I think so too!

卡卡尼亚愕然地从座位上站起来，罔顾自己的帽子从膝盖上滑落。\
Kakania rises up from her seat, her hat sliding off her knee, stunned hands failing to catch it.

**卡卡尼亚**：不，怎么会这样……我，我没有和她说过要这么做——\
**Kakania**: What, how? I did not tell her to ...

**海因里希**：朋友们！观众们！幸存者们！请冷静！\
**Heinrich**: Ladies and gentlemen! Dear friends! Calm down!

男人的声音从展厅之家的另一头响起。\
A man's voice booms from the other end of the exhibition hall.

**海因里希**：不用慌张，因为我已为诸位找到了拯救之道！\
**Heinrich**: Do not panic, for I have found salvation for you!

**卡卡尼亚**：……海因里希？！你身后的是——\
**Kakania**: Heinrich? What is that behind you ...

**通讯器**：——霍夫曼调查员，目标出现了！但是，我们遭遇了戈连群！\
**Communicator**: Hofmann, the targets showed up! But golems are attacking us!

**霍夫曼**：……我也看见了。\
**Hofmann**: I see it too.

**霍夫曼**：物品附魔的神秘术吗？马库斯，阅读一下原理。\
**Hofmann**: The arcane skill of object enchantment? Marcus, give it a read.

盔甲石像簇拥着海因里希，像是舞台上的布景道具。\
Armored statues surround Heinrich, reaching a motionless still that creates an odd, if dramatic, tableau.

**海因里希**：请不要忽略伊索尔德小姐的话语——我们正处于世界毁灭的试验场上！\
**Heinrich**: Please do not ignore what Ms. Dattersdorf is saying! This is a proving ground of a world-ending experiment!

**海因里希**：巨大的浩劫正在向我们逼近，战栗的乌云已经在天空中聚集。\
**Heinrich**: A catastrophe is coming. The clouds of war are filling up the sky.

**海因里希**：睁开眼睛看看我们目前所有的一切吧。一切动听的音乐，美好的艺术，进步的理想——\
**Heinrich**: Open your eyes and look at all we have now. The music, the art, the ambitions of progress ...

**海因里希**：都将在人类创造的炮火中毁灭！\
**Heinrich**: Man's gunfire will destroy them all!

**卡卡尼亚**：……什么？\
**Kakania**: ... What?

**卡卡尼亚**：你们……都在说什么？\
**Kakania**: What ... are you all talking about?

**伊索尔德**：医生，别担心，您只是现在还不知道。\
**Isolde**: Not to worry, doctor. You simply don't know yet.

女人伸出手来。\
The woman, now so strange in the doctor's eyes, reaches out her hand.

**伊索尔德**：请跟我走，我会告诉您一切——您的梦想，有属于它的归处。\
**Isolde**: Follow me, and I'll show you everything, where your dream has taken root.

戈连的出现刺激了人群，宾客们开始骚动。\
The appearance of the golems agitates the crowd, and the ripple becomes a chaotic crash of waves.

**沙龙宾客Ⅲ**：太荒谬了！建立一个独立的王国？这是公然叛国！\
**Guest III**: This is ridiculous! An independent kingdom? It is treason!

**沙龙宾客Ⅲ**：我们是维也纳人，为什么要离开自己的国家？\
**Guest III**: We are Viennese! Why would we want to leave our own country?

**沙龙宾客Ⅳ**：这些戈连也是艺术品吗？噢，它们看起来很有份量，我也想收藏一个……\
**Guest IV**: Are these golems works of art too? They look expensive, I'd like one in my collection.

**沙龙宾客Ⅰ**：把门打开，继续聆听这些疯话是对我人格的一种亵渎！！！\
**Guest I**: Open the door and let us go! This travesty is a disgrace!

特效-神秘术辉光

术法的辉光打在了戈连上，却没有留下任何踪迹。\
The glow of arcane skill strikes against the golem but leaves no trace of damage.

**行动队员**：该死，这些戈连是免疫神秘术的吗？我们靠近不了海因里希！\
**Team Member**: D**n, are these golems immune to arcanum? We can't get to Heinrich!

**马库斯**：霍夫曼女士，我读出来了，是操纵相关的神秘术刻痕，和基金会分部大门那次的情况一样！\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann, I read them! Object enchantment strokes, the same ones we found at the Foundation branch!

**霍夫曼**：有重塑之手的术式痕迹吗？\
**Hofmann**: Any signs of the Manus's rituals?

**马库斯**：没有，我还没有发现——\
**Marcus**: No, nothing yet.

霍夫曼点了点头，再次按下通讯器。\
Hofmann nods, pressing the communicator again.

**霍夫曼**：戈连只能从内部瓦解，马库斯，把方法告诉其他人。\
奥拉，疏散人群，动用消声咒，不能让更多人听到“时代”的信息了！\
**Hofmann**: Golems can only be broken from within. Marcus, tell everyone the method.\
Olla, evacuate everyone and use the mute spell. Don't let more people hear about the "era"!

她拿出配枪，拨开慌乱的人群。\
The mentor, now agent, draws her sidearm, pushing through the panicked crowd.

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

于戈连的缝隙中，她敏锐捕捉到一抹粉色的衣裙消失在挂画后方。\
Through the gaps between the golems, she keenly spots a pink dress disappearing behind a painting.

**霍夫曼**：——海因里希带着伊索尔德逃跑了，那幅画后有其他出口。\
**Hofmann**: Heinrich's escaped with Isolde. There's an opening behind the painting.

**霍夫曼**：跟上他们！\
**Hofmann**: After them!

## 6TH-13 岛 / The Island

低矮的石桌并不适宜写作，但此刻别无所选。\
The low stone table is ill-suited for writing, but there is little other choice for the moment.

**维尔汀**：……感谢您在委员会内做出的斡旋，我同意您的判断。\
**Vertin**: Thank you for your mediation within the committee. I think you're right.

**维尔汀**：贸然向岛上增派人员只会加剧眼前的信任危机，而这正是阿尔卡纳的目的。\
**Vertin**: Sending more people to the island will only exacerbate the trust issue. They don't trust us, and that's what Arcana wants.

**维尔汀**：目前局势刚刚和缓，任何加码都会让这台岌岌可危的天平立刻倾斜。\
**Vertin**: Things have just got better, and we can't let anything else upset this delicate balance.

**维尔汀**：而我的想法是——\
**Vertin**: I think ...

落笔犹豫了一瞬，最终，它还是被付诸纸上。\
The pen hesitates for a moment, but driven by need, it commits to the paper.

**维尔汀**：——即使我们最终无法与阿派朗学派达成合作，也必须阻止他们倒向重塑之手。\
**Vertin**: If we somehow can't come to an agreement with the Apeiron, we should at least prevent them from allying with the Manus in turn.

信件在指尖上停留片刻。\
The letter lingers dangerously on her fingertips.

然后，它扇动翅膀，像蝴蝶一般飞离客室，奔向圣洛夫基金会总部。\
Then, it flutters its wings, flying out of the room as a butterfly, heading at speed toward the headquarters of the St. Pavlov Foundation.

门口响起了适时的敲击声。\
A timely knock breaks the tension in her.

**维尔汀**：请进。\
**Vertin**: Come in please.

来人掀开了帘子。\
The visitor lifts the curtain.

阿派朗学派的客房并没有房门。\
The rooms of the School of Apeiron rarely have doors.

这只是照顾岛外客人的一个礼节。\
Such curtains are merely a courtesy for guests from beyond the island.

**玛尔塔**：早安，维尔汀小姐。\
**Marta**: Good morning, Ms. Vertin.

**玛尔塔**：我来询问您是否有什么需要帮助的。\
**Marta**: I'm here to see if you need help with anything.

**维尔汀**：能给我一些新的纸笔吗？\
**Vertin**: May I have some more paper?

**玛尔塔**：当然，我们从不会疏于给予沉思者的养料。\
**Marta**: Of course. We are always generous in our support of the contemplative.

**维尔汀**：……谢谢您，玛尔塔女士。\
**Vertin**: Thank you, Ms. Marta.

**维尔汀**：您不问我写信做什么吗？\
**Vertin**: Don't you want to ask me what I'm writing letters for?

**玛尔塔**：即使发生了诸多不快之事，但您灵魂数字的正直是毋庸置疑的。\
**Marta**: Despite all the unpleasant events, the integrity of your soul number is unquestionable.

学派的使者静静矗立着，眼帘下并未映出她的目光。\
The school's envoy stands silently, her gaze not reflected beneath narrowed eyelids.

**维尔汀**：……基金会总部正在极力与外界进行协商，以和平的方式平息这起莫须有的领土纠纷。\
**Vertin**: The Foundation is negotiating with the outside world. They're trying to resolve this unfounded territorial dispute peacefully.

**维尔汀**：我们并未泄露岛屿的坐标，也没有任何扩大冲突的意图。\
**Vertin**: We've yet to reveal the coordinates of the island, and don't want to exacerbate the conflict.

**维尔汀**：希望您代为传达我们的诚意。\
**Vertin**: Could you convey our sincere intentions?

**玛尔塔**：……呵呵，您明明还只是个孩子，说话却如此官方。\
**Marta**: ... Heh heh. You're such a young girl, yet you sound like an official.

她轻轻叹了一口气。\
She sighs resignedly.

**玛尔塔**：我也只是一个没有数字的修行者，在时代的风暴中漂至此处。时间并不比您长许久。\
**Marta**: But I'm just a practitioner without a number, a roamer of turbulent times. I haven't been on this island much longer than you.

**玛尔塔**：我会传达您的诉求，但我并没有裁决价值的资格。\
**Marta**: I will send your message, but I'm not the one who makes the decisions.

**玛尔塔**：——只是，以我对教义浅显的了解，您的努力并非他们所关心的，维尔汀小姐。\
**Marta**: It's just, from what I know about the teachings of Apeiron, what you're striving for is not of their concern, Ms. Vertin.

**维尔汀**：我不明白。\
**Vertin**: I don't understand.

**玛尔塔**：因为现象世界的一切琐碎，都是所有无足轻重中最为无关紧要的。\
**Marta**: All that is trivial in the phenomenal world is the trivialist of trivialities.

风自空洞处吹来。\
A wind blows in from beyond the void.

在海风拂来的方向，沙滩已经光复如新，不复数周前炮火打击的痕迹。\
In the direction of the sea breeze, one can see that the beach has been restored as if it were new, no longer bearing the scars of battle that had littered it only a short time ago.

**玛尔塔**：如果“流溢”降临，一切都会被冲刷。\
**Marta**: If the "Emanation" arrives, everything will be washed away.

**玛尔塔**：战争也好。纠纷也好。\
**Marta**: Wars, disputes.

**玛尔塔**：人们最关心的是……如何一劳永逸地获得“拯救”。\
**Marta**: Their number one priority is ... how to find "salvation," once and for all.

争论已经持续了数日。\
The debate has been ongoing for days.

这座真理的殿堂已经被现实的喧嚣占据。\
The Hall of Truth occupied by the clamor of their crushing reality.

**教众Ⅰ**：事实就是，我们正在误入歧途！\
**Believer I**: The fact is, we're going astray!

**教众Ⅰ**：1999年的“流溢”，令我们几乎损失了所有在外的联络点。\
**Believer I**: The "Emanation" in 1999 had taken away almost all our outside contacts.

**教众Ⅰ**：四年前的事故后，我们彻底切断了和外界的联系，在“流溢”中沦为一座孤岛！\
**Believer I**: Ever since the incident four years ago, we've been cut off from the outside world and have become an isolated island in the "Emanation."

**教众Ⅰ**：而这四年里，对“流溢”的研究毫无进展，对“流溢”规律的纯理论研究最终被证明为完全错误。\
**Believer I**: And during these four years, no research on the "Emanation" progressed. In the end, the theoretical study of its patterns was proven completely wrong.

**教众Ⅰ**：我们要这样被动到什么时候？到人类占领这里为止吗？！\
**Believer I**: How long should we sit idly by? Until the humans take over our island?

**教众Ⅰ**：基金会和重塑之手，肯定有一方要为这次的坐标暴露负责！\
**Believer I**: No matter who revealed our coordinates, be it the Foundation or Manus Vindictae, someone should be held responsible!

**教众Ⅱ**：“流溢”研究的负责人是37，你的质疑应当等她醒来，6已经在为她治疗。\
**Believer II**: 37 is the one in charge of studying the "Emanation." Save your questions until after she wakes up. 6 is treating her now.

**教众Ⅱ**：现在回顾四年前的方向选择也没有任何意义。\
**Believer II**: Also, talking about the decisions made four years ago is meaningless now.

**教众Ⅱ**：何况，基金会并未展露敌意，他们的确最小化了此次泄露事态的影响。\
**Believer II**: What's more, the Foundation is not hostile. They helped us minimize the damage from the reveal.

**教众Ⅱ**：在我们因四年前的失败陷入困难时，重塑之手也一直予以物资支持。\
**Believer II**: Manus Vindictae has also given us constant material support since that difficult time four years ago.

**教众Ⅲ**：哈，37……！她只是个孩子，连自己的事都搞不清楚。自从她带了那个外人去圣地，一切都变了……\
**Believer III**: Ha, 37? She's just a child, can't even handle her own business. Ever since she brought outsiders to the sacred place, everything has changed ...

**教众Ⅳ**：那你又为何要攻击一个尚在昏迷的孩子？！即使37做得不对，她也付出了代价！\
**Believer IV**: You know you're judging a child in a coma? Even if 37 did something wrong, she's certainly paying for it!

人们彼此瞪视，怒气冲冲。\
Those gathered glare at each other from the edges of the room, seething with anger.

这不是只待掷出卵石的正式表决，它甚至尚未得出明确的议题。\
Far from their formal votes awaiting the casting of stones—the debate has yet to even produce a clear topic of debate.

仅仅是往日对真理的探讨被现象世界的烟尘所搅乱。\
The pursuit of truth of days past, now muddied by the dust and blood of the phenomenal world.

**210**：不用如此恼火，我想42想说的其实很简单。\
**210**: Don't get angry. What 42 is trying to say is simple.

**210**：“即使‘流溢’到来后，人类的军队全都会化为乌有，可是‘流溢’什么时候会到来？”\
**210**: "Even if the 'Emanation' will take away the human army, when is it coming?"

**210**：“在模型失败之后，我们应该如何得知此事？又如何应对后续的‘流溢’？”\
**210**: "Now that our model has failed, how can we be informed of the next 'Emanation,' and act accordingly?"

**210**：“假如纯理论研究注定是失败的，我们必须向外探索，又得如何与外界重新建立联系？”\
**210**: "If pure theoretical research is doomed to failure, and if we must look outward, how can we restore communication with the outside world?"

**210**：“选择基金会，还是选择重塑之手？”\
**210**: "Do we stand with the Foundation, or with Manus Vindictae?"

台下响起了旗帜鲜明的反对声。\
A clear voice of opposition rises from below.

**教众Ⅲ**：210，你的发言诱导性太强了！\
**Believer III**: 210, your words are provocation!

**教众Ⅲ**：你是叫我们舍弃掉中立，卷入无止境的派系纠纷吗？这违背学派的基本立场！\
**Believer III**: Are you saying that we should stop being neutral and get involved in the endless faction disputes? This is against what Apeiron stands for!

**教众Ⅱ**：我也不能苟同您……真理应让人远离生之巨轮的流转，而不是踏入。\
**Believer II**: I can't agree either. The truth is supposed to keep us off the wheel of birth, not on it.

**210**：我只是翻译了一下42的潜台词。\
**210**: I was just interpreting what 42 had in mind.

**210**：况且，我们已经被迫卷入了生之巨轮的流转——人类的炮弹在这里落下过，是不争的事实。\
**210**: Moreover, we're already caught in the wheel of birth—human weapons were undeniably dropped on our island before.

**210**：后续扬起的烟尘，以及为此追责的意愿，只会让我们在这条链条里越陷越深。\
**210**: The tragedies it caused, and the thirst for justice will only keep us trapped in this cycle!

**210**：可这链条的起源是什么呢？\
**210**: But what caused this cycle to begin with?

**210**：敬爱的兄弟姐妹们，你们都被那些扬起的碎片迷花了眼，以至忽略了“本质”。让我来告诉你们吧——\
**210**: Brothers and sisters, you are blinded by the shrapnels of that conflict, and you're missing the "essence." Listen to me and I will tell you—

**教众Ⅳ**：你废话太多了，210，我看你是被扬起的形容词迷花了眼！\
**Believer IV**: Cut to the chase, 210! It seems you're the one blinded by your own rhetorics!

**教众Ⅲ**：谁能去6的座位上拿一下石钟？我今天非得敲晕他……\
**Believer III**: Who can get me the stone clock on 6's seat? I'll clobber him myself!

修辞学家只是讥讽地敲了敲额头，对同僚的不满置若罔闻。\
The rhetorician taps his forehead mockingly, ignoring the dissatisfaction of his cohorts.

**210**：一切的起源是，我们自身在“流溢”研究上遭遇的失败。\
**210**: The original cause, is the failure of our research on "Emanation."

**210**：我们的非凡来源于我们的信仰。一旦真理的光辉弃绝了我们，我们独立于世的基底便将不复存在。\
**210**: Our excellence comes from our beliefs. Once the truth fails us, the foundation that sets us apart from the world will also fail us.

**210**：但诸位智慧的同仁啊，请设想一下这种最坏的可能……\
**210**: However, my people of great wisdom, forgive me for imagining a worst case for you ...

**210**：我们笃信自然之书是用数学写成的，而每个数字都是居于永恒天国上的超越存在。\
**210**: We believe the book of nature was written in the language of mathematics, and every number is a transcendental existence living in the kingdom of eternity ...

**210**：通过数学，我们得以通达真理。通过对规律的找寻和计算，我们得以追寻世界最本质、最重要的知识：灵性的起源。\
**210**: Math is the path to truth. The calculation of math patterns has led us to pursue the fundamental knowledge of the world: the origin of pneuma.

**210**：但如果那至高无上的存在就是无规律的呢？如果那灵性的潮汐涌动就是混沌无理的呢？\
**210**: But, what if the supreme existence has no pattern at all? What if the ebb and tide of pneuma is chaotic and irrational?

一片哗然。\
An uproar ensues.

**教众Ⅲ**：210，你要否定所有人的信念吗？！\
**Believer III**: 210, are you denying our beliefs?

**教众Ⅲ**：按照这个说法，我们此前取得的切实成果，难道只是一种凑巧吗？\
**Believer III**: Are you saying the results we've achieved are just coincidences?

**教众Ⅲ**：古代数学应用至今的基础定理，现代数学对世界的切实改造和应用，潜藏在原子钟和叶脉序里的数理规律……\
**Believer III**: The fundamental theorems of ancient mathematics, the applications and improvements from modern mathematics, the mathematical laws in atomic clocks and leaf venation,

**教众Ⅲ**：先前每一个应验了的“流溢”年代，难道都是一场大梦吗？\
**Believer III**: and every prophecy of "Emanation" that were proven correct ... Were they all just a collective dream of ours?

**210**：哎，我只是请诸位设想一下最坏的可能。\
**210**: Well, like I said, I was just imagining a worst case scenario.

**210**：穷举也是一种证明的思路。\
**210**: Exhaustion is also a common method of proof.

这句若有可无的辩解消失在激烈的声讨中。\
Their further defense becomes untenable amid loud denunciations.

呼声一阵高过一阵，以至于穿过了殿堂的石墙，抵达门外无资格的旁观者耳中。\
The calls rise one after another, bouncing against the stone walls of the hall and reaching the ears of listeners outside as an echoed cacophony.

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

**苏菲亚**：无限定者啊，请您帮帮我……\
**Sophia**: Please help us, O Apeiron.

**苏菲亚**：清除我们灵魂的错误，纠正我们过度的倾向……使心灵适度于躯体，意志适度于生命，使城邦免于动乱，使身体免于灾厄……\
**Sophia**: Correct the errors of our souls, bring us back on the right path ... Harmonize our spirit with the flesh, our will with life; avoid sedition from a city; purge sickness from the body ...

**苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia**: ...

苏菲亚揉去泪水。\
Sophia wipes away her tears.

远处的沙滩上，群鸟正张翅飞行。\
A flock of seagulls flies over the beach.

它们盘旋起舞，双翼轻薄，像数只苍白的蝴蝶。\
They circle and dance in the air with an unusually delicate grace, more like butterflies than birds.

**苏菲亚**：……是我看错了吗？那似乎不是海鸥……\
**Sophia**: They don't look like seagulls, or am I mistaken?

除错师往前走去。\
The Corrector moves forward.

在一碧如洗的阳光中……\
Stepping into the crystal-clear sunlight ...

属于圣洛夫基金会特急信件的红色火漆清晰可见。\
Where the red wax seal of the St. Pavlov Foundation's express letter is clearly visible.

**苏菲亚**：这些全是……从岛外发来的？\
**Sophia**: Are these all from the outside world?

**苏菲亚**：外面……又发生什么了？\
**Sophia**: What's happening out there?

## 6TH-14 费切尔怪鸟 / Fitcher's Bird

**卡卡尼亚**：我找伊索尔德·冯·迪塔斯多夫。\
**Kakania**: I'm looking for Isolde von Dittarsdorf.

排气窗上出现了一双警惕的眼睛。\
Two vigilant eyes appear from within the vent.

来人沉默地看了一眼卡卡尼亚，打开了地下通道。\
The watcher silently looks over Kakania, then opens the underground passage.

**卡卡尼亚**：我找伊索尔德·冯·迪塔斯多夫。\
**Kakania**: I'm looking for Isolde von Dittarsdorf.

石墙的上方开启了一扇小窗。\
A small window opens high along the stone wall.

来人漠然地看了一眼卡卡尼亚，用钥匙开启了铁门。\
A different watcher now looks at Kakania again, more indifferently this time, unlocking the iron door with a key.

**卡卡尼亚**：我找伊索尔德·冯·迪塔斯多夫。\
**Kakania**: I'm looking for Isolde von Dittarsdorf.

衣着褴褛的小贩点点头，卡卡尼亚从未见过他。\
The ragged peddler, a stranger to Kakania, nods with strange recognition.

他将一件五颜六色的羽毛斗篷披到卡卡尼亚身上，快步穿越走廊。\
He drapes a colorful feathered cloak over Kakania and hurries through the corridor.

**卡卡尼亚**：……你确定这个可靠？\
**Kakania**: You sure this will work?

**小贩Ⅱ**：现在可不是您挑剔的时候，医生。有人愿意帮您就不错了。\
**Vendor II**: No time to complain, doctor. You should be very grateful that I'm helping you.

**小贩Ⅱ**：这是来自波西米亚的隐形斗篷，熬秃了整整两个巫婆的头发才炼制成功。就算您穿着它从卫兵的鼻子下走过，也不会有人认出您……\
**Vendor II**: This is an invisibility cloak from Bohemia. It took the hair of two witches to make one. No one will see you, even if you were right under their noses.

**卡卡尼亚**：……好。\
**Kakania**: ... Okay.

坚硬的羽毛披覆了全身，卡卡尼亚感觉自己是一只巨大的不会飞的彩色的鸟。\
The stiff feathers cover her entirely, making Kakania feel like an odd, flightless, if colorful bird.

忍耐着气味的不适，她加快了自己的脚步。\
Enduring the discomfort of the smell, she quickens her pace.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

仅有一个人能听到的脚步也叫人心跳加速。转过一个转角，又穿过一条走廊。\
The sound of her own footfalls accelerates her heartbeat, though she tries to remember they are only audible to her. She turns a corner, then passes through to another corridor.

这本该很顺利——如果没有一些意想不到的副作用。\
Things might well have gone smoothly—if not for some unexpected occurrences.

**维也纳警卫**：……？！\
**Vienna Guard**: ...?!

**维也纳警卫**：这是哪里来的羽毛？\
**Vienna Guard**: Where did the feathers come from?

**卡卡尼亚**：该死的，这玩意儿居然掉毛——！我早知道这类神秘学小商品没一个靠谱的！\
**Kakania**: Holy—it's losing feathers! I should have known these arcane devices were unreliable!

**卡卡尼亚**：明明就差几步了！\
**Kakania**: I'm so close!

卡卡尼亚索性奔跑起来，她飞扬的衣角脱离斗篷的覆盖，突兀出现在空气中。\
Kakania breaks into a run, her billowing skirt escaping the cloak's cover, and so appearing in the air behind her.

**维也纳警卫**：嘿，等等……\
**Vienna Guard**: Hey, wait.

**维也纳警卫**：那是通缉犯卡卡尼亚吗？！那个叛国贼！\
**Vienna Guard**: Isn't that the wanted criminal, Kakania?! That traitor!

**维也纳警卫**：扰乱治安，教唆叛国，使用神秘术蛊惑市民！竟然还敢到政府机关里来！\
**Vienna Guard**: Disturbing the peace, inciting treason, and bewitching citizens with arcane skills! How dare she infiltrate the government!

**维也纳警卫**：——停下，你被逮捕了！\
**Vienna Guard**: Halt, you're under arrest!

**卡卡尼亚**：……呼……呼！\
**Kakania**: *panting*

卡卡尼亚“砰”地关上房门，将追兵阻隔在身后。\
Kakania slams the door shut, barricading her pursuers behind her.

室内空旷得古怪。\
The room she finds herself in is oddly spacious.

在那尘封的书柜后，缓缓走出了一道倩影。\
A graceful figure emerges out from behind the bookshelves.

**伊索尔德**：……医生！您终于来了。\
**Isolde**: ... Doctor! You've finally come.

**伊索尔德**：我一直在等您……\
**Isolde**: I've been waiting for you.

伊索尔德像一缕幽魂般飘向卡卡尼亚。\
Isolde drifts toward Kakania like a wisp, as if not fully real.

**伊索尔德**：我一直在等您！您来的时候还顺利吗？您近来还无恙吗？\
**Isolde**: For so long! Was your journey here safe? How have you been?

卡卡尼亚只是警觉地向后退了一步。\
Kakania can't help but step back cautiously.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德，这究竟是怎么回事？您和海因里希究竟都做了什么？\
**Kakania**: Isolde, what is going on? What have you and Heinrich done?

**卡卡尼亚**：您为什么突然要在沙龙上那么说？一路上帮助我的人们又都是谁？\
**Kakania**: Why did you say that at the exhibition? Who were those people helping me on my way here?

**卡卡尼亚**：那些戈连，那条密道，那场骚乱又是怎么回事？\
**Kakania**: What's with the golems, the secret tunnels, and that turmoil?

**卡卡尼亚**：您突然消失，“魔圈”则被视为叛国组织，许多成员都遭到了通缉！\
**Kakania**: You vanished from the exhibition, and now "The Circle" is considered a treasonous organization and our members are now wanted!

**卡卡尼亚**：各大报纸都在痛斥我们，《新自由报》甚至评价为“和离家出走一般幼稚的叛国”……\
**Kakania**: Newspapers are criticizing us! The New Free Press called us "treasonous and naive, like a teenage runaway."

**卡卡尼亚**：如今“魔圈”真的成了那些官僚口中的危险团体，我也成了通缉犯！他们甚至认为，这场骚乱和之后的一系列动荡都是我策划的！\
**Kakania**: And now "The Circle" has become subversives, and I'm wanted! They even thought the chaos and subsequent turmoil were planned by me!

**卡卡尼亚**：这，这不是我组织它的初衷……！\
**Kakania**: This-this is not why I founded it!

**卡卡尼亚**：现在您又邀请我来会面，说为我找到了“实现理想的坦途”……\
**Kakania**: And now you invite me here, claiming to have found "the way to realize my dream" ...

**卡卡尼亚**：您完全把我弄糊涂了！您真的还是我所认识的伊索尔德吗？您……\
**Kakania**: You're confusing me! Are you still the Isolde I know? You ...

**伊索尔德**：医生，请您听我说！我一直都想告诉您，一直都想……\
**Isolde**: Please listen to me, doctor! I've been meaning to tell you, from the beginning.

**伊索尔德**：可是海因里希阻止了我，他说，画展是一个更合适的时机。\
**Isolde**: But Heinrich stopped me and told me the exhibition was a better time.

**伊索尔德**：他告诉我，您的理想是面向所有人的，所以我们也得在所有人面前宣告才行。\
**Isolde**: He said your dream is a dream for everyone, and that's why we should announce it in front of everyone.

**伊索尔德**：很抱歉，我不曾料想事情会这样。我让您的名誉受损了，您为此永远记恨我也是应当的。\
**Isolde**: I should apologize. I did not see this coming. I have discredited you, and you have every reason to hate me.

她失落地垂下了头，眼里的光芒一瞬间黯淡下去。\
She poorly hides the disappointment from her face, wilting as the light in her eyes dims momentarily.

**伊索尔德**：但您不用担心，医生，我向您保证，很快这一切都不用担心了。\
**Isolde**: But worry not, doctor, I give you my word, soon you won't have to worry about anything.

**伊索尔德**：那些人不理解您的理想，他们也不会成为您的同党。\
**Isolde**: These people don't understand your dream, and they won't become your allies.

**伊索尔德**：但是——我们是不同的！\
**Isolde**: But we—we are different!

**卡卡尼亚**：我们……？\
**Kakania**: We?

她皱起眉头，警觉地咀嚼着这个词。\
She furrows her brow, mulling over the word with full weight and prudence.

**卡卡尼亚**：……那位代您给我送来消息的先生，一路上引导我的那些人……他们的面孔如此陌生，我之前从未见过……\
**Kakania**: The mister who sent me your message, the people showing me the way, all were unfamiliar faces, I've never met any of them before.

**卡卡尼亚**：他们……不，“你们”是谁……？\
**Kakania**: Who are they? No, who are you?

**卡卡尼亚**：“你们”究竟想做什么？！\
**Kakania**: What is "your" purpose?

**伊索尔德**：呵呵……医生，这不重要，医生……！\
**Isolde**: Heh heh, doctor, it doesn't matter, doctor!

**伊索尔德**：重要的是，“我们”与您有着同样的梦想，“我们”与您憧憬着同一个乐土……\
**Isolde**: What matters is that, "we" share the same dream with you, "we" long for the same paradise as you do.

**伊索尔德**：那片流光溢彩的自由王国！\
**Isolde**: That glorious kingdom of freedom!

她朝着虚空动情地迈步，笑容一如舞台上美丽。\
She steps toward the void again with staged emotion, her smile as beautiful as it had been in any performance.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德小姐……您，您又出现幻觉了吗？\
**Kakania**: Isolde ... Are you seeing illusions again?

**伊索尔德**：不，医生，不。我已经完全痊愈了，您完全将我治愈了——！\
**Isolde**: No, doctor, I'm completely cured. You healed me!

**伊索尔德**：现在，轮到我同您一起治疗整个世界。剜掉那最上层的油彩，露出底色，重新塑造它——\
**Isolde**: And now, it's my turn to treat the world with you. Let's scrape the paint off the top, reveal its true colors, and reshape it.

**伊索尔德**：然后，将它变为完美的社会奉献到您的手上……！\
**Isolde**: Until it is transformed into a perfect world, a perfect society!

**伊索尔德**：因为我们是被选中的人……！\
**Isolde**: Because we are the chosen ones!

**卡卡尼亚**：你们……\
**Kakania**: You ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……是你们煽动了利奥波德区移民的骚动吗？还有那些以重塑社会为名的游行……\
**Kakania**: You planned the riots in Leopoldstadt, right? And the march demanding the transformation of society.

伊索尔德微笑着，沉默着。\
Isolde smiles half-mischievously.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德小姐，我不知道你受到了怎样的威胁和教唆，但你不能再和他们在一起了！\
**Kakania**: Isolde, I don't know what they said to threaten you, but you can't stay with them!

**卡卡尼亚**：这不是治疗——这是犯罪！\
**Kakania**: They're not treating you—you're committing a crime!

她恍惚着，感到了困惑。\
The actress stands bewildered, as if she had never considered it at all.

**伊索尔德**：可是，我完全是按照您所说的做的，医生。\
**Isolde**: But I did exactly what you told me to do, doctor.

**卡卡尼亚**：……我？\
**Kakania**: Me?

伊索尔德迈着轻盈的步伐，微微后退了两步。\
Isolde takes light steps, retreating but not turning.

**伊索尔德**：您告诉我，要解除压抑，释放内心的激情，做一个真诚、自由的人。\
**Isolde**: It was you who told me to stop repressing myself, to release my inner desires, and to be sincere, to be free.

她将以自己的艺术向那场精彩的独幕剧致敬——属于她的舞台拉开了帷幕。\
The graceful woman takes her place. Soon, she will pay homage to that splendid one-act play with her art—the curtain of her stage is about to rise.

视频-伊索尔德戴上重塑之手的面具。（如果有资源可以只把最后一句话做成视频，只做一个戴面具的动作）\
Isolde nods, turning in a move at first bashful.

伊索尔德微微颔首。

黑色的面具覆盖住她的面庞。\
But then her face returns, now hidden behind a black mask.

**伊索尔德**：您告诉我，社会生病了，世界需要一场大手术，神秘学家需要自己的新生活。\
**Isolde**: It was you who told me that our society needs a surgery, and that we arcanists need a new life that belongs to us.

**伊索尔德**：难道这不是您的梦想吗？\
**Isolde**: Is this not your dream?

**伊索尔德**：我只是……想把世界的真相献给您。\
**Isolde**: I just ... want to give you the truth of the world.

**伊索尔德**：想把您的梦想还给您。\
**Isolde**: I just want to give you back your dream.

## 6TH-15 重燃灯火时 / With Hope Rekindled

**霍夫曼**：把这些信全部烧毁，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: Burn these letters, Marcus.

**霍夫曼**：用符合《外勤派遣手册》第三百四十一条的安全方式，不能让我们之外的人再次阅读。\
**Hofmann**: Destroy them in accordance with the Field Mission Manual Article 341 so that no one else can read them.

霍夫曼快步走着，将刚刚查阅完毕的信件递给旁边的助手。\
Hofmann walks briskly, handing over the latest reviewed letter to her assistant.

**马库斯**：好的，霍夫曼女士……可是我们不用回复委外合约小队吗？\
**Marcus**: Ok, Madam Hofmann ... But shouldn't we reply to these messages from the Field squad?

**霍夫曼**：不用，这些密信是寄给所有在外执勤的四级以上的调查员的。\
**Hofmann**: Don't bother. The secret letters are sent to all active investigators above rank four.

**霍夫曼**：委外合约小队就像是临界点的勘察队。他们会收集并记录与历史出入的大事件，汇总给基金会，作为当前时代稳定性的参数来源。\
**Hofmann**: The squad is like the watchers of the Critical Points. They collect and record every event different to the ones in history and report to the Foundation. These incidents will be the index for evaluating the stability of the current era.

**霍夫曼**：换而言之，他们的报告寄来的越多，时代的不稳定性就越强。\
**Hofmann**: In other words, the more reports they send, the more unstable the era is.

**霍夫曼**：这项同步措施是为了方便一线调查员判断目前的局势，及时规划下一步，因为过去有太多信息不通导致的悲剧。\
**Hofmann**: This keeps every field investigator up to date on the situation so they can plan their next move. In the past, we have seen too many tragedies caused by a lack of information.

**霍夫曼**：——我们自己的任务比这更紧急。\
**Hofmann**: But now, our own task is more urgent.

霍夫曼女士紧咬着嘴唇，带着马库斯快速经过一个拐角。\
Hofmann bites her lip, rushing Marcus around a corner.

近来发生的变故让她的头发又白了几分。\
Recent events have added a few more strands of white to her hair.

**霍夫曼**：“魔圈”公开叛国，伊索尔德和海因里希不见踪影，卡卡尼亚被通缉。\
**Hofmann**: "The Circle" publicly committed treason, Isolde and Heinrich disappeared, Kakania became wanted.

**霍夫曼**：利奥波德区移民的暴乱和下层神秘学家组织的游行，很可能也与之有直接关系。\
**Hofmann**: The Leopoldstadt riots and the march of the lower-class arcanists may be directly related to them.

**霍夫曼**：伊索尔德和海因里希的宣言就像一枚火苗，点燃了维也纳这口炸锅……这段时间的骚动就没停止过。\
**Hofmann**: Heinrich and Isolde's speech is like the spark that ignited the powder keg that is Vienna. The riots have been going on for days.

**马库斯**：可是……为什么反倒是卡卡尼亚小姐被官方通缉？\
**Marcus**: But ... Why was Ms. Kakania wanted?

**马库斯**：她在沙龙上没有做任何出格的举动，也表现得毫不知情。她只是得到了那本不属于时代的小说，海因里希显然什么都没有告诉她！\
**Marcus**: She didn't act out of line in the exhibition, and seemed totally unaware of the speech. All she had was the book which didn't belong to this era. Clearly, Heinrich didn't tell her a thing!

**霍夫曼**：因为她是“魔圈”公开的创始人，也是一个缺乏背景的中产阶级。\
**Hofmann**: It's because she is the known founder of "The Circle," and a middle class with no background.

**霍夫曼**：这对我们是好消息，马库斯，卡卡尼亚是一个突破口——他们没保下她，说明她还没被这个精英贵族团体正式吸纳。\
**Hofmann**: This is good news for us, Marcus. We can start with Kakania. They didn't protect her from being wanted, which means she hasn't been fully assimilated into this elite group of nobles.

**霍夫曼**：这很符合重塑之手一贯的精英血种主义作风，我们得尽快找到她。\
**Hofmann**: How typical of Manus Vindictae. We need to find her fast.

**霍夫曼**：幸运的是，你之前放到她身上的“蛛尾巴”终于又有了反应——\
**Hofmann**: Luckily, the Spider Tail you put on her is reacting.

“——砰！”\
*crash*

碎石擦着头顶飞过。\
Stones scrape over the top of her head.

调查员们错愕地回头。\
The investigators turn back in shock.

基金会驻维也纳分部的入口石像被炸得粉身碎骨。\
The statue standing at the entrance to the Foundation's Vienna branch has just been shattered to pieces.

四楼的窗户处，传来一声歇斯底里的大笑。\
A hysterical laugh can be heard booming from the fourth-floor window.

**暴动分子**：哈哈哈哈！去死吧！你们这些陈腐、肮脏的官僚！\
**Rioter**: Hahahaha! Go to hell, you dirty, disgusting officials!

**暴动分子**：——为了自由的王国！\
**Rioter**: For a kingdom of freedom!

**马库斯**：……！\
**Marcus**: ...!

**马库斯**：为了……自由的王国……\
**Marcus**: For a ... kingdom of freedom ...?

**霍夫曼**：见鬼，他们竟然猖狂到直接对基金会分部动手吗？\
**Hofmann**: Shoot, they're attacking the Foundation branch?

**霍夫曼**：其他事先慢点想，马库斯！有人在卡特纳大道上召集了大量魔精，正朝这边过来了！\
**Hofmann**: Focus on what's important, Marcus! Someone's summoned a bunch of critters on Carinthian Street! They're coming this way!

**霍夫曼**：咳咳……！\
**Hofmann**: *coughing*

气味古怪的烟尘在街道上弥漫，使原本混乱的场面变得更加棘手。\
A strangely scented smoke spreads out over the street, making the already chaotic scene even more incomprehensible.

**霍夫曼**：这个烟雾不对劲……！像是某种汽化后的神秘术药剂。咳！这个味道……应该有魔鬼鞋带的成分。唔，为了增加扩散性吗？\
**Hofmann**: Something's wrong with this mist. Maybe the evaporation of the arcane potion. *cough* Devil's Shoestring, judging by the smell ... For better diffusivity?

**霍夫曼**：马库斯，捂住口鼻。等它散去后我们再进入基金会分部。\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, cover your mouth and nose. We'll enter the Foundation's branch when it clears up.

霍夫曼拉着马库斯的手快速穿越人潮，避免再吸入更多的不明气体。\
Hofmann pulls Marcus's hand, darting through the crowd at speed to avoid inhaling more of the unknown gas.

这是一处尚未被混乱裹挟的空地。\
At last, they reach an area not yet engulfed by chaos.

此时，唯有稍作等待。\
For now, all that's left for them is to wait.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

第一次执行任务的青涩调查员愣然地站着，表情是前所未有的呆滞。\
The unseasoned investigator stands stunned and uncharacteristically vacant in mind.

**霍夫曼**：……怎么了，马库斯，这道烟雾对你的身体出现了什么影响吗？\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, are you ok? Did the mist get to you?

**马库斯**：不是的……\
**Marcus**: No ...

马库斯低下头，她的额头上泛起了一层冷汗。\
Marcus pats her head, where a layer of cold sweat has formed.

**马库斯**：霍夫曼女士，刚刚的暴动分子，还有游行队伍里的人，他们喊着“为了自由的王国”的口号……\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann, the terrorists and the people in the march, what they shouted, "for a kingdom of freedom" ...

**马库斯**：这，这是伊索尔德小姐在沙龙上的发言。她的话语又引用自卡卡尼亚医生……\
**Marcus**: That's-that's what Ms. Dittarsdorf said in the exhibit, and she quoted that from Dr. Kakania ...

**马库斯**：而在最早，是我……是我把这些话告诉了卡卡尼亚！我告诉了她那座岛的事，我告诉她那是一个神秘学家的自由地……！\
**Marcus**: And-and it was me ... I told that to Dr. Kakania! I told her about the island, I told her it's a place of freedom for arcanists!

**马库斯**：点燃这场灾害的人，其实是我……！是我泄露了黄金岛的机密，导致了后续的连锁！\
**Marcus**: So-so I'm the one who caused this turmoil! I told them the secret of the Golden Isle and caused the chain reaction!

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

霍夫曼女士也沉默了片刻。\
Hofmann seems to have neither words of comfort nor criticism planned. She bites her tongue in her mouth.

马库斯近乎崩溃地蹲下，抱住了头。\
Marcus, meanwhile, collapses slowly to the ground as she holds her head.

**马库斯**：我没有聆听您的教导……我，太冲动了，缺乏理智，不稳定，不可控，唯一可取的神秘术也没有派上用场……\
**Marcus**: I didn't listen to you ... I'm too reckless, I lack rational thinking, I'm unstable and out of control ... And the one thing I can control, my arcane skill, didn't help at all ...

**马库斯**：您承担了风险，将我从总部带出来参加外勤，可是我……！\
**Marcus**: You vouched for me and appointed me to the field mission from the headquarters, but I ...!

**霍夫曼**：……也许是这样吧。\
**Hofmann**: ... Maybe it is like what you said.

霍夫曼揉着太阳穴，罔顾下属的脸色变得愈发煞白。\
Hofmann rubs her temples figuratively, ignoring the now-pale complexion of her subordinate.

**霍夫曼**：也许你的确错误参与了时代的一隅，在一系列偶然的碰撞下，引发了历史的震荡。\
**Hofmann**: Maybe you did play a role in this era, causing a butterfly effect in history ...

**霍夫曼**：但试图为超出自己能力的一切事情负责，只是一种非理性的狂妄。\
**Hofmann**: But trying to be responsible for everything beyond one's capability is a symbol of irrational hubris.

**马库斯**：——！\
**Marcus**: —!

**霍夫曼**：首先，在这个民族冲突、刺杀案、间谍案频出的时代，制造混乱本就是极容易的。\
**Hofmann**: First of all, creating chaos in this chaotic time is more than easy. Just look at all the frequent ethnic conflicts, assassinations, and espionage.

**霍夫曼**：没有“魔圈”与伊索尔德，重塑之手也会找到另一枚引信。\
**Hofmann**: If not "The Circle" and Isolde, the Manus will find themselves a different flashpoint.

**霍夫曼**：你也无从事先知晓泄露给卡卡尼亚的信息会如何发酵，它的后续扩散属于不可抗力，再为此懊悔是无用的。\
**Hofmann**: You never know how the leaked information will simmer. Its subsequent spread is uncontrollable, and remorse would be useless.

**霍夫曼**：更显著的事实是，人们早已对那座岛冠以自己的期望，你只是印证了他们原有的想法。\
**Hofmann**: The thing is, everyone has their own ideas about that island. Your words just deepened their expectations.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

她的脸颊终于又有了血色。\
Her cheeks finally regain some color.

**霍夫曼**：至于你的自我评价……\
**Hofmann**: As for your self assessment ...

**霍夫曼**：我们都听过这样的说法：人类更加理智，神秘学家更加感性。\
**Hofmann**: We have all heard it: humans are more rational and arcanists are more emotional.

**霍夫曼**：他们对世界的幽微之处更加敏感，因此也更容易沉浸于自我的情绪，忽略客观的现实。\
**Hofmann**: They're sensitive to the darkness in the world, so they can easily become absorbed in their own emotions and ignore reality.

**霍夫曼**：但我想，倘若将一个人类孩子放到神秘学家的处境，倘若他从小就要因为独特而对抗世界，因为天赋而不被理解——\
**Hofmann**: But if we put a human child in the position of an arcanist, who always takes on the world because of his uniqueness, who is never understood for his talents ...

**霍夫曼**：那么或许，他也会变得冲动，敏感，不成熟，不稳定。\
**Hofmann**: Maybe he too will become impulsive, sensitive, immature and unstable.

**霍夫曼**：由此，我曾经想过：如果将一个神秘学家孩子放到人类的处境，倘若他能接受充分的关爱、良好的教育、足够的正向反馈——\
**Hofmann**: And that's why it sometimes dawns on me that if we put an arcanist child in the position of a human being who receives enough love, education, and positive feedback ...

**霍夫曼**：……这些“不稳定”就至少是可控的——至少，不会让他们烧伤自己，烧伤他人。\
**Hofmann**: These "instabilities" might be controllable. At least enough to keep them from hurting themselves or others.

**马库斯**：霍夫曼女士……\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann ...

**霍夫曼**：我曾在1912年那场“暴雨”中将你带离。这么长的日子里，我知道时间再度拨回这个时代——拨回1914年，对你来说是何种珍贵之事。\
**Hofmann**: I took you away from the "Storm" in 1912. It's been a long time after that, so I know how precious it must be for you to return to 1914.

**霍夫曼**：我理解你想迫切完成任务，重回罗马尼亚看看的心情。\
**Hofmann**: And your urge to complete the mission, and go back to Romania.

**霍夫曼**：……你并不是冲动，马库斯，你只是还在成长。\
**Hofmann**: You're not an impulsive person, Marcus, you're just growing up.

**霍夫曼**：你也需要成长。\
**Hofmann**: And you do need to grow.

霍夫曼将手放到嘴边，小声咳嗽了几声。\
Hofmann brings her hand to her mouth, coughing softly and hesitantly.

**霍夫曼**：至于我申请将你从总部调出来，是我个人的想法。\
**Hofmann**: As for appointing you, it was by my own will.

**霍夫曼**：——因为，人类的时代已经结束了。\
**Hofmann**: Because, the age of humans has come to an end.

**马库斯**：……人类的时代……结束？\
**Marcus**: The age of humans ... is ending?

马库斯摇摇晃晃地站起身来。\
Marcus staggers back to her feet.

不同于她的惊讶，霍夫曼女士的面色并无波澜。\
Contrary to her expectations, Hofmann's expression is unchanged.

仿佛只是在陈述一件既定的事实。\
As if she is merely stating an established fact.

**霍夫曼**：如果时代持续倒退，那么人类的科技成果不会积攒下来。\
**Hofmann**: If the eras keep on regressing, human technologies would fail to accumulate.

**霍夫曼**：而完全仰赖个人能力的神秘术会大放异彩。\
**Hofmann**: Meanwhile, arcane skills that depend largely on the individual's potential, will shine.

**霍夫曼**：在这场重返未来的时间战争中，最终留存的会是你们，而非我们。因此，你迟早需要独当一面。\
**Hofmann**: In this war of reversals, futures, and time, it is you who will survive, not us. And that's why sooner or later, you'll have to go at it alone.

**霍夫曼**：——为了文明的延续，我只是做了最理性的判断。\
**Hofmann**: This is the most rational assessment I can make for the continuation of civilization.

**马库斯**：理性……\
**Marcus**: Rational ...

**马库斯**：可是，我也很努力地去运用它了。我不断地阅读，反复地练习，用训练的方式分析信息……\
**Marcus**: But I've been doing my best to be rational as well. Even though I keep reading and practicing information analysis ...

**马库斯**：但我做不出选择。万一我选择的是错的呢？万一这里就没有正确答案呢？如果我当初没有告诉卡卡尼亚……\
**Marcus**: I ... can't make a choice. What if I make a wrong choice? What if there's no right answer? What if I never told Kakania about ...

**霍夫曼**：——停，你又步入幽微了。\
**Hofmann**: Enough. You're getting carried away.

**霍夫曼**：理性并不神秘，它很多时候只是一种思维的工具。带我们走出幽微，重回事情的本质。\
**Hofmann**: There is nothing mysterious about rationality. It simply guides us out of confusion and straight to the essence of things.

**马库斯**：本质……？\
**Marcus**: The essence?

**霍夫曼**：我们为何会在此执行任务，其实是一件非常简单的事，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: The reason why we're doing a job here is simple, Marcus.

**霍夫曼**：神秘学家接连不断地倒向重塑，是因为他们许诺“拯救”，而我们不能。\
**Hofmann**: Arcanists keep going to the Manus. It's because they can promise the "salvation," while we can't.

**霍夫曼**：因此最重要的是破译重塑免疫“暴雨”的术式。倘若我们做不到，仅凭一小块孤立的土地，早晚会在这场时间灾害中走向灭亡。\
**Hofmann**: Therefore, decoding their immunity ritual against the "Storm" is top priority. If we can't, being isolated on a small piece of land, we're bound to meet our end in this temporal catastrophe.

**霍夫曼**：总部派出的调查员并非只有我们。我们只需要尽可能地追查、搜集重塑留下的神秘学痕迹，并将它传回科算中心。\
**Hofmann**: We are not the only investigators sent by the headquarters. So our mission is to collect every clue left by the Manus and send them back to Laplace.

**霍夫曼**：除此之外，一切都是次要的。\
**Hofmann**: Everything else is secondary.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

马库斯紧紧抿着嘴唇，不再言语。\
Marcus presses her lips tightly, not wanting to speak.

她深呼吸，跟随着霍夫曼女士如灯塔般的话语步出幽微。\
She takes a deep breath, following Hofmann's words as they step out of the darkness.

——只是专心致志地思考着现有的状况。\
She can do nothing more than focus intently on their current situation.

**马库斯**：……霍夫曼女士，除了卡卡尼亚，我们也许还有另一个突破口。\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann, besides finding Ms. Kakania, there may be another way.

**马库斯**：那幅画，西奥菲尔的遗作，《拯救》。它有问题。\
**Marcus**: That painting, the last work of Theophil, The Salvation. Something's off with it.

**马库斯**：在沙龙上再次阅读它时，我察觉到了一种似曾相识的“灵感”。它被巧妙地遮掩了，遮掩的痕迹却留了下来。\
**Marcus**: When I read it in the exhibition, I felt a familiar afflatus. It was concealed in a clever way, but I noticed the traces of concealment.

**霍夫曼**：……重塑之手的神秘术吗？\
**Hofmann**: Manus's arcane skill?

马库斯犹豫了片刻，点了点头，又摇了摇头。\
Marcus hesitates for a moment, performing at once a nod and shaking her head, creating a muddled response.

**马库斯**：但是我的探知范围有限，无法再进一步阅读。如果我们能说服卡卡尼亚小姐，让她用自己的神秘术帮忙的话……\
**Marcus**: But I couldn't read anything more from it. If we can persuade Ms. Kakania to help us with her arcane skill ...

**霍夫曼**：她的神秘术也是你这个领域的吗？\
**Hofmann**: Is her arcane skill similar to yours?

**马库斯**：不，很不一样。但我和她交手过，我想，也许有一种可能，如果能集齐一些条件，我们也许可以互补……\
**Marcus**: No, quite different. I fought her once. I feel that under certain conditions, our arcane skills might be complementary.

马库斯全心假设着，又一次陷入了自己的思维漫游中。\
Marcus posits wholeheartedly, once again drifting into her own thoughts.

**霍夫曼**：很好，马库斯。这是只有你能做到的事。\
**Hofmann**: Well done, Marcus. This is something only you can do.

**霍夫曼**：那幅画现在被政府收容，我们可以让委外合约小队帮忙拿回。\
**Hofmann**: The government has the painting now. The Field Agent Squad can retrieve it for us.

霍夫曼点了点头，给子弹上好膛。\
Hofmann nods, loading more bullets into the chamber.

**霍夫曼**：——烟雾已经散了，走吧。\
**Hofmann**: The fog is cleared. Let's go.

**霍夫曼**：眼下，我们要先找到卡卡尼亚。\
**Hofmann**: Now, we need to find Kakania.

## 6TH-16 林间旅途 / Quest in the Woods

**卡卡尼亚**：您在说什么……？\
**Kakania**: What are you talking about?

**卡卡尼亚**：“暴雨”、战争……？我不明白。\
**Kakania**: The "Storm," the war ...? I don't understand.

卡卡尼亚捂住头，仓促地后退一步。\
Kakania covers her head, retreating backwards.

**卡卡尼亚**：如果你们说的话是真的，那我们所生活的这个世界，这个时代，以及在其上生活的一切人……\
**Kakania**: If that's true, then the world we are living in, the era, and the people ...

**卡卡尼亚**：都会在不久后迎来毁灭？\
**Kakania**: Everything will be destroyed in the near future?

窗外，是暴乱发生后升起的滚滚浓烟。远远的，咖啡厅落地窗被石子砸碎，人们四散奔逃。\
Outside, the thick smoke of the riot rises. Far away, the windows of the café are shattered by debris, and people scatter in all directions.

而在更远处的那些辉煌殿堂里，种满玫瑰的精致府邸里，这个庞大帝国的华尔兹舞曲仍在奏响。\
And in the distant grand halls, and in the exquisite mansions filled with roses, the waltz of the great empire continues to play.

**卡卡尼亚**：——“被拣选者能通过‘暴雨’”，那其他人呢？那些对“暴雨”一无所知的，千千万万的人们呢？\
**Kakania**: "Only the chosen ones will survive the 'Storm.'" What about the others? Millions out there have never even heard of the "Storm"!

**伊索尔德**：唯有被拣选者能通过“暴雨”。这是一场试炼呀，医生。\
**Isolde**: Yes, only the chosen ones will survive the "Storm." This is a trial, doctor.

她依然微笑着，平静着。\
She remains smiling and calm, like an uncanny portrait of her former self.

卡卡尼亚觉得自己不再熟悉她了。\
A person Kakania feels she no longer knows ... or maybe never did.

**卡卡尼亚**：试炼……？\
**Kakania**: A trial?

**卡卡尼亚**：那又是谁发起了试炼，又是谁决定了拣选的标准？\
**Kakania**: Then who started it? Who decided the standard?

**卡卡尼亚**：您吗？所谓的引导之人吗？神吗？至高无上的、伟大的、超越的存在吗？！\
**Kakania**: You? Or the so-called Guiding One? God? Or the supreme existence?

**卡卡尼亚**：——是谁给了他们这种决定他人生死的权力，让这一切荒诞理所当然地发生？\
**Kakania**: Who gave them the power to decide the fate of others? Who allows such absurdities to happen?

她近乎不解地上前一步，问出发自内心的困惑。\
She steps forward with each salvo in her barrage of questions, voicing the confusion burning in her mind.

**卡卡尼亚**：又是什么叫作“秩序正确的过去”？倘若时代只是不断地倒退，又要退到什么地方、什么时候？\
**Kakania**: What is "the past with the right order"? If time just keeps going backwards, when and where will it stop?

**卡卡尼亚**：退到所有人不复存在之前吗？退到文明也不复存在之前吗？\
**Kakania**: To a time when man did not exist? Or to a time before civilization?

**卡卡尼亚**：那我们所追求的一切，这些诗歌、艺术、文化，一切的进步和创造——又有什么意义？！\
**Kakania**: Then why did we write poems, pursue art, and develop civilization? Why did we try so hard to make progress? What was the point of it all?!

她的胸膛因几乎焚毁大脑的困惑与怒火剧烈起伏着。\
Her chest heaves like a burning furnace, rage red-hot in her face.

而她对面，那张精致的面庞上，眉毛只是微微皱了皱。\
Meanwhile, the delicate figure ahead only slightly furrows its brow.

**伊索尔德**：我不明白，医生……\
**Isolde**: I don't understand, doctor ...

那张脸上充满真实的困惑，她甚至轻轻地歪了歪头——\
The cold face tilts as if taken with genuine bewilderment.

**伊索尔德**：——您为什么这么在意“其他人”呢？\
**Isolde**: Why are you so concerned about "the others"?

**卡卡尼亚**：……？！\
**Kakania**: ...?!

卡卡尼亚突然觉得手脚冰凉。\
Kakania suddenly feels a chill rising from her hands and feet.

**伊索尔德**：倘若我们前往了新世界……我们就能完全按照您的梦想去设计它，创造一个所有人都能幸福的自由王国。\
**Isolde**: When we reach the new world ... we can fully realize your dream. We will create a kingdom of freedom for everyone!

**伊索尔德**：而这些旧世界的残余……这些病灶上的创口，罹患恶疾的病体，理应切除的存在……\
**Isolde**: As for the embers of the old world ... they are like a tumor that should be removed ...

**伊索尔德**：您又为什么要在意呢？\
**Isolde**: Why care about them?

**卡卡尼亚**：理应切除……？\
**Kakania**: A tumor that should be removed ...?

卡卡尼亚看着她躬身行礼。\
Kakania watches her bow.

她仍伫立于舞台之上。\
She remains standing on the stage.

伊索尔德轻轻提起裙摆，她摇晃着身体，像是在起舞；她声音婉转，如同歌唱。\
Isolde gently lifts her skirt, swaying her body as if dancing. Her voice melodious, as if singing.

再无第二人能听到的舞曲伴随着窗外的爆炸声轰然奏起。\
No one else hears the silent waltz she's dancing to beneath the drumbeat of explosions outside.

**伊索尔德**：您看呀，这画幅如此混乱！\
**Isolde**: Look at this painting. How chaotic it is!

**伊索尔德**：您瞧呀，这些幽微之处的压抑，埋藏在人们心中的野兽，金箔之下的腐烂。\
**Isolde**: Look at the repression in the darkness. Look at the beasts in the people's hearts, and the maggots under the golden surface.

**伊索尔德**：我听见它来，一如它聆听我。\
**Isolde**: I listen to them, as they listen to me.

**伊索尔德**：这些颅骨内的幽暗回响，色彩混乱的灵性之声，理性裱画旁的污点，光辉大道前的污渍——\
**Isolde**: The shadowy echoes inside the skulls, the cacophonies of chaotic colors, the smudges on the canvas of rationality, and the filth in front of magnificent boulevards ...

**伊索尔德**：它们曾被切割、被无视、被剜掉最上层的油彩，涂抹成千篇一律的白。\
**Isolde**: They were excised, suppressed, the top paint scraped off and replaced with an empty, monotonous white.

**伊索尔德**：可它们终会释放，释放，向一切敞开！\
**Isolde**: Yet in the end, they will be released, to the fullest, to everything!

她转了一圈，那是华尔兹的舞步，裙摆随着高跟的缎面鞋子温驯地画了一个圆。\
She spins, performing the steps of her waltz, her skirt tracing a circle as demure as the satin shoes on her feet.

随着她的起舞，窗口处传来一声巨大的轰鸣。\
As she dances, a close cacophonous roar rises from the window.

**卡卡尼亚**：——？！\
**Kakania**: ...?!

**卡卡尼亚**：这是……楼下发生了爆炸？您——\
**Kakania**: Downstairs ... Is that an explosion? You ...

眼前的舞者让她感到危险。但鞋子上像是被涂满了松脂，挪不开半步。\
The dancer before her suddenly seems more dangerous than ever, but her feet are stuck, as if coated in resin, unable to move a step.

**伊索尔德**：西奥菲尔离开了！他如愿以偿，谢幕得熠熠生辉。\
**Isolde**: Theophil has left! He shone like a star in the end, just as he wished.

**伊索尔德**：可余下的人，那石子儿砸碎了玻璃——他们仍在挣扎着。\
**Isolde**: But the rest of them, with their rocks and shattered windows, are still left to struggle.

**伊索尔德**：我要是能像帮西奥菲尔一样，也能帮帮他们就好了。\
**Isolde**: If only I could help them, just like how I helped Theophil.

**卡卡尼亚**：……什么意思，您帮助了西奥菲尔？\
**Kakania**: ... What do you mean you helped Theophil?

她笑了，那弧度充满了甜蜜的怜悯。\
She smiles—an arc filled with saccharine pity.

**伊索尔德**：您没有听到！您没有看到。\
**Isolde**: You didn't hear him! You were not there.

**伊索尔德**：他奔逃着向我走来，结结巴巴，仓促地呼唤我的名。\
**Isolde**: He ran at me, stuttering my name.

**伊索尔德**：火焰灼烧着他的每寸皮肤，他如此痛苦，如此舒展。\
**Isolde**: Every inch of his skin was ravaged by flame. So much pain. So much spectacle.

**伊索尔德**：我要去找水来！可他已被点燃。\
**Isolde**: "I need to get water!" But he was already on fire.

**伊索尔德**：流动的汁液，只存在于他的脑浆、他的血管。\
**Isolde**: And the only water I found was in his skull and veins.

她忽地停住了，就像是乐谱奏到了休止符。\
She suddenly stops, as if the music score has reached a rest.

伊索尔德的手臂伸得笔直。她拇指向上，食指向前，小臂轻轻一抬。\
Isolde's arm extends straight. Her thumb points up, her index finger extends forward pointedly, her forearm lifts into a shooter's stance.

**伊索尔德**：——砰。\
**Isolde**: Bang.

这声虚空的枪响同样落在了卡卡尼亚身上。\
The sound of this empty gunshot pierces straight through Kakania, as surely as a bullet.

**卡卡尼亚**：不，伊索尔德小姐……伊索尔德……您……\
**Kakania**: No, Ms. Dittarsdorf ... Isolde ... You ...

**卡卡尼亚**：您是主动朝西奥菲尔开的枪——？\
**Kakania**: You shot Theophil on purpose ...?

医生的双唇嗫嚅着，吐出一个只有自己听得清的疑问。\
The doctor's lips mutter, voicing the question as if to herself, as if searching for the proof in her own memory.

她仍记得那日怀抱中脆弱的颤动，还有颈项处被泪水浸湿的触感。\
She still remembers the fragile trembling that filled her embrace that day, and the sensation of tears soaking her neck.

**卡卡尼亚**：这才是您压抑的真实吗——？您——\
**Kakania**: So this is the truth you had repressed? You ...

演员转过身来，她从未如此真实。\
The actress turns around, never before so true to life.

**伊索尔德**：医生，您说得对，解除压抑和禁锢，正是治疗的第一步。——现在我已经完全康复了！\
**Isolde**: You were right, doctor. Lifting your repression is the first step to liberation. I am fully cured!

**伊索尔德**：——您瞧，我做得好吗？\
**Isolde**: Look at me. Did I do a good job?

**卡卡尼亚**：……！\
**Kakania**: ...!

楼下再度传来了爆炸声，烟雾在街道上弥漫。\
Once again, an explosion rocks the ground from below, and smoke begins to pour over the streets, rising into view.

这个历史悠久的房间同样被震起了阵阵灰尘。\
This room, so rich in history, is shaken by bursts of long-aged dust.

**伊索尔德**：来吧，医生，我邀请您，正如您曾邀请我的那样。\
**Isolde**: Come with me, doctor. I am inviting you, just like how you invited me.

**伊索尔德**：——与我们一同拯救这个世界，治疗这个世界！\
**Isolde**: Let's heal the world and save it together!

她伸出手，面前却已经空无一人。\
The actress turns and reaches out, but now there is no one before her.

只有来时的房门还开着。\
Only an empty door.

**伊索尔德**：……？\
**Isolde**: ...?

**伊索尔德**：医生……？\
**Isolde**: Doctor ...?

**卡卡尼亚**：呼，呼——\
**Kakania**: *pants*

她奔跑着，头脑一片空白。\
She runs, her mind forcefully blank.

没有思考原因的余裕，只是基于本能的逃离。\
Without the luxury of reason, direction, or purpose, she flees on instinct alone.

终于，来时的道路隐没了，一切在烟尘中开始歪曲。\
Finding her way back quickly reaches a dead end. The path she came by is obscured. Everything warping beneath the unsettled dust.

**小贩Ⅰ**：啊，那是卡卡尼亚医生吗？！\
**Vendor I**: There, is that Ms. Kakania?!

**小贩Ⅰ**：嘿，大家别紧张，卡卡尼亚医生和我们是一块的！她之前帮了很多忙！\
**Vendor I**: Relax, people. Ms. Kakania is on our side! She has helped us a lot!

**卡卡尼亚**：伊里奇……\
**Kakania**: Illich ...

伊里奇身后站着一群浩浩荡荡的怪人——\
Behind Illich stands a throng of bizarre figures.

拿不到居留证的移民，付不出房钱的工人，失去土地的农民，讨不到生意的小商贩，在城市里无处可去的魔精。\
Immigrants without residence permits, workers who can't pay their rent, farmers who have lost their land, traders who can't afford their wares, critters with nowhere to go within the city.

**卡卡尼亚**：你们这是在……？\
**Kakania**: What are you doing ...?

**小贩Ⅰ**：有个美国来的先生告诉我们能大干一场，我就把大家都叫来了！\
**Vendor I**: A gentleman from America said we could do something big here, so I gathered everyone!

**小贩Ⅰ**：从卡特纳大道开始，一路走到维也纳分部入口，口号就喊“为了神秘学家的自由和平等”……真是地道的美国佬！\
**Vendor I**: We will march down to the Carinthian Street, to the Vienna branch of the Foundation. Our slogan will be "EQUAL RIGHTS AND FREEDOM FOR ARCANISTS" ... How American is that?

小贩咂了咂嘴，但神情依然振奋。\
The peddler feigns a smile, yet his expression remains spirited.

**小贩Ⅰ**：可他似乎是个很有头脸的人物，口袋里有大把的克朗，认识当局不少要员！\
**Vendor I**: He seems to be quite a big shot with wads of cash in his pocket and reliable connections in the government!

**小贩Ⅰ**：他说，只要干了这一票，我们就再也不用担心居留证和神秘术许可证的事了……！\
**Vendor I**: He said we no longer have to worry about the residence permit and the arcanum license after this job!

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：再也不用担心……\
**Kakania**: No longer ...

卡卡尼亚恍惚地咀嚼着这个词，但沉浸在希冀中的对方并未注意到。\
Kakania chews on the words absentmindedly, but the hopeful figure immersed does not seem to notice.

**小贩Ⅰ**：医生，你不和我们一起来吗？你不是最热衷这类活动了吗？\
**Vendor I**: Aren't you coming with us, miss? This kind of activity is your favorite, isn't it?

**小贩Ⅰ**：……嘿，医生，你要去哪？\
**Vendor I**: ... Hey, where are you going?

是啊，你要去哪？\
Right. Where are you headed?

——“卡卡尼亚医生，这不是你最热衷的吗？”\
"Doctor Kakania, isn't this exactly what you've always been so passionate about?"

——“医生，这不是您所叮嘱的吗？”\
"Doctor, isn't this exactly what you've espoused, just put in practice?"

没由来的，她想起那首诗。\
Out of nowhere, she recalls the words of that poem.

——“我去林间寻觅，西勒诺斯。”\
"Seeking Silenus in the woods, I asked him."

一道尖锐的诘问，自颅骨深处响起。\
A sharp question shoots up out of her skull.

**？？？**：——卡卡尼亚，你应受审判！\
**???**: Kakania, you should be tried and punished!

**卡卡尼亚**：为什么？\
**Kakania**: Why?

**？？？**：你曾予以你的朋友希望，嘱咐以药方，发誓与他们站在一起。但是现在，你沉默，你转身——这是一种背弃。\
**???**: You gave your friends hope, prescribed them treatment, and vowed to stand by their side. But now you're silent and turning away. This is a betrayal!

**？？？**：你背弃你的病人，你逃离你的同胞。你枉为医生，枉为一个人！\
**???**: You betrayed your patient, you ran away from your kind. You are unfit to be a psychiatrist, you're not worthy to be a human being!

**卡卡尼亚**：那我又要怎么做？！\
**Kakania**: What am I supposed to do then?!

**卡卡尼亚**：我的病人，我从未料想过她的真实心境。我的同胞，他们都是一无所知的人，被手握筹码者恶意地煽动。\
**Kakania**: My patient, I never figured out her true thoughts and feelings. And my fellow kinfolk, they were innocent and unaware of the manipulations of the influential.

**卡卡尼亚**：而我自己，也尚且处于迷雾之中。我不曾拥有的真相，要如何给予他们？！\
**Kakania**: Even I was in confusion. How could I tell them the truth that I didn't know?

**卡卡尼亚**：——仅仅凭我，又该如何面对这些压倒性的疯狂和毁灭？\
**Kakania**: How am I supposed to face the overwhelming madness and destruction on my own?!

**？？？**：所以你只是一个恰好知道真相的人，一个恰好站在岸上的人！\
**???**: So, you're just someone who happens to stumble upon the truth, a bystander who happens to be watching from the shore!

**？？？**：这便是属于你的耻辱。\
**???**: This is why you are a disgrace.

**？？？**：倘若你只是在一边看着，那就是犯罪；假如你给以承诺，却没有能力带他们上岸，你也是在犯罪；假如你狠心无视这一切，抽身离去，那更是最大的罪！\
**???**: It's a sin to just stand by and watch; it's a sin to promise salvation but fail to bring them ashore; it's an even greater sin to ignore this tragedy and turn away!

**卡卡尼亚**：……是的，我承认。\
**Kakania**: ... Yes. I admit.

**卡卡尼亚**：我承认，我是一个伪善的人。\
**Kakania**: I'm a hypocrite.

**卡卡尼亚**：我曾那么渴望帮助同伴，他们真的需要我帮助时，我却背过身去，畏葸不前。\
**Kakania**: I used to be so eager to help my friends, but when they really needed me, I turned my back on them.

**卡卡尼亚**：我告诉她要释放内心的压抑——可当她真的做到时，我却承受不住它毁灭性的后果。\
**Kakania**: I told her to release her repressions, but when she actually did, I couldn't face the destructive consequences.

**卡卡尼亚**：我那么热情地宣扬我的梦想——渴望所有同胞都能迎来自由的朝阳，可它以这种方式到来时，却成了世界上最为可怖的噩梦！\
**Kakania**: I propagated my dream with great enthusiasm, hoping all my kith could live in a free world. But if it's realized in this way, it's the worst nightmare imaginable for everyone!

**卡卡尼亚**：我说要创建神秘学家的分离派，可这究竟是新生，还是一种彻头彻尾的背叛？\
**Kakania**: I said I would start the secession of the arcanists, but what is the essence of this movement? A rebirth, or a complete betrayal?

**卡卡尼亚**：就像我的父亲、母亲、哥哥，一旦完成了阶级跨越，便致力于和“贩卖小商品的神秘学家”划清关系……\
**Kakania**: I'm just like my father, mother, and brother, who tried to shed the label of "arcanists selling small wares" as soon as they climbed up the social ladder.

**卡卡尼亚**：我不明白。因此我恳求您，请您告诉我……我究竟该怎么办？\
**Kakania**: I'm lost. So please, tell me ... What should I do?

她得到了一声冷笑。\
The reply is a cold laugh.

**？？？**：你不是已经知道了吗？\
**???**: You already know, don't you?

**？？？**：——“雨幕之下，谁将泯没。”\
**???**: "Who shall vanish in the rain?"

**？？？**：——“又有谁会获得那永恒的幸福，无上的恩赐——”\
**???**: "Who shall be granted the eternal happiness, the grace from above—"

**？？？**：——“那不复存在的虚无？”\
**???**: "And that emptiness, the cessation of existence?"

恍惚间，她站在环城大道之中，任由混乱和躁动从身旁经过。\
In a daze, she stands in the middle of the Ring Road, letting the chaos pass by around her.

一道爆炸导致的碎石朝她飞来，但她浑然不觉。\
A stone debris from another explosion flies toward her, but her stance remains unchanged, as if oblivious or welcoming of it.

**马库斯**：——卡卡尼亚小姐！\
**Marcus**: Ms. Kakania!

特效-神秘术的闪光

碎石忽地改变了落下的弧度。\
The stone suddenly changes its trajectory.

身体被拽开了，那个急切摇晃自己的身影十分熟悉。\
Her body is pulled away. The figure shaking her is a familiar face.

**马库斯**：太好了，您没有事——我一直、一直在找您。\
**Marcus**: You are fine. Thank goodness! I've been trying so hard to find you.

**马库斯**：我有非常重要的事要告诉您。\
**Marcus**: I have something important to tell you.

年轻的助手紧紧抓着医生的衣袖。\
The young assistant clutches the doctor's sleeve tightly.

**马库斯**：这个世界即将面临一场颠覆性的危机。\
**Marcus**: A catastrophe is about to sweep across the globe.

**马库斯**：而如果我们顺利……也许还能救下许多人。\
**Marcus**: But there are still things we can do. If it goes smoothly ... perhaps we can save plenty of lives.

## 6TH-17 艺术至上 / Art Above All

**霍夫曼**：……委外合约小队将无法参与这次行动，他们有更紧急的任务。\
**Hofmann**: ... The Field Agent Squad cannot make it this time. They have a more urgent mission.

**霍夫曼**：不过，虽然我们没有透露太多内幕，但维也纳分部对之前明目张胆的破坏极度恼火，已经申请了军队出面。\
**Hofmann**: But the Vienna Branch already requested support from the army, even though we haven't told them what is happening. They are irritated by the blatant attack.

**霍夫曼**：眼下最好是借助“时代”的力量。\
**Hofmann**: We'd better use the power of the "era" now.

霍夫曼把拉普拉斯配发的通讯器别回腰间。\
Hofmann clips a Laplace-issued communicator back on her waist.

**霍夫曼**：唯一的问题是……我们的情报来源准确吗，马库斯？\
**Hofmann**: Only one question remains. Is the source of this intel reliable, Marcus?

**霍夫曼**：伊索尔德和海因里希，真的还会来参加《托斯卡》的首演？\
**Hofmann**: Are Isolde and Heinrich really playing in the premiere of Tosca?

她对着助手提问，目光却直直指向了呆坐在一旁的卡卡尼亚。\
She questions her assistant, but her gaze is fixed on Kakania, who sits there idle in thought and action.

**马库斯**：是的，虽然这听起来有些不合常理，但我想卡卡尼亚小姐的推论是……\
**Marcus**: Yes. It may sound a bit absurd, but that is Ms. Kakania's inference ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……是你们来找我合作的。我也尽了自己的力，说出了我知道的、推断的一切。\
**Kakania**: ... It is you who asked for cooperation. I've done what I can and told you everything I know.

她垂着头，声音空前的低落。\
She hangs her head, her voice uncharacteristically dispirited.

**卡卡尼亚**：只要《托斯卡》的演出没有被取消，伊索尔德就一定会来。她对自己的作品有强迫症般的完美心态。\
**Kakania**: Unless the show is canceled, Isolde will show up. She is a perfectionist when it comes to her work.

**卡卡尼亚**：她来了，海因里希也一定会来。\
**Kakania**: If she shows up, so will Heinrich.

**卡卡尼亚**：您也知道，他们二人都没有受到通缉。贵族阶层里有很多人热爱伊索尔德的歌剧，保障一场演出对他们来说不是难事。\
**Kakania**: Neither of them is under bounty. And the upper class loves her performance, so it's not hard for them to guarantee a show even in these troubled times.

**卡卡尼亚**：她会来的，以我对她的了解……\
**Kakania**: I know her well. She will be there ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……如果我真的了解她的话。\
**Kakania**: ... If I know her as well as I think I do.

卡卡尼亚不再言语，只是出神地望着那道幕布。\
Kakania says nothing more, and her eyes fix on a curtain, locking into a trance.

歌剧即将开演。观众们陆陆续续地穿过走道，在软椅上就座。\
The opera is about to begin. The audience pass through the aisles and take their seats on the soft chairs.

**马库斯**：……霍夫曼女士，委外合约小队遭遇了什么状况？\
**Marcus**: ... Madam Hofmann, what mission is the Field Agent Squad dealing with?

马库斯开口，缓解了这片刻的尴尬。\
Marcus speaks up, trying, in the manner of her books on conversation, to ease the momentary awkwardness.

**霍夫曼**：最近三天，帝国境内的刺杀案件突然高发，他们在维护重要人物的安全。\
**Hofmann**: Assassinations. There's been an outbreak in the Empire over the past three days. They are sent to guard the important people.

**霍夫曼**：……在人手如此紧急的情况下，指望支援是不现实的。\
**Hofmann**: We're out of manpower right now, so don't expect any backup.

**霍夫曼**：但我们也不需要击溃或者俘获重塑之手，只需设法追查他们的术式。\
**Hofmann**: But don't worry. We don't need to capture or defeat the Manus. Just focus on the original ritual.

**霍夫曼**：凡事以保全自己为优先。明白了吗，马库斯？\
**Hofmann**: Put your own safety first. Understand, Marcus?

马库斯点了点头。她再一次“阅读”起人民歌剧院内部来。\
Marcus signals her understanding. Once again, she dives into her "read" on the interior of the Vienna People's Opera.

**马库斯**：嗯……？观众似乎来得比售票人次多。\
**Marcus**: Hmm? The audience is bigger than the tickets sold.

**马库斯**：算上售空的包厢和楼座的票，正厅的人也有点太多了……是维也纳分部安插的人吗？\
**Marcus**: I counted the seats in the balcony and gallery. There are still too many people in the main hall. Are they all staff of the Vienna branch?

**霍夫曼**：不，也有可能是重塑之手的伪装。\
**Hofmann**: No. This could be the doing of Manus Vindictae.

**卡卡尼亚**：——哈哈。\
**Kakania**: Haha.

**霍夫曼**：……您在笑什么？\
**Hofmann**: What are you laughing at?

**卡卡尼亚**：笑您似乎一点都不明白这儿的状况，政府女士。这里是维也纳，音乐之都！\
**Kakania**: At you, Ms. Foundation. You have no idea where you are. This is Vienna, the city of music!

**卡卡尼亚**：——而这是伊索尔德和《托斯卡》，人们为这出戏发疯！\
**Kakania**: And this is Isolde and Tosca! People are crazy about them!

**卡卡尼亚**：我敢打赌要是他们卖站票，那每层楼的外面都会挂满了人……\
**Kakania**: I bet they would even stand outside the railings if standing tickets were sold ...

**卡卡尼亚**：而到了第三幕，他们就会和托斯卡一样从城墙上一跃而下，嘴里高喊：“上帝面前见吧！”\
**Kakania**: And when it reaches act three, they would fling themselves over the edge, crying "O Scarpia, avanti a Dio!"

霍夫曼女士警惕地皱起了眉头。\
Hofmann's brow hangs heavy with vigilance.

**霍夫曼**：我不懂您在说什么，但这听起来比重塑之手更糟糕。\
**Hofmann**: I don't get what you're saying, but it sounds even worse than Manus Vindictae.

**马库斯**：我，我提前搜集了这出戏剧的资料……\
**Marcus**: I-I collected information about this opera ...

马库斯将一叠纸质资料递到导师的手里。\
Marcus hands off another stack of material to her mentor.

**霍夫曼**：“……1800年的罗马，画家卡瓦拉多西和歌剧演员托斯卡是一对恋人……”\
**Hofmann**: "Rome, 1800. Painter Mario Cavaradossi and singer Tosca are two lovers ..."

**霍夫曼**：“卡瓦拉多西因为庇佑越狱的革命党人安杰罗提被羁押。”\
**Hofmann**: "Cavaradossi has been arrested for helping the fugitive Cesare Angelotti, former consul to the Roman Republic."

**霍夫曼**：“托斯卡为了拯救恋人，找到警察局长斯卡比亚，希望获得宽大处理。”\
**Hofmann**: "To save her lover, Tosca turns to Scarpia, the Chief of Police."

**霍夫曼**：“斯卡比亚垂涎她的美貌已久。于是便要求她出卖自己的身体，以换取卡瓦拉多西的生命和自由。”\
**Hofmann**: "Scarpia has coveted Tosca for a long time, so he proposes that Cavaradossi will be freed if Tosca gives herself to him."

**霍夫曼**：“托斯卡屈服了，但在警察局长准备拥抱她时，她拿起桌子上的一把匕首，猛然刺进了斯卡比亚的心脏……”\
**Hofmann**: "Tosca submits to him, but when he tries to embrace her, Tosca stabs him in the heart with a dagger ..."

**卡卡尼亚**：——上天啊！您怎么能把这出戏念得这么无趣？！\
**Kakania**: For heaven's sake! How did you make that sound so boring?!

卡卡尼亚忍无可忍地站了起来。\
Kakania stands up, unable to bear the indignity any longer.

她伸出手，一把夺过了那叠资料。\
She reaches out, snatching the stack.

**卡卡尼亚**：要我说，您根本就不需要事先阅读剧本，这把什么惊喜都毁了。\
**Kakania**: I don't think you should read the script ahead of time. It takes away all the surprises.

**卡卡尼亚**：您只需要跟随演员的指引，沉浸到那个世界里……\
**Kakania**: Just let the singer guide you and immerse yourself in this world ...

**卡卡尼亚**：而伊索尔德在这一点上是最好的演员。她是最棒的！\
**Kakania**: Isolde is very good in guiding the audience. She's the best there is!

卡卡尼亚用力握着剧本，极力为自己所喜爱的剧目辩护。\
Kakania grips the script tightly, ready and willing to defend her beloved play.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德是一个降灵者。她那不可思议的神秘术，让她在舞台上就像是角色本人降临一样。\
**Kakania**: As a seancer, her incredible arcane skills allow her to act like the characters themselves on stage.

**卡卡尼亚**：她能模仿各种各样的歌喉，发出不属于她的声音……完全地成为另一个人，带我们步入那超现实的世界。\
**Kakania**: She can do all kinds of voices, even those that seem physically impossible ... When she does this, she becomes a completely different person, taking us to a world beyond reality.

**卡卡尼亚**：那感觉就像是在圣堂目睹奇迹。\
**Kakania**: It'll feel like witnessing a miracle firsthand.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

她也意识到自己有些不合时宜了。\
She realizes her behavior is, for the moment, quite grossly inappropriate.

卡卡尼亚重新坐回椅子上。她缓缓地摘下眼镜，将它拿在手里。\
Kakania slinks back down and removes her glasses, holding them in her hand.

**卡卡尼亚**：……抱歉，我只是，有些激动。\
**Kakania**: ... Sorry. I got a little excited.

**卡卡尼亚**：我曾经是这样期待这场歌剧……\
**Kakania**: So this is how much I looked forward to this opera ...

她颤抖地扶住额头，声音近乎抽噎。\
She trembles as her hands reach up to grasp her forehead, her voice falling into a sob.

马库斯犹豫了一会，还是伸出手，搭上了她的肩膀。\
Marcus hesitates, but eventually reaches out, placing a hand on her shoulder.

**马库斯**：……对不起。我知道，您仍然把她视作朋友。\
**Marcus**: I'm sorry. I know you still see her as a friend.

**卡卡尼亚**：不，我只是在想……\
**Kakania**: No. I'm just thinking ...

**卡卡尼亚**：我以为我了解我的朋友，了解我的同胞，但即使我有这些心理学知识，有神秘术——有这些镜子……我仍然对人们内心的真相一无所知。\
**Kakania**: I thought I knew my friends and my kin, but really I had no idea what they were truly thinking, even with this mirror and all the psychological theories.

**卡卡尼亚**：我就像一个打开潘多拉盒子的人，不知道里面潜藏的是毁灭还是希望……\
**Kakania**: I am like Pandora who opened the box without knowing what was inside. Was it hope, or destruction?

**马库斯**：这听起来……很幽微。\
**Marcus**: That sounds ... dark ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……但是，我想。\
**Kakania**: But I also think ...

**卡卡尼亚**：也许我们永远无法真正理解另一个人。可如果因此而放弃，事情也不会变得更好。\
**Kakania**: ... Perhaps we can never truly understand one another, but things won't get any better if I give up because of it.

卡卡尼亚摇了摇头。她用力地擦了一下眼眶，戴上了眼镜。\
Kakania shakes her head, rubs her eyes forcefully, then puts on her glasses once more.

**卡卡尼亚**：从未降生的空白——那之中无路可寻。\
**Kakania**: I can not turn my back on this.

**卡卡尼亚**：马库斯小姐，您不用为我担心，我既然来到了这里，就一定会履行我的诺言。\
**Kakania**: Don't worry about me, Ms. Marcus. Now that I'm here, I will fulfill my promise.

**卡卡尼亚**：我一定会阻止她的。\
**Kakania**: I will stop her.

**卡卡尼亚**：至于你们所说的末日……说实话，我不知道怎么应对。\
**Kakania**: As for the doomsday you talked about ... I don't know what I can do about it, to be honest.

**卡卡尼亚**：我只知道，如果我今天没能阻止她，此后我活着的每一天都会像世界末日。\
**Kakania**: All I know is, if I don't stop her today, every day of my life will feel like doomsday.

**卡卡尼亚**：……无论如何，演出要开始了。\
**Kakania**: No matter what happens from here, the show has begun.

灯光变暗了。\
The lights dim.

正如她所说的那样。\
Just as she had scripted it.

黑发的歌剧演员登上台前。\
The black-haired opera singer steps to the front of the stage.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**马库斯**：——！\
**Marcus**: —!

**卡卡尼亚**：……请欣赏吧。\
**Kakania**: Please, enjoy.

**卡卡尼亚**：即使明天就是世界末日，我们也还有一场歌剧。\
**Kakania**: Even if the world ends tomorrow, we still have a show to enjoy.

**马库斯**：但她究竟是从哪里登台的？后台并没有人见过她……！\
**Marcus**: But how did she get on stage? No one saw her backstage!
