**Hofmann**: A secret passage, like at the exhibition.

**霍夫曼**：马库斯，你在看台上看着伊索尔德，我去找海因里希。她一从台上下来，基金会分部的人就会动手。\

**Hofmann**: I'll talk to you on the intercom.

霍夫曼女士起身离开座位。\
Hofmann rises from her seat.

旁边的听众不满地对她报以注视。\
The surrounding audience look at her disapprovingly.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

马库斯全神贯注地凝视舞台。\
Marcus stares intently at the stage.

光束亮起，投射在这舞台唯一的主角身上。\
The spotlight shines, casting its beam on the stage's sole protagonist.

她是整个维也纳独一无二的夜莺。\
Vienna's unparalleled nightingale.

而马库斯无心欣赏那些优美的歌曲，只是计算着戏剧的进度。\
But Marcus has no interest in her beautiful songs—she is only calculating the progress of the unseen drama.

第一幕结束

gundongzimu_2#0.1#49

**马库斯**：现在是第二幕，托斯卡被警察局长斯卡比亚逼迫。\
**Marcus**: This is the second act. Scarpia, the chief of police, will propose a bargain.

**马库斯**：她假意答应，要求斯卡比亚给她和恋人签发两张便于逃亡的通行证。\
**Marcus**: Tosca will pretend to submit, and request safe-conduct for her and Cavaradossi.

**马库斯**：而当斯卡比亚低头签字时……\
**Marcus**: When Scarpia signs the paper ...

全神贯注的状态使得视野无限缩小。马库斯甚至能感受到演员歌唱时微微颤动的发梢。\
Her focused state narrows her vision. Marcus can even feel the slight tremble of the star's hair as she sings.

**马库斯**：……呼……\
**Marcus**: *deep breath*

托斯卡俯首在雕像足下，酝酿着一场复仇。\
Tosca bows before the statue, brewing her revenge.

**斯卡比亚**：走哪条路？\
**Scarpia**: And which road do you choose?

**马库斯**：“——最近的路。奇维塔韦基亚港。”\
**Marcus**: "The shortest one! Civitavecchia."

小小的纸张自托斯卡的指尖被抽回。\
A small piece of paper is retracted from Tosca's fingertips.

**马库斯**：……还差一点，还差一点。\
**Marcus**: ... Almost there, almost there.

托斯卡托起桌上的红色丝绸。\
Tosca lifts the red silk from the table.

——而后拿起匕首，刺入了警察局长的心脏。\
She picks up the dagger, plunging it into the heart of the police chief.

面对躺在血泊中的男人，她大笑着——\
Facing the man lying in a pool of blood, she laughs aloud and maniacally.

**伊索尔德**：——这就是托斯卡之吻！\
**Isolde**: This is Tosca's kiss!

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**“斯卡比亚”**：——啊！\
**“Scarpia”**: Ah!

**马库斯**：等一下，有一点不对。\
**Marcus**: Wait. Something's wrong.

**伊索尔德**：被自己的血呛住了吧……！\
**Isolde**: Are you choking on your blood?

**马库斯**：这个倒在地上的男人……\
**Marcus**: The man lying on the ground ...

**马库斯**：是分部的卡尔先生？！\
**Marcus**: That's Mr. Karl, from the branch?!

**马库斯**：他……真的在流血？！\
**Marcus**: Is he really ... bleeding?!

马库斯猛地从看台上站起。\
Marcus shoots up from the gallery.

“阅读”透露的信息令望远镜从她手中滑落。\
The information her "reading" reveals causes the telescope to slip from her hands.

**卡卡尼亚**：——什么？你没有看错吗？！\
**Kakania**: What? Are you sure?!

**马库斯**：绝没有，卡卡尼亚小姐！这不是演戏，这是血！卡尔先生的血！！\
**Marcus**: Definitely, Ms. Kakania! He's not acting. That's real blood! Coming out of Mr. Karl's body!

**马库斯**：舞台上的刺杀变成了真实的刺杀……！为什么演出还在继续？！\
**Marcus**: The assassination in the story has become reality! Why is the show still on?!

**马库斯**：为什么……为什么观众没有反应？！基金会分部的成员呢？\
**Marcus**: Why ... Why isn't the audience reacting?! What about the branch staff?

**马库斯**：霍夫曼女士！您能听到我吗？！\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann! Can you hear me?!

无人理睬她的呐喊。人们依然全神贯注，保持肃静。\
Her cries go unheard. The audience remains attentive and silent.

通讯器那边也没有声音。\
There is no sound from the communicator.

**卡卡尼亚**：——该死的，怎么会这样！！\
**Kakania**: D**n it. What is going on?!

卡卡尼亚飞快地冲下座位。\
Kakania rushes down from her seat.

她奔跑着穿过面色如常的观众们，径直冲到台前。\
She runs through the audience, whose expressions remain unchanged, with heads locked straight to the front of the stage.

**卡卡尼亚**：真的是……卡尔先生……\
**Kakania**: It really is ... Mr. Karl ...

卡尔身下的血泊缓缓扩散着，在微冷的空气中蒸腾着热气。\
The pool of blood beneath Karl slowly spreads, steaming in the cool air.

**卡卡尼亚**：为什么，为什么没有人……\
**Kakania**: Why? Why is no one ...

**卡卡尼亚**：你们疯了吗？！难道都没有发现有人死了吗？！演出暂停！！！\
**Kakania**: Are you all mad?! A man has been killed, don't you see?! Stop the show!!

观众安然地坐着。\
The audience sits calmly and unfazed.

奏乐也尚在继续。\
The music continues.

舞台上，饰演托斯卡的伊索尔德转过身来，露出欣然的神色。\
On the stage, Isolde, playing Tosca, turns around, revealing a pleased expression.

**伊索尔德**：卡瓦拉多西，您逃出来了吗？\
**Isolde**: Cavaradossi, have you escaped from jail?

**卡卡尼亚**：什、什么……？\
**Kakania**: W-What?

**伊索尔德**：我可怜的恋人，您只是过于好心，却背负上了政治犯的重罪。我一直想洗刷您的污名。\
**Isolde**: My poor lover, you were put into jail only because you were too kindhearted. I've been trying to clear your name.

**伊索尔德**：斯卡比亚威胁我，要我当了他的情妇，与他做恶毒的交易。\
**Isolde**: Scarpia proposed an unfair deal. He wanted me as his mistress.

**伊索尔德**：——而如今，这个男人终于死了！过去整个罗马曾在他脚下颤栗不安。\
**Isolde**: But now he is dead, at last! The whole of Rome was overshadowed by his power.

**卡卡尼亚**：你，你在说什么啊，伊索尔德……？这不是《托斯卡》里的情节……\
**Kakania**: W-What are you talking about, Isolde? That's not what the story is like ...

**伊索尔德**：和我一同逃离这里吧！卡瓦拉多西。我拿到了通行证。\
**Isolde**: Run away with me, Cavaradossi! I have the safe conduct.

**伊索尔德**：去一个没有人认识我们的……神圣的、幸福的自由王国！\
**Isolde**: We will go to the sacred kingdom of happiness and freedom ... where no one knows us!

视频2-暴雨开始 没有没有

**马库斯**：……这，这是什么……\
**Marcus**: What, what are these ...

**马库斯**：“波蒂奥拉卡中毒身亡”……“弗拉斯尼克被枪杀”……还……还有！“赫岑霍夫遇刺”……“希腊国王遇刺”……“弗朗茨大公遇刺”——\
**Marcus**: "Ausker Botiorak poisoned to death." ... "Frasnik shot dead." ... And ... "Hötzenhof assassinated."... "King of Greece assassinated." ... "Archduke Franz assassinated."

**马库斯**：这么多刺杀新闻……在同一天，同一刻……？\
**Marcus**: All these assassinations ... at the same time?

一开始，只是几声零星的躁动。\
Applause comes from the main hall, from the balconies, from beneath the dome, from beyond the unreachable sky, all converging into an unstoppable frenzy of sound.

掌声自正厅里，自楼座上，自穹顶之下，自不可凝望的天空彼端袭来，汇成这不可阻挡的狂乱之声。\
It rings through the hall like a torrential downpour.

如同一场暴雨。

**通讯器**：“——”\
**Communicator**: ...

**霍夫曼**：马——库斯，计划有变。\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, change of plan.

**霍夫曼**：出现——了一级紧急事态。立刻——从那里撤离。\
**Hofmann**: We have a code red. Evacuate immediately.

## 6TH-19 浪潮的重逢 / The Clashing Tides

**马库斯**：他们……他们的面孔正在变形，像那些油画一样……\
**Marcus**: Their faces are distorting ... like those paintings ...

**马库斯**：这也是某种群体癔症吗，还是……？\
**Marcus**: Is this also some kind of mass hysteria, or ...?

歌剧院空前喧嚣，人们正在躁动。\
The opera house is bizarrely noisy, and the people within are restless.

**楼座观众**：谁看到我的望远镜了吗？把它递给我一下好吗？\
**Balcony Audience**: Anyone seen my glasses? Could you pass them to me?

**楼座观众**：噢，原来它长在我的眼睛上……没事了……\
**Balcony Audience**: Oh, they've grown on my eyes. Don't mind me ...

欢呼的人群站在了椅子上，他们不能自已地鼓掌，嘴里发出狂热的咆哮。\
The cheering crowd stands on their chairs, clapping uncontrollably, shouting with maddened fervor.

**后座观众**：——这就是托斯卡之吻！\
**Back Audience**: This is Tosca's kiss!

**后座观众**：来吧！朋友们，同胞们！握紧你们的匕首，到上面去！我们也要拥有属于自己的斯卡比亚！\
**Back Audience**: Come, friends, kith and kin! Take your daggers and get up there! We will all kill our own Scarpia!

**后座观众**：那些徒有其表的上层阶级，根本就配不上那么好的座位！\
**Back Audience**: Those so-called upper class people don't deserve the best seats!

**后座观众**：Vissi d'arte, vissi d'amore!\
**Back Audience**: Vissi d'arte, vissi d'amore!

越来越多的人离开了座位，有人高呼着从他人的膝盖上踩了过去。\
More and more people leave their seats, some shouting as they step up and over to lean over railings and into the aisles.

而奏乐仍在继续，大幕也仍未落下。\
The music still plays, and the curtain has yet to fall.

**包厢观众**：太精彩了，我几乎能感到血液溅到我的脸上……！\
**Guest in Box**: Splendid! I can almost feel the blood splashing on my face!

**包厢观众**：这无疑是一种艺术，一种用真实取代虚假的动人愿望……我从未看过如此精彩的演出……\
**Guest in Box**: There is no doubt this is art! The way in which reality replaces fantasy ... I've never seen a show like this before ...

**包厢观众**：哦！西拉，奥尔夫，你们怎么了？血也溅到你们脸上了吗？这是演出的一部分吗，还是？\
**Guest in Box**: Selah, Orff, what happened? Have you got blood on your faces, too? Is this part of the show, or ...?

**包厢观众**：——唔哦！\
**Guest in Box**: Woww!

人群混成了一团黏稠的油彩，如同海浪般汹涌冲刷着歌剧院的每一个角落。\
The crowd blends like a thick oil paint, surging and washing over every corner of the opera house.

**马库斯**：他们在狂热地互相杀戮……！就没有人注意到这一切吗……？\
**Marcus**: They're killing each other in a frenzy! Is no one noticing this?

**马库斯**：霍夫曼女士，我这里的情况很紧急，我——\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann, I have an emergency here. I ...

马库斯一个趔趄，险些被疯狂的人群撞倒，通讯器的联络也因此中断。\
Marcus stumbles, knocked over by the frenzied crowd, and the connection to her communicator is lost.

**马库斯**：不行，什么都听不见！\
**Marcus**: No, I can't hear anything!

**马库斯**：人们源源不绝……我得开出一条路！\
**Marcus**: The crowd won't let me leave ... I need to make way myself!

有人从阴暗处冲了出来，拔出腰上的佩枪。\
Someone rushes out from the shadows, drawing a sidearm.

**军人**：安静，都安静！！\
**Soldier**: Quiet, be quiet!

**军人**：你们这些暴乱分子，都见上帝去吧！\
**Soldier**: Go to hell, you terrorists!

原定的维护秩序之人只让现场变得更加混乱。\
If their arrival had meant to bring order, it succeeded only in making the scene that much more chaotic.

枪声、尖叫声、嘶吼声、咆哮声混杂一团。\
Gunshots, screams, roars, and bellows meld together.

有少数的基金会分部的职员穿梭其中，但他们要么也被癔症沾染，要么被人潮的洪流冲走。\
A few staff members from the Foundation branch weave through the crowd, but they are either infected with hysteria or swept away in the flood of people.

马库斯狼狈地在其中闪躲，像洪水中的一片落叶。\
Marcus dodges awkwardly among them, like a leaf in a rushing river.

**马库斯**：我得，我得疏散他们，至少把散场通道的门打开——\
**Marcus**: I need to ... I need to disperse them. At least open up the exit ...

**马库斯**：——呃！\
**Marcus**: Ugh!

**霍夫曼**：马库斯！你还在做什么？！命令是撤退！！\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, what are you doing?! I said evacuate!!

导师匆匆地从帷幕另一端走来，将马库斯从蜂拥的人潮中拉走。\
Hofmann hurries from the other side of the curtain, pulling Marcus away from the swarming crowd.

**马库斯**：可是人们正在死去——！我们的职责是——\
**Marcus**: But people are dying! It is our duty to ...

**霍夫曼**：……基金会总部刚刚传来了通讯。\
**Hofmann**: I just got a message from the headquarters.

**霍夫曼**：司辰发布了24小时倒计时通知。\
**Hofmann**: The Timekeeper has issued a twenty-four hour "Storm" warning.

**马库斯**：……什么？\
**Marcus**: ... What?

**霍夫曼**：重塑在同一天发动了多起刺杀案，时代的不稳定性抵达了临界点。\
**Hofmann**: The Manus has carried out several assassinations on the same day. The instability of this era has reached the Critical Point.

**霍夫曼**：——“暴雨”就要发生了。\
**Hofmann**: ... Which means the "Storm" is coming.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

马库斯颓然地倒地。\
Marcus collapses to the ground.

她缓缓地、不可置信地用手抓散了自己的头发。\
Slowly, bewilderedly, she begins raking her hands through her hair.

**马库斯**：不，不……怎么会……导致“暴雨”……\
**Marcus**: N-no ... No way ... The "Storm" ...

**马库斯**：是我……都是因为我……\
**Marcus**: It was me ... It was me ...

**马库斯**：这一切连锁反应的起源是我……是我把那座岛的消息透露了出去……是我……！\
**Marcus**: It was me who started the chain reaction ... It was me who leaked out the details of the island ... It was me!

**霍夫曼**：——不要步入幽微，马库斯！\
**Hofmann**: Get a hold of yourself, Marcus!

一双有力的手把她从地上拉了起来。\
A pair of strong hands pull her up from the ground.

**霍夫曼**：在这场混沌无比的时间风暴中，你我都只是无足轻重的一粒石子。\
**Hofmann**: This is the "Storm" of time. Compared to the chaos it causes, you and I mean nothing more than a pebble.

**霍夫曼**：在你之前，“暴雨”已经发生了数次。在你之后，“暴雨”还将发生无数次。\
**Hofmann**: It happened many times before you did anything, and it will happen countless times more.

**霍夫曼**：时代反复消失，人们反复死去，没有哪一次比哪一次更糟。\
**Hofmann**: The eras in history will disappear again and again, and so will the people. The situation can't get any worse.

**霍夫曼**：我们唯一能做的，就是找到免疫“暴雨”的术式。这样才能救下更多的人！\
**Hofmann**: The only thing we can do now is to find the ritual that grants immunity to the "Storm." It's the only way to save more lives!

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**霍夫曼**：基金会已经发布了避难通知，所有外派人员，必须在“暴雨”前回到总部。\
**Hofmann**: The Foundation has issued the evacuation notice. All staff must return to the headquarters before the "Storm" arrives.

**霍夫曼**：离我们最近的撤退点是维也纳火车站，时间是，两小时后。\
**Hofmann**: The closest evacuation point is Vienna Central Station. They'll pick us up there in two hours.

**马库斯**：——两小时？\
**Marcus**: Two hours?

马库斯飞快地回忆起了来时见过的地图。\
Marcus recalls the map she saw on her way with picture clarity.

**马库斯**：我们从这里过去要不了——\
**Marcus**: It takes less than two hours to get ...

**霍夫曼**：……是的，在“暴雨”真正落下前的这一段时间里，我们还有一些能做的事。\
**Hofmann**: I know. There are still things we can do, before the "Storm" truly arrives.

**霍夫曼**：但敌人的实力可能远超我们，我们也无法再取得任何支持。\
**Hofmann**: But the enemies are probably much stronger than we are, and there will be no backup for us.

不远处，维也纳分部的原负责人正惊恐地躺着，作为一桩罪行的证明。\
Not far away, the head of the Vienna branch lies slain, his face wrenched in horror, a testament to a crime.

舞台之下，穿华服的人，穿制服的人，穿戏服的人，他们咆哮着，涌动着，已经难分彼此。\
Below the stage, people in fancy dress, in uniform, in costume, roar and surge about, forming an indistinguishable mass.

**马库斯**：……您曾对我说过，您不害怕死，您害怕的是一无所知地死去。\
**Marcus**: You once told me what really scared you was not the threat to your life, but the possibility of dying ignorant.

**马库斯**：我现在……也许能明白一些这种心情了。\
**Marcus**: I think ... I understand what you mean now.

**马库斯**：我也不想这样……我不想这样什么都没做到地回到基金会！\
**Marcus**: I don't want that either ... I don't want to go back to the headquarters without doing anything at all!

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

**霍夫曼**：很好，走吧，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: Well said, Marcus. Let's go.

**霍夫曼**：去找海因里希和伊索尔德，可能得知术式的人，我们的重要线索。\
**Hofmann**: Find Heinrich and Isolde. They might know the ritual, or have the clues we need.

**霍夫曼**：顺利的话，我们还来得及赶上最后一趟班车。\
**Hofmann**: We can still catch the last train if everything goes smoothly.

霍夫曼熟练地给子弹上膛，马库斯也握紧了自己的提灯。\
Hofmann expertly loads her weapon again, and Marcus grips her lamp tightly.

**霍夫曼**：——卡卡尼亚没有和你在一起吗？\
**Hofmann**: Kakania is not with you?

**马库斯**：唔，卡卡尼亚小姐当时冲到了台上，她和伊索尔德——\
**Marcus**: Mmm, Ms. Kakania ran up to the stage. She and Isolde ...

越过人们耸动的肩膀，台上已经没有绿色的身影。\
Beyond the shoulders of the crowd, the green figure has disappeared from the stage.

马库斯眯起眼睛，仔细检查帷幔和舞台道具。\
Marcus squints, inspecting the curtains and stage props.

**马库斯**：海因里希给它们全都附上了神秘术，这些布景道具里一定有通往暗室的机关。\
**Marcus**: Heinrich has enchanted all the props. There must be a hidden entrance to the secret chamber.

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚和伊索尔德……她们一定还在这座歌剧院里!\
**Marcus**: I am sure ... Ms. Kakania and Isolde are still in this theater!

**霍夫曼**：——过来！\
**Hofmann**: Come here!

深紫色的咒文辉光破空而来。\
The deep purple glow of an incantation radiates from the darkness.

霍夫曼及时将马库斯的肩膀向后一扳，这道咒语仅是灼伤了她的头发。\
Hofmann pulls Marcus back by the shoulder. The incantation flies past her hair, singeing it.

**海因里希**：……\
**Heinrich**: ...

绅士熟悉的身影一晃而过。\
The familiar figure of a gentleman flits into the scene.

**马库斯**：海因里希！\
**Marcus**: Heinrich!

脚下骤然踏空了一步。\
A foot almost steps on air.

**霍夫曼**：……！\
**Hofmann**: ...!

**霍夫曼**：唔，地板上有陷阱……！\
**Hofmann**: Ugh, there are traps under the floor!

这里十分静谧。\
This opera is silent.

没有观众，没有奏乐，没有碍事的其他演员。\
No audience, no music, not a word or note from any actors.

一处理想的地点。\
A space to think.

**卡卡尼亚**：——伊索尔德！\
**Kakania**: Isolde!

呼喊声从帷幔的另一端传来。\
Cries echo from behind the curtain.

她睁开眼睛，看着自己所等的另一个主角跳上舞台。\
She opens her eyes as another protagonist leaps onto the stage.

**伊索尔德**：……医生。\
**Isolde**: Doctor.

## 6TH-20 战争与和平 / War and Peace

我望向它来，关乎一切的，生的巨环。 你的双手合围成圆，宣判。 最后可塑的白日，历史消逝的黄昏。 世界呵！头吞食着脚，足抵着鼻尖。 人呵！栖居于大地，等待天空沉坠。 昨日转向明日，明日成为昨日。 雨幕之下，谁将泯没——\
I looked at it, the ring of life, the ring of all lives. Your hands form the ring, and the judgment is pronounced. On the doomsday, at the dusk when history fades away. Oh world! Its head bites its feet, its knees touch its nose. Oh man! They inhabit the earth, waiting for the sky to fall. Yesterday turns into tomorrow, tomorrow reverts to yesterday. Who shall vanish in the rain?

又有谁会获得那永恒的幸福，无上的恩赐—— ——那不复存在的虚无？\
Who shall be granted the eternal happiness, the grace from above— And that emptiness, the cessation of existence?

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德，您到底想做什么？！\
**Kakania**: What is it that you want, Isolde?!

**卡卡尼亚**：我还以为基金会的人夸大了事实。可您现在，您现在——\
**Kakania**: I thought the Foundation was exaggerating the truth. But you, you are ...

**伊索尔德**：——您在生气吗，医生？因为我杀死了卡尔先生？\
**Isolde**: Are you mad, doctor? Because I killed Mr. Karl?

**伊索尔德**：……我以为您会高兴。\
**Isolde**: ... I thought it would make you happy.

**卡卡尼亚**：——我？我为什么会高兴？\
**Kakania**: Happy? Why would I be happy?

**伊索尔德**：因为他是一个徒有其表的人，一个违背您医嘱的人，一个造成我们时代普遍压抑的人，一个您最痛恨的官僚。\
**Isolde**: Because he was a boastful man, his ideas were at odds with yours, and he contributed to the repression of this era. A bureaucrat you hate the most.

**伊索尔德**：他对待我们，正如墙壁上的一处污点，仓促掩埋了事。要是贴了金子，他就将它撕下来，藏在自己的口袋里。\
**Isolde**: He treated us like stains on the wall to be covered up in shame. And he was the kind of man who'd pocket the gold foil whenever he found any.

**伊索尔德**：而社会就在伪装中败坏。难道我们不应做一场大手术，将这样的人从我们的社会中切割出去吗？\
**Isolde**: Society is dying because of these hypocrites. Don't you think we should have the surgery and remove them?

她的话语真挚而纯粹。\
Her words, mad as they are, manage to convey a warm sincerity.

**卡卡尼亚**：……我不知道……\
**Kakania**: ... I didn't know ...

**卡卡尼亚**：我不知道，您会这样理解那些话。\
**Kakania**: I didn't know you would interpret my words this way.

**卡卡尼亚**：我真后悔把这些话告诉您……\
**Kakania**: I deeply regret ever telling you that ...

**伊索尔德**：……什么？\
**Isolde**: ... What?

**伊索尔德**：您为什么要说出这么狠心的话？\
**Isolde**: Why? Why are you being so cruel to me?

**伊索尔德**：是您对我说，我们每个人都生病了，冠冕堂皇，奄奄一息，但这病灶并非长在我们自己身上，而是在我们每天呼吸的时代的病态之中。\
**Isolde**: It was you who said that everyone was sick and dying, even though they pretended to be fine. Yet the source of the sickness lay not in ourselves, but in the twisted era we lived in.

**伊索尔德**：要想终结这丑恶的一切，唯有通过一场彻底的手术……\
**Isolde**: A radical surgery is the only way to remove this ugly tumor ...

**伊索尔德**：是您告诉我，我们须释放心中的压抑，拥抱原初的激情，将世界还原为它的本来面目，一个自由平等的独立王国。那时所有人都会获得幸福和快乐……\
**Isolde**: And it was also you who told me to stop repressing and to embrace my desires. We should restore the world to what it was like, a kingdom of freedom where everyone will be happy ...

**伊索尔德**：我哪里听错了吗……？我哪里理解错了吗？\
**Isolde**: Are these not your words? Or have I misunderstood them?

**卡卡尼亚**：…………\
**Kakania**: ...

**伊索尔德**：您为什么不愿意抬头看我……？因为我犯下的过错如此重大，让您不愿再见到我吗？\
**Isolde**: Why won't you look at me? Have I made such a big mistake that you don't want to see me again?

**伊索尔德**：不，不……\
**Isolde**: No, no, no ...

**伊索尔德**：请您回答我，我乞求您。因为您是我唯一的朋友，也是我世界上最珍视的人……\
**Isolde**: Please answer me, I'm begging you. You are my only friend and the one I cherish most in the whole world ...

**伊索尔德**：医生，我究竟是哪里做错了，让您不能原谅我？\
**Isolde**: Doctor, what on earth have I done wrong? Why won't you forgive me?

卡卡尼亚只是沉默着，像一个冰冷的雕塑。\
Kakania's stone-like visage does not crack.

伊索尔德不可控制地抽噎了。\
Isolde chokes dramatically.

**伊索尔德**：是因为我太笨……所以理解错了吗？\
**Isolde**: Is it because ... I'm too stupid to understand your words?

**伊索尔德**：还是因为我也生病了，所以无药可救……？\
**Isolde**: Or because I'm also sick with the incurable tumor?

**伊索尔德**：那样的话，就请您救救我吧……像过去那样牵起我的手，抚摸我的面孔，揽住我的肩膀，同我说一些亲切的话。\
**Isolde**: If that's the case, please help me ... Hold my hands, touch my face, hug me, and talk to me heart to heart like you used to.

**伊索尔德**：医生，医生……\
**Isolde**: Doctor, doctor ...

她缓缓地走到卡卡尼亚身边。\
Isolde approaches.

试图抓住一片缥缈的衣角。\
She reaches out a grasping hand at a fleeting corner of her garment.

**伊索尔德**：……我在您的梦想中映出自己，就像凝望一面镜子。\
**Isolde**: ... I saw myself in that dream of yours, like looking into a mirror.

**伊索尔德**：在与您对谈的黄昏，我第一次见到太阳。\
**Isolde**: It was dusk when we had that conversation. It was the first time in my life that I saw the sun.

**伊索尔德**：是您的梦想填满了我空虚的生命，让我不再是诅咒的容器。\
**Isolde**: Your dream filled my empty life with meaning. You saved me from being just a cursed vessel.

**伊索尔德**：它很美……\
**Isolde**: That was a beautiful dream ...

**伊索尔德**：美到在对它的凝视中，我忘却了自己的丑陋。\
**Isolde**: So beautiful that I forgot how ugly I was while staring at it.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

**伊索尔德**：我只是想把您的理想还给您。\
**Isolde**: I'm just trying to realize your dream.

**伊索尔德**：我……错了吗？\
**Isolde**: Am I ... wrong?

**卡卡尼亚**：……但我从来没有想过，您因此会去犯罪。\
**Kakania**: ... I never thought you would commit a crime over my words.

**伊索尔德**：犯罪？您是指我现在所做的事吗？您不喜欢这样吗？\
**Isolde**: Crime? You mean what I'm doing right now? You don't like it?

她焦急地上前一步，生恐自己错过了什么。\
She steps forward anxiously, fearing she might miss something.

**伊索尔德**：基金会知道所有的真相，却不曾告诉我们分毫。\
**Isolde**: The Foundation knows all the truths, yet they won't tell us anything.

**伊索尔德**：因此，我们需释放他们所压抑的一切……新闻、癔症、暴动、混乱。这是重塑之手告诉我的。\
**Isolde**: That's why we have to release everything they repress ... the news, the hysteria, the riots, the chaos. That's what Manus Vindictae told me.

**伊索尔德**：这和您的理念并不一致吗？是我会错意了吗？\
**Isolde**: Is this not like your dream? Did I misunderstand?

**卡卡尼亚**：什么？他们该死的都告诉了你什么？\
**Kakania**: What? What in the world did they tell you?

**伊索尔德**：呵呵……他们给了我拯救的方法，医生。\
**Isolde**: Heh heh ... They told me the method of salvation, doctor.

**伊索尔德**：他们让我有机会拯救那些被您爱着的人，拯救世界——拯救您的梦想。\
**Isolde**: They gave me the opportunity to save your loved ones, the world, and your dream.

身体摔得很痛。\
The fall is painful.

舞台下方的空间宽阔得超乎了意料。\
The space below the stage feels unexpectedly vast.

**马库斯**：咳咳……\
**Marcus**: *coughs*

**马库斯**：这是什么地方？\
**Marcus**: Where am I?

巨大的舞台道具充斥着空间，黑白描绘的光影被直接画在了地上。\
Enormous props fill the back area, with black and white shadows painted directly onto the floor.

这里就像舞台之下的另一个舞台。\
Forming another stage beneath the stage.

似曾相识的古怪香气在空气中弥漫，马库斯忍不住揉了揉鼻子。\
A familiar scent lingers in the air, prompting Marcus to rub her nose.

**马库斯**：咳咳，好熟悉的味道……\
**Marcus**: *coughs* I've smelled this before ...

**霍夫曼**：……！\
**Hofmann**: ...!

**海因里希**：欢迎你们。安杰罗提，和不知名字的政府女士。\
**Heinrich**: Welcome, Angelotti, and Unknown Lady from the Foundation.

**海因里希**：——欢迎来到我们重塑世界的小小起点。\
**Heinrich**: Welcome to the small beginning of our new world.

舞台之上，他看上去仍是一位无害的绅士。\
On the stage, he still gives a perfect impression of a harmless gentleman.

音效-子弹打出，音效。

**海因里希**：喔！拉普拉斯的催眠孢子弹头……女士，您险些就打中我了！\
现在可不是能让你们过去的时候，主演正忙着呢。\
**Heinrich**: Whoa! Sleeping bullets from Laplace ... You almost hit me, miss!\
I can't let you through, though, not now. The leading actress is busy.

海因里希抱怨着，往旁边跳了一步。\
Heinrich complains, hopping to the side and out of the bullet's path.

**海因里希**：女士们，舞台刚刚拉开帷幕，一切尚待开始。在灯光亮起之前，何不敞开心扉？\
**Heinrich**: The curtain has been raised, ladies, and the show is about to begin. Why not open your hearts before the lights come on?

**海因里希**：让我们像个文明人那样，坐下来好好谈谈——噢！\
**Heinrich**: Let's sit down and have a civilized conversa—whoa!

这发子弹射得更准了，但空气中的那些烟尘干扰了视线。\
This next bullet fires true, but the air is so clouded with dust that the target had already moved before it struck.

**霍夫曼**：……和恐怖分子没有什么好说的。\
**Hofmann**: There is no need to negotiate with a terrorist.

**霍夫曼**：把你带回基金会总部后，会有专员与你详谈。\
**Hofmann**: You will have the chance to talk to our specialist after I take you to the headquarters.

**海因里希**：恐怖分子！您竟然这样称呼我？！\
**Heinrich**: A terrorist? You wound me!

**海因里希**：是因为我戴上了宽仁面具？因为我们揭开了你们隐瞒的真相？还是因为我们——\
**Heinrich**: Is it because I wear the mask of Manus? Because I revealed the truth you've been hiding? Or because ...

**海因里希**：加速了“暴雨”，让这个时代提前落幕？\
**Heinrich**: ... we accelerated the "Storm" and made this era end earlier than expected?

回应他的是一道破空而来的术式辉光。\
A glow of arcane skill breaks through in response to his query.

马库斯抬起手，那盏提灯驱散了一部分黑暗。\
Marcus raises her hand, the lamp dispelling some of the darkness.

**马库斯**：我来协助您，霍夫曼女士——\
**Marcus**: Let me help you, Madam Hofmann!

**海因里希**：天呐，安杰罗提，您又为何要与仇人为伍？您也应是我们中的一员。\
**Heinrich**: My Angelotti, why are you standing with the enemy? You're supposed to be one of us.

**马库斯**：安杰罗提……？他是在说我？\
**Marcus**: Angelotti ...? Is that me?

**海因里希**：——我是在“拯救”您，从真正的恐怖分子手中！\
**Heinrich**: I am your "salvation," from the real terrorists of the world!

**马库斯**：……拯救？\
**Marcus**: ... "Salvation"?

熟悉的名词令她警觉地抬起头。\
This familiar term catches her ears, burning in them.

不知为何，普通的话语却令人无比烦躁。\
This ordinary word has become most irritating.

布景道具中，那场隐藏在阴影中的演讲还在继续。\
The speech, given from the cover of the props, continues.

**海因里希**：拿着书箱的安杰罗提！您阅读过那么多书目，处理过那么多文书，但它们中可有任何一本——\
**Heinrich**: Angelotti with a full case of books! Tell me, of all the books you have read and all the documents you have worked with, did any of them ...

**海因里希**：向您介绍那场真实历史的灾难，将在1914年的夏天猛然爆发的——\
**Heinrich**: ... mention the catastrophe that suddenly broke out in the summer of 1914?

**海因里希**：那场20世纪的浩劫？\
**Heinrich**: The scourge of the 20th century, the real history!

**伊索尔德**：您还不知道，医生，像您这样心肠柔软的人，又怎么会承受得住呢？\
**Isolde**: You have such a kind heart, doctor, yet you don't know the truth. How are you going to bear the pain when you do?

**伊索尔德**：西奥菲尔点燃了自己，本吊死了，伊曼纽尔躺在了铁轨上——\
**Isolde**: Theophil set himself on fire, Ben hanged himself to death, Emmanuel laid himself on the railroad tracks ...

**卡卡尼亚**：这些是维也纳之前死于自杀的人……？重塑都接触了他们……？\
**Kakania**: Are they the suicide cases in Vienna? They all came into contact with the Manus?

伊索尔德仰起脖子，口中发出破碎的笑声。\
Isolde tilts her head back, laughing brokenly.

**伊索尔德**：呵呵，哈哈哈哈哈……我也看得见他们，我听得见他们，这些未来历史的幽灵，徘徊在这座城市的上空！\
**Isolde**: Heh heh, hahahaha ... I can see them, I can hear them, the ghosts of future history, haunting the city from above!

**伊索尔德**：带着窟窿的脑袋！嵌着弹片的脑袋！空空的胃袋！幼小的，如同婴儿一般的幽灵……我看得到，看得到！被炸成废墟的城市，载着人的火车直直地冲向死亡！\
**Isolde**: Heads full of holes! Heads covered in shrapnel! Empty stomachs! Even the ghosts of little children ... I can see them all! Cities bombed to the ground, and trains full of people headed straight for death!

**伊索尔德**：这一切马上就要来了，马上就要到啦！绕在枝桠上的肠子比春日的花还要艳哩！子弹，头盔，纱布……哈哈哈！\
**Isolde**: It is coming, IT IS COMING! By then, the guts hanging from trees will be more vibrant than spring flowers! There will be bullets, helmets, gauze! Hahaha!

**伊索尔德**：——我们已经没有未来了，医生！\
**Isolde**: We have no future, doctor!

**海因里希**：我多希望那真的是一场闹剧，一场夺去一千多万普通人性命的闹剧，一场几十个国家首脑也跟着参与的闹剧。\
**Heinrich**: How I wish it were a farce, a farce that claimed the lives of more than ten million people, a farce that dozens of leaders decided to take part in.

**海因里希**：……本，我的友人，他演奏过最精彩的《a小调前奏曲》——但他回来的时候，左臂与左腿都被留在了战场上。\
**Heinrich**: ... Ben, a dear friend of mine ... He played the best Fantasia in A Minor ever, but came back from the battlefield missing an arm and a leg.

他仍记得那天。慷慨的勿忘我先生踏过甲板，将他急切的询问用一沓厚厚的信件堵在了喉咙里。\
He remembers that day. When the generous Mr. Forget Me Not stepped across the deck, his questions stifled by a stack of thick letters.

**海因里希**：伊曼纽尔，他那双手只应为写诗而生，可他没日没夜地挖壕沟，最终死在一场疫病里。\
**Heinrich**: And Emmanuel. His hands were born to write poetry, but he was sent to the front and dug trenches until he died of disease.

伊曼纽尔又是从何时起不再画画了呢？就连友人的笔迹也在记忆里变得模糊。\
When did Emanuel stop painting? He could not even recall his old friend's handwriting ... It was blurry now.

唯有愤怒如此鲜明。\
Only his anger remains vivid.

**海因里希**：我们的双手本该握着画笔，按动琴键，书写故事……却因为你们的狭隘和虚伪，被煽动、被怂恿，一批一批地暴露于炮火之下。\
**Heinrich**: Our hands are meant to hold paintbrushes, play pianos, and write stories ... but they end up in gunfire because you narrow-minded hypocrites keep inciting them to violence.

**海因里希**：我们因自己的天赋曾受尽排挤，却又要眼睁睁地看着我这些充满天赋的友人为了人类的博弈与“小脾气”殒命。\
**Heinrich**: We've already suffered for our gifts. Now we have to watch our talented friends sacrifice themselves for man's childish tantrums.

**海因里希**：女士，你们熟知这些——又怎么能将我们唤作恐怖分子呢？\
**Heinrich**: Ladies, you know all of this ... yet you call us terrorists?

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

**霍夫曼**：……咳！\
**Hofmann**: *coughs weakly*

一直没有说话的霍夫曼突然咳出了一口鲜血。\
Having been quiet for a worrying amount of time, Hofmann coughs up a mouthful of blood, dragging attention back to her.

**马库斯**：……？！\
**Marcus**: ...?!

霍夫曼捂住胸口，近乎跌倒地半蹲下去。\
Hofmann clutches her chest, falling just short of collapsing to her knees.

她的脸色煞白，马库斯第一次见到那张淡然的脸上如此痛苦。\
Her face is now deathly pale, and Marcus watches as the cold face she wears contorts with streaks of pain and unease.

**马库斯**：霍夫曼女士……？霍夫曼女士！\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann? Madam Hofmann!

而海因里希只是自顾自地继续说下去。\
Heinrich continues to speak, entirely unconcerned.

他指向霍夫曼。\
He points at Hofmann.

**海因里希**：真正的恐怖分子是你们——人类！\
**Heinrich**: The real terrorists are you, humans!

**海因里希**：是你们发起了那场战争！\
**Heinrich**: It was you who started that war!

## 6TH-21 回旋镖 / Double Cross

从闻到后台的香味起，她就觉得有些奇怪。\
The scent from backstage strikes her as odd.

体内仿佛有一处被忽略的地方被重新唤醒，有什么在胸腔中跳动，不停地跳动，跳动，跳动。\
Something neglected within her stirs to life, pulsing in her chest—constantly pulsing, pulsing, pulsing.

**马库斯**：……霍夫曼，女士？\
**Marcus**: ... Madam ... Hofmann?

马库斯愣然地站着，看着那个可靠的身影朝地面倒去。\
Marcus stands stunned, watching her role model sink back to the ground.

**海因里希**：好在，引导之人听见了我们的哭喊，允诺我们以救恩。\
**Heinrich**: Fortunately, the Guiding One has heard our cries and promised us salvation.

**海因里希**：在一切美好的、艺术的、动人心弦的消失之前，“暴雨”为这场狂乱的曲目安上了休止符。\
**Heinrich**: The "Storm" will put a stop to this frenetic melody before all the good, artistic, heartfelt things in life are destroyed before our eyes.

**海因里希**：它会帮助我们冲刷掉未被挽留的、无足轻重之人——而那些罪魁祸首，应该得到更重的审判。\
**Heinrich**: It will wash away the unwanted, the unimportant. The creators of this chaos will be severely punished.

海因里希掏出怀表，看了一眼。\
Heinrich checks his watch expectantly.

**海因里希**：勿忘我先生应允过我起效时间还差一点，但演员们应该就位了。\
**Heinrich**: It's still a little early for what Mr. Forget Me Not has planned. But the actors and actresses are in place.

**海因里希**：请您放心，安杰罗提小姐……我们不会落下任何一个同胞——也不会放过任何一个敌人。\
**Heinrich**: Don't worry, Ms. Angelotti ... We won't leave anyone behind ... Nor will we leave any enemy spared.

**海因里希**：我会帮助您认清自己，也会帮您清除敌人。\
**Heinrich**: I will eliminate the obstacles for you, and help you better understand yourself.

**马库斯**：……什么？你在说什么？\
**Marcus**: What? What are you talking about?

血液在体内奔流，如同上膛的枪。\
Blood courses through her in rapid fire.

越来越大，越来越响。\
The sound grows louder and more intense until she can hear it pounding in her ears.

**海因里希**：“筛选”已经开始了，女士们。\
**Heinrich**: The "sifting" has begun, ladies.

**海因里希**：这是勿忘我先生特意调配的药剂——来源自苦目树的馈赠。\
**Heinrich**: Enjoy! The potion specially made by Mr. Forget Me Not—a gift from the Picrasma tree.

**海因里希**：对拥有血脉的我们来说，它无疑能让我们的神秘学能力更加活跃，无论是身体，还是思维。\
**Heinrich**: For those who have arcanist blood, it will undoubtedly enhance their powers, both physically and mentally.

**海因里希**：但对于并无能力的人类混血种……它将是致命的毒药。\
**Heinrich**: But for the powerless mixed-blood humans ... It is lethal poison.

望着在烟雾作用下已经精神恍惚的年轻神秘学家，海因里希几不可闻地轻笑了一下。\
Watching the young arcanist stupefied by the smoke, Heinrich only chuckles.

**海因里希**：其实我们并没有那么大的区别，不是吗？神秘学家与人类早已通婚了许久。\
**Heinrich**: People sometimes forget how different humans and arcanists are, don't they? Marriages between the two races have been common for some time.

**海因里希**：构成社会多数的——是这些有一点神秘学血统，却因无能而理所当然地站在人类中的混血种。他们中多数只有不到四分之一的血统，甚至更低。\
**Heinrich**: The mixed-bloods have become the majority of society. Those with less than one-fourth arcanist blood, some with even less, have blended in amongst the humans because they don't have any arcane power.

**海因里希**：因而无论在官方认知上，还是自我认知上，他们都被视作人类……\
**Heinrich**: And so, they are seen as humans both by the public and by themselves ...

**海因里希**：而这就是背叛的惩罚！你们本该与我们站在一起，却在漫长的时间里与仇人狼狈为奸。\
**Heinrich**: And now, the punishment for betraying your own kind! You should've stood with us, but instead you sided with the enemy and watched your own kin suffer.

**海因里希**：那份存在在身体中却被忽略、被背叛的血脉将苏醒，炸开，从内部撕裂你。\
**Heinrich**: The blood that you have ignored and forsaken will awaken, explode, and tear you apart from within.

马库斯咬牙保持着理智，执拗地搀扶着霍夫曼的臂膀。而霍夫曼抬起一只手，拒绝了她。\
Marcus stubbornly supports Hofmann's arm, but Hofmann raises a hand to refuse her help.

**霍夫曼**：……没事，我没事……我只是有点——我还能站得住。\
**Hofmann**: ... I'm fine ... I'm just a bit ... I can still stand.

**海因里希**：很遗憾，您不会没事的。\
**Heinrich**: Sadly, you won't be fine for long.

**海因里希**：勿忘我先生对魔药的研究非常深入。他的配比应当会尽可能放大您的痛苦，女士——在死亡到来之前，这份痛苦将非常漫长。\
**Heinrich**: Mr. Forget Me Not is one of the best potion-makers. The formula is carefully designed to prolong your suffering until sweet death finally spreads its wings over you.

**海因里希**：但比起我同胞的遭遇，这又快得如同瞬息，您应当知足。\
**Heinrich**: But resent not! Your pain is fleeting compared to what my people were made to endure.

**海因里希**：——而现在，安杰罗提小姐，您又要如何选择？\
**Heinrich**: As for you, Ms. Angelotti, a choice lies before you.

在香味古怪的烟尘中，海因里希抬起了手。\
In the oddly scented smoke, Heinrich raises his hand.

**马库斯**：我……？\
**Marcus**: Me ...?

**海因里希**：您一直被蒙骗了，被人类编造出的历史。他们以伟大的名义造就了何等漫长的族群屠杀！\
**Heinrich**: You have been lied to. Humans have whispered lies through their petty, made-up history. There has been genocide, the lengthy, vicious kind, under the banner of high-minded reason.

**海因里希**：那名为进步和理性的，将世界泾渭分明地一分为二的欲望！它又导致了多少死亡和毁灭？\
**Heinrich**: They tried to split the world in two, so that the progressives cannot be stopped by the "non-progressives," so that the irrational cannot speak against the rational. When they do, death and destruction follow.

**海因里希**：而您，一个被抛弃在孤儿院的神秘学家孩子。您应当也能听见血脉在叩响您的心脏，呼唤您被遗落的魂灵。\
**Heinrich**: You're one of us, an arcanist child abandoned at an orphanage. You must've heard your heart pounding like a knock on the door; it's the sound of a long-lost soul coming home.

**海因里希**：它要您摒弃理智的枷锁，撕开历史的谎言，拥抱原初的激情，释放那与生俱来的天赋！\
**Heinrich**: It calls to you to rid your shackles of reason, to expose the lies of history, to embrace your primal passions, and unleash the powers of your gift!

**海因里希**：——您也理应是我们中的一员，从来如此！\
**Heinrich**: You should be one of us, as you always should have been!

**马库斯**：——\
**Marcus**: ...

苦目树的香气钻入了脑海。\
The aroma of the Picrasma tree comes to mind.

是的，她听见了。\
Yes, she hears it.

越过灰白格子织造的理智，穿过繁芜丛杂的信息之海，自爬虫脑响起的古老回声。\
Echoes up from the reptilian brain, reverberating along tangled knots of reason and knowledge.

——他说的是对的，马库斯！这就是你没能在基金会继续查阅的历史！\
He's right, Marcus! This is the missing part of history that they didn't let you go through!

——霍夫曼女士一直什么都不让你知道，不是吗？她骗了你！\
Hofmann kept everything from you, didn't she? She's a liar!

——你到这儿来只是想要知道真相，你从来都没有必要为人类的机构卖命！\
You're here because you want to find the truth. You don't have to work for a human institution!

无法遏制，连绵不绝。\
The invasion of thoughts continues without end.

“——咚。”\
*thud*

一把匕首被扔到了地面，握柄在地上打了几个旋儿。\
A dagger is thrown to the ground, spinning on its handle.

**海因里希**：捡起它，杀死您的导师，表决您的决心。\
**Heinrich**: Pick it up. Drive it into your mentor's heart. Show us your resolve.

**海因里希**：这是一个机会，一个得知自己真正是谁，起源何处，又因何被抛弃的机会。\
**Heinrich**: An opportunity has arisen. Take it. A chance to learn who you really are, where you came from, and why you were abandoned.

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

她捡起了匕首，刀尖向外。\
She picks up the dagger with blade pointing outward.

**霍夫曼**：马库斯……\
**Hofmann**: Marcus ...

**海因里希**：很好，安杰罗提！\
**Heinrich**: Very good, Angelotti!

**海因里希**：在午夜的至高者落下怜悯的泪水，洗刷尽一切人类的罪孽之前——通过这场筛选，加入我们吧。\
**Heinrich**: Before the High One of Midnight sheds merciful tears and washes away the sins of man—pass the test and join us.

**海因里希**：然后，我们将带您越过“暴雨”，重回——属于我们的时代。\
**Heinrich**: And we will take you through the "Storm," back to our era.

**马库斯**：……属于我们的时代？\
**Marcus**: Our ... era?

一滴泪水从她的脸上滑落。\
A tear slides across her face.

**马库斯**：可是属于我的时代……已经到来了。\
**Marcus**: But my era has already come.

**马库斯**：被您用“暴雨”所毁灭的1914年——正是我的时代！\
**Marcus**: 1914, the year you once wiped out with the "Storm," is my era!

**海因里希**：……？\
**Heinrich**: ...?

她握着匕首，绝望地仰望着有顶的穹幕。\
She holds the dagger, looking up at the dome in despair.

**马库斯**：我在荒岛上等待，在白屋子里等待，等过时间的车轮历经1966，掠过1929，终于重回这个年代……\
**Marcus**: I waited in the abandoned lighthouse of that island, I waited in the marble house of the Foundation, watching the time go back to 1966, to 1929, and finally back here ...

**马库斯**：您说您在拯救，可是你们只是用毁灭取代了另一场毁灭，用死亡取代了另一场死亡。\
**Marcus**: You say this is salvation, but you're just replacing one annihilation with another.

**马库斯**：我们本来有可能避免这一切，你们却在加速悲剧的发生。你们根本不关心这个时代，也不关心生活在上面的人。\
**Marcus**: The Foundation wants to stop the destruction, but you are speeding it up. You don't care about this era, nor the people living in it.

**马库斯**：你们只是抛弃他们，躲到一个属于你们的空中王国去，一个尚不存在的玫瑰花园去，那里有艺术、诗歌，也许还有一架钢琴……呵呵呵，呵呵呵呵呵……\
**Marcus**: You abandon them. You hide in your empty kingdom, in-in your garden that doesn't yet exist, with your, haha, with your art, your-your poems, and your pianos, hahahaha!

**马库斯**：而我，我只是……想回去看一眼。为什么这么简单的心愿你也要阻碍？！\
**Marcus**: And me, I just wanted to go home for a visit. Why would you take away even that?!

**霍夫曼**：马库斯，不要步入疯狂——\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, don't lose control of yourself!

已经晚了。\
It's too late.

她不顾一切地冲向了男人。\
She charges toward the man.

**马库斯**：——海因里希，我要杀了你！！！\
**Marcus**: ... I'll kill you, Heinrich!!!

**伊索尔德**：……有人在呼唤着我。\
**Isolde**: ... Someone is calling me.

**伊索尔德**：和我一起离开吧，医生。在这个旧世界被雨幕冲刷时，我们将一起在新世界建设您的梦想。\
**Isolde**: Leave here with me, doctor. Let the rain wash away the old world, so we can build your dream in a new one.

**伊索尔德**：在释放压抑上，我们的目标是一致的。在给予神秘学家自由上，我们也是一致的。\
**Isolde**: I thought we were on the same side of liberating our repression, giving freedom to the arcanists.

她期盼地伸出手。\
She stretches out her hand to her.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

可是卡卡尼亚只是站在那里。她握紧拳头，又松开，这样徒劳地反复。\
But Kakania stands stiff, clenching and unclenching her fist in futile repetition.

**卡卡尼亚**：我只是……\
**Kakania**: I just …

**卡卡尼亚**：我从没想过你……你会去杀人，伊索尔德。\
**Kakania**: I never thought that you would take people's lives, Isolde.

伊索尔德欣喜地抬起头来。\
Isolde looks up with a maddening joy plastered on her face.

**伊索尔德**：所以这就是原因？\
**Isolde**: Is this why you hesitate?

**伊索尔德**：因为我杀错了人吗？因为我杀了一个基金会的先生？是因为您刚认识的那个小助手吗？\
**Isolde**: Because I killed a person who shouldn't be killed? A person from the Foundation? After you befriended the young lady?

**伊索尔德**：是因为您已经原谅了基金会，我却和他们的敌人——重塑之手走在一起吗？\
**Isolde**: Is it because you made peace with the Foundation, and yet I became associated with Manus Vindictae?

她得到了答案，眼中也因此闪烁着喜悦的光。\
She found her answer. Her eyes twinkle with delight.

**伊索尔德**：我知道了，我明白了，医生。我会弥补我犯下的错误。\
**Isolde**: I see now, I understand, doctor. I will correct my mistakes.

**卡卡尼亚**：……伊索尔德？\
**Kakania**: ... Isolde?

**伊索尔德**：我杀了一位基金会的先生，您认为我将重塑之手的理念置于您的理想之上。这让您不满了，对吗？\
**Isolde**: I killed a man of the Foundation, thus you thought I was imposing Manus Vindictae's cause over yours. It displeased you, am I right?

**伊索尔德**：——那么，我会证明我的立场。\
**Isolde**: ... Then I shall prove myself to you.

她从裙摆下拿出一把手枪。\
She produces a pistol out from beneath her skirt.

它曾帮助西奥菲尔结束了痛苦，这次又接下了更重大的使命。\
It once helped end Theophil's suffering, and now it will take on a greater mission.

**伊索尔德**：我会去杀了海因里希，这样就公平了。\
**Isolde**: I will take Heinrich's life, for that would make it fair.

**伊索尔德**：请您在一旁为我见证，医生。\
**Isolde**: Please come with me and witness my commitment, doctor.

**卡卡尼亚**：……？！\
**Kakania**: ...?!

**卡卡尼亚**：……什么？你在说什么？……你要杀了谁？\
**Kakania**: What? What did you say? ... You're going to kill ... who?

但是，伊索尔德已经提起裙摆，优雅地行了一个礼。\
But Isolde has already lifted her skirt, bowing gracefully to the doctor.

熟悉的神秘术波动——正是那道送卡尔登上舞台的传送咒文。\
The familiar surge of arcane energy—the same teleportation incantation that brought Karl to the stage.

短暂的眩目之后，她们已经身处舞台的另一端。\
After a brief flash of light, they find themselves on the other side of the stage.

这里刚刚经历了一番激烈的搏斗。\
Where a fierce battle has just taken place.

**霍夫曼**：……呃……\
**Hofmann**: ... Ugh ...

霍夫曼痛苦地半跪在地上，她扯开自己的领巾，可怖的目状纹路已经从心脏蔓延到了胸口。\
Hofmann kneels in agony, tearing off her scarf to reveal the terrifying pattern of toxic veins that has spread from her heart across her chest.

药剂确实是致命的——原本薄弱的血脉被强行激活，这具躯体就像一架超负荷运转的机器，稍加移动就会从内部炸开。\
The potion is indeed lethal—forcefully activating her already weak blood vessels, turning her body into an overburdened machine, ready to explode on the slightest movement.

海因里希没有说谎，她将在不可回避的漫长痛苦中迈向死亡。\
Heinrich then did not lie—she was destined for a long, unavoidable, agonizing march toward death.

**马库斯**：呜……我要杀了你…………\
**Marcus**: *growls* I'm going to kill ...

而马库斯也如同预定一般，在血脉的影响下陷入了巨大的情绪旋涡。\
And Marcus, pulled as if by fate, finds herself caught in an all-consuming emotional whirlwind from her revelations.

但她的天赋却并非为战斗而生，错误的用法仅是让她更加失控。\
Her gift was not meant for battle—its misuse only makes her lose control even more.

**海因里希**：安杰罗提小姐，如果您释放自己后也仍旧执迷不悟，那您便不再是我们的同胞。\
**Heinrich**: Ms. Angelotti, if you still don't see the big picture after returning to your true self, you are not one of us.

**海因里希**：在“暴雨”落下之前，好好享受我们的“筛选”吧。\
**Heinrich**: Enjoy the "sifting" before the "Storm."

海因里希怜悯地踢了她一脚，不再将这个初出茅庐的神秘学家放在眼里。\
Heinrich kicks her away with indifference, no longer regarding the novice arcanist with any concern.

而伊索尔德恰在此刻从虚空中降临，如有神灵附身。\
And at this moment, Isolde descends from the void, as if possessed by some strange deity.

**海因里希**：伊索尔德，你来得正好，这两个人已经无药可救——\
**Heinrich**: Isolde, you're just in time. These two are hopeless—

狂热者的话音未落——\
The zealot's words hang in the air ...

而她微笑着抬起手臂。\
As she smiles and raises her arm.

那把致命的火器对准了曾经的友人，基线笔直，弧度优雅。\
The deadly firearm is aimed at her once-friend, with a straight baseline and graceful arc.

**伊索尔德**：——再见，海因里希。\
**Isolde**: ... Goodbye, Heinrich.

## 6TH-22 空白页 / Finished Page

**霍夫曼**：呼，呼啊……\
**Hofmann**: *pants*

前所未有的痛楚，就像强行击发一把被塞入错误子弹的手枪。\
An unprecedented agony, like the bursting of a bullet in a chamber too small for it, only writ large to each vein across her body.

想要调动理智，但得到的只有破碎的思绪。\
She tries to summon her reason, looking for a way out, but only shattered half-thoughts come to her.

——把海因里希带回去，他知道很重要的信息！\
Heinrich must be taken to the headquarters. He has vital information!

——任务已经失败了，不会再有支援到来。“暴雨”倒计时已经发布，所有人都必须回到总部。\
The mission has failed. There will be no back-up. The "Storm" countdown has begun, everyone will be called back to the headquarters.

——这已经是第九次“暴雨”了！错过这一次，又要等到哪一次？！\
This is the ninth "Storm"! How much longer will we have to wait if we miss this opportunity?!

——再不撤离，马库斯也会沾染暴雨症候群，她已经失控了！\
Must leave at once. Marcus will have the Storm Syndrome if she stays here. She's losing herself!

——有枪声。伊索尔德，卡卡尼亚。她们为什么在这里？\
Gun shot. Isolde, Kakania. Why are they here?

**海因里希**：啊啊——！托斯卡……！你竟然，将匕首对准我！\
**Heinrich**: Ahh! Tosca ...! You're turning your dagger at me?!

**海因里希**：是我，将拯救之道分享给你们——！是我，带你们面见引导之人——！\
**Heinrich**: Me! The one who showed you the way to salvation! Me! The one who brought you all to the Guiding One!

**海因里希**：是我，替你向勿忘我求情，只为再给卡卡尼亚一个资格……\
**Heinrich**: I even pleaded with Forget Me Not to keep a spot for Kakania, for your sake ...

**海因里希**：你凭什么这样对我？！\
**Heinrich**: How could you do this to me?!

子弹在击发过程中受到了些许偏移，这一发只是射中了海因里希的小腿。\
The bullet deviates slightly as it fires, hitting Heinrich's calf in a painful but not immediately lethal shot.

**伊索尔德**：医生，您为什么要阻止我？\
**Isolde**: Doctor, why are you trying to stop me?

**卡卡尼亚**：您也还认为我是医生？！我不能再让您杀人了！\
**Kakania**: You still think of me as a doctor!? I can't let you do any more killing!

**卡卡尼亚**：马库斯小姐，您能站起来吗？我来牵制他们，您带霍夫曼女士先去安全的地方……\
**Kakania**: Ms. Marcus, can you get on your feet? I'll slow them down, get Madam Hofmann to safety ...

喧嚣远去了，耳边只有血液在血管中奔流的声音。\
The clamor fades away, leaving only the sound of turgid blood stickily moving through her veins.

啊，原来这就是神秘学家的世界。理智是那么无处可寻，一切都被放大为了感受。\
Alas, this is the world of the arcanist. Reason is nowhere to be found, and everything is magnified by the senses.

地板冰冷，声音喧闹，空气中弥散着香气——就是这种香气将致她于死地。\
The floor is cold, the din loud, the air filled with a scent—one that will lead her to her death.

视野有着锐利的边缘，一切都那么缓慢，陷入梦魇的马库斯，极力阻止伊索尔德的卡卡尼亚。\
Her vision has sharp edges cutting into her sight, and everything moves slow, making out Marcus as she is plunged into a nightmare, then the good doctor Kakania desperately attempting to hold back Isolde.

以及——伊索尔德的枪口指向的海因里希。\
And—Isolde's gun pointed at Heinrich.

**伊索尔德**：海因里希……你看起来很痛苦。\
**Isolde**: Heinrich ... You seem to be in pain.

**伊索尔德**：嘘，没关系的……你很快就会从这里解脱了。\
**Isolde**: Shhh, it's alright ... Soon you will be freed from the pain.

**霍夫曼**：……\
**Hofmann**: ...

——你疯了，霍夫曼，不能这么做！应有更稳妥的方式！\
You're out of your mind, Hofmann. Don't! There must be a better way.

——错过这一次，又要等到什么时候？！难道我还能搭上返程的火车？难道我还会有下一次？！\
But how long do we have to wait for another opportunity like this?! You think you can still make it back to the headquarters? You think there will be a second chance for you?

——即使失败了，也要保下马库斯。\
Even if we fail, Marcus will be safe.

——局势变化了，扭转战局的关键在卡卡尼亚的选择。\
The situation has changed. Kakania's decision is the key to victory.

——不能让线索在这里断掉！\
Can't let the clues end here!

——这是最理智的决断。\
This is the wisest decision.

她用全身的力气动了起来。\
She rises with all her strength.

伊索尔德并未看到新的阻碍，她只是专注于最初的敌人。\
Isolde sees no new obstacles, focusing only on her initial enemy.

她扣下了扳机。\
She pulls the trigger.

**马库斯**：……霍夫曼，女士？\
**Marcus**: ... Madam ... Hofmann?

陷入混乱的女孩目睹了这一幕。\
The girl, mired in chaos, witnesses this scene.

“阅读”罔顾个人意志地开启了。\
Her "reading" commences, disregarding her own personal will.

“不能让伊索尔德杀死重要的线索人物——霍夫曼女士是这样想的，可是，她好些了吗？”\
"'I can't let Isolde kill such a vital source of information.' That's what Madam Hofmann's thinking, but ... what about her poison?"

“子弹上有着灵的气息……啊，是的，那是伊索尔德的神秘术。”\
"The bullet reeks of ghosts and spirits ... Oh right, it's Isolde's arcane skill."

“卡卡尼亚……她好像呆住了，她的大脑一片空白，我什么都读不到。”\
"Kakania ... She has gone blank. I can't read anything from her mind."

“海因里希——他自诩为拯救者。在这个时候，他又在想什么呢……？”\
"And there's Heinrich, who claims to be the savior. What is he thinking right now?"

“——砰！”\
*crash*

枪声终于落地。\
The gunshot finally hits true.

一条弹道，两条人命。\
One shot, two lives.

伊索尔德的子弹同时贯穿了霍夫曼和海因里希。\
Isolde's bullet pierces through both Hofmann and Heinrich.

——这是“阅读”给出的信息。\
This is the information her "reading" provides.

**马库斯**：不——霍夫曼女士！\
**Marcus**: No! Madam Hofmann!!!

她几乎是手脚并用地爬到了导师的身边。\
She crawls on hands and knees to her mentor's side.

**马库斯**：不，不……！\
**Marcus**: No, no!

**霍夫曼**：咳……\
**Hofmann**: *coughs weakly*

**霍夫曼**：……海因里希，还活着吗？\
**Hofmann**: ... Is Heinrich ... still alive?

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

马库斯看着被血泊覆盖的舞台，声音颤抖着。\
Marcus looks at the stage, now coated with blood, her voice trembling.

**马库斯**：他……死了……\
**Marcus**: He ... he's gone ...

**霍夫曼**：……是吗，没能赶上。\
**Hofmann**: ... I see. Should have been faster.

**霍夫曼**：那么，你立刻带卡卡尼亚离开，她有能力从伊索尔德手中保护你。看目前的情况，她并不会选择重塑之手。\
**Hofmann**: You must take Kakania and leave. She can protect you from Isolde. She won't side with the Manus, from what I see.

**霍夫曼**：把我的避难名额给她，她的神秘术将能在以后的行动上派上用处。\
**Hofmann**: Give her my place in the "Storm" shelter. Her arcane power will be useful to us.

**霍夫曼**：这样一来，至少你们能安全撤离。\
**Hofmann**: So the both of you can evacuate safely.

**马库斯**：……您，都计划好了吗？\
**Marcus**: Did, did you plan this all along?

**霍夫曼**：咳……马库斯，不要落泪。我知道自己在做什么。\
**Hofmann**: *coughs weakly* Don't cry, Marcus. I know what I'm doing.

**霍夫曼**：在死神到来之前，我反而取回了理智。痛苦不会更加漫长，如今仍能带着理性死去，也是我的荣幸。\
**Hofmann**: I have taken back my senses before I die. I'm glad. The pain will cease. To die with my sanity and rationality still intact ... it has been an honor.

**马库斯**：不！！！\
**Marcus**: NO!!

**马库斯**：卡卡尼亚医生，您能做一个紧急治疗，把霍夫曼女士送去维也纳火车站吗！那里有其他基金会的人，他们有更精良的设备，一定可以……\
**Marcus**: Kakania, can you give her first aid and take her to the train station? You'll meet the Foundation there. They have better equipment, they'll know what to do ...

**马库斯**：即使海因里希死了，他身上一定也还藏着线索。还没有结束，我一定能完成任务……\
**Marcus**: Heinrich is dead, but there must still be clues on him. This isn't over yet, I have to finish the mission ...

霍夫曼只是微微摇了摇头，艰难地从怀中掏出一张纸。\
Hofmann just shakes her head; weak fingers struggle to pull out a piece of paper from her bosom.

**霍夫曼**：……马库斯，我有东西要给你。\
**Hofmann**: Marcus, take this.

**霍夫曼**：这个号码可以联系上那所收养你长大的罗马尼亚福利院。\
**Hofmann**: The number of that Orphanage in Romania.

**霍夫曼**：我很早就拿到了它，但是……\
**Hofmann**: I've had it with me for a while now. But ...

**马库斯**：……别说了，霍夫曼女士，这不是现在最重要的……\
**Marcus**: Please save your strength, madam, this isn't what we need to worry about ...

**霍夫曼**：……哪里有那么多重要的事。任务已经结束了，傻孩子。\
**Hofmann**: We don't have anything else to worry about. The mission is over, silly child.

**霍夫曼**：在“暴雨”落下之前，回家打一个电话吧。\
**Hofmann**: Ring home. Before the "Storm" comes.

**霍夫曼**：未来是……你们的时代。\
**Hofmann**: The future ... is yours.

她的手向下滑落——\
Her hand slides down.

这是近乎永恒的一秒钟。\
This last second between them becomes an age to itself.

**马库斯**：不，不，一定还有什么我能做的！\
**Marcus**: No, no! There must be something I can do!

**马库斯**：“一切都是书，一切都可以阅读！”\
**Marcus**: "Everything is a book. Everything can be read!"

**马库斯**：致命的……致命的是毒药……\
**Marcus**: The most immediate threat to her life ... is that potion ...

**马库斯**：魔鬼鞋带、颠茄、水仙根，苦目树树根和果实……\
**Marcus**: Devil's shoestring, belladonna, narcissus tazetta roots, and the fruits and roots of the Picrasma tree ...

**马库斯**：是勿忘我研制的配方，苦目树的比例在药剂中超过了百分之五十……和拉普拉斯的调制思路不同，魔药学家的配比几乎是依照灵感的指引……\
**Marcus**: It's the formula made by Forget Me Not. The Picrasma extract makes up more than 50% of the potion ... This is very different from Laplace's formula. Arcanist potions seem to be a concoction of instincts and inspiration.

**马库斯**：不……不！这无解。苦目树本身并非是毒药，只是人类……\
**Marcus**: Argh! Is there nothing else I can do? The Picrasma extract is not a poison in itself. Just that humans cannot ...

**马库斯**：一定还有办法……！但霍夫曼女士，霍夫曼女士很痛苦……\
**Marcus**: There must be a way! Madam ... Please! She's in pain ...

**马库斯**：只要我持续地阅读……一定会找到……\
**Marcus**: Don't give up, keep reading ... I will find a way ...

在翻页的瞬间，她意识到了一件事。\
As she turns the page, the realization hits.

即使她可以无穷无尽地阅读这一页，直到穷尽它的每一个细节……\
Even if she could read every detail, every exhaustive note on this page ...

也无法从火中救回一本燃烧的书。\
She cannot rescue a burning book from a fire. It's already gone.

**马库斯**：啊……\
**Marcus**: No ...

**霍夫曼**：书总是会读完的，马库斯。\
**Hofmann**: Every book has an end, Marcus.

**霍夫曼**：无论你想在这一页上停留多久，它总是会翻页的。\
**Hofmann**: There's nothing more on a finished page, no matter how reluctant you are to flip the page and get to the end.

**霍夫曼**：就像时间。\
**Hofmann**: You will move on to a new chapter.

**马库斯**：——不！！不要翻页！！！永远停在这一页上吧！求求您了！！\
**Marcus**: No no no!! No! Don't turn the page!!! Stop here, stop now! Please!!

**马库斯**：我，我无法再读下去了……\
**Marcus**: I, I can't read on ...

**马库斯**：我不喜欢这个结局……\
**Marcus**: I don't like this ending ...

**马库斯**：…………\
**Marcus**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：她死了……\
**Kakania**: She's gone ...

**马库斯**：……

**马库斯**：…………\
**Marcus**: ...

**伊索尔德**：……她是一位了不起的女士。\
**Isolde**: She was an incredible woman.

卡卡尼亚惊愕地看着她的脸——那上面浮现了她说过的……\
Kakania looks at her face in shock—studying it to find again the same face she'd spoken of.

——怜悯。\
Mercy.

**伊索尔德**：希望她不会再获得痛苦。\
**Isolde**: Her suffering ends here.

**伊索尔德**：医生。现在……您可以告诉我您的选择了吗？\
**Isolde**: Doctor. Have you ... decided?

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

卡卡尼亚只是失神地站着。\
Kakania can only stand there, dazed.

直到歌剧院外传来了响亮的轰鸣。\
Until a loud roar booms outside the opera house.

**伊索尔德**：……我必须离开了。\
**Isolde**: I must leave.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**伊索尔德**：……我会一直等待您的答复。\
**Isolde**: But I will wait for your answer.

第三幕，鞠躬，而后帷幕垂下。\
The third act, a bow, and then the curtain falls.

演员退场。\
The actors exit.

这就是故事的结局。\
This is the end of the story.

## 6TH-23 汉赛尔与格蕾特 / Hansel and Gretel

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

马库斯一直握着霍夫曼的手。\
Marcus holds Hofmann's hand all the while.

泪水一滴滴地打湿了字条。\
Tears wet the note, drop by drop.

让上面的墨水晕染开来。\
Causing the ink on it to bleed.

脑中狂乱的思绪全部退去了，血液奔流的轰鸣声也停止了。\
The chaotic thoughts in her mind all recede away. The roaring of her heart begins to slow.

在此刻的仅有，沉痛与茫然。\
At this moment, only grief and bewilderment remain.

**马库斯**：……为什么，霍夫曼女士会那么平静呢？她不害怕死亡吗？\
**Marcus**: Madam Hofmann was calm till the end. Why? Was she not afraid?

**马库斯**：……不，我读到了，从她指尖的战栗，她也是害怕的。\
**Marcus**: No. I just read her fear through her trembling fingers ...

**马库斯**：可是，她知道。假如她流露出来，会让我更加害怕……\
**Marcus**: But she would not show it. She knew it would've frightened me ...

**马库斯**：……\
**Marcus**: ...

**通讯器**：重复。\
**Communicator**: Repeat.

通讯器唐突地响了起来。\
The communicator rings again.

**通讯器**：“暴雨”倒计时24小时。所有外勤人员，立刻返回基金会总部避难。\
**Communicator**: This is the 24 hour countdown to the "Storm." All personnel must return to the headquarters.

**通讯器**：重复。“暴雨”倒计时24小时……\
**Communicator**: Repeat. This is the 24 hour countdown to the "Storm" ...

**通讯器**：哔哔——\
**Communicator**: Beep.

**通讯器**：霍夫曼，我是塞梅尔维斯。已经到最后预定的撤离时间了。\
**Communicator**: Hofmann, this is Semmelweis. You must leave now. Last call.

**通讯器**：……你知道的，如果时间已到，我们不会等待。\
**Communicator**: ... You know we won't wait if you miss it.

马库斯一把关闭了通讯器。\
Marcus turns off the communicator with one hand.

**马库斯**：……医生，“暴雨”就要落下了。\
**Marcus**: ... The "Storm" is coming, doctor.

**马库斯**：和我一起回总部避难吧……您可以使用霍夫曼女士的名额。\
**Marcus**: Come with me to the headquarters. You can take Madam Hofmann's place in the shelter.

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

医生未置一词。\
The doctor says nothing.

只是抬起头，凝望不存在的天幕。\
She just lifts her head, gazing up at a non-existent canopy.

然后，她开口了——像一个独角戏演员，对天上的众神做出自己的陈词。\
Then, she speaks—as if making a plea to the gods above.

**卡卡尼亚**：国王弥达斯在林间苦苦寻觅酒神的伴护，最智慧的精灵，聪明的西勒诺斯。\
**Kakania**: King Midas hunted in the woods, in search of Silenus, the wisest Satyr, the companion of the wine god.

**卡卡尼亚**：国王问：“对我们来说，什么样的东西好而美妙？”\
**Kakania**: "What is the best and most enticing thing for a man?" The king asked.

**卡卡尼亚**：而精灵回答：“随波逐流的苦难的孩子啊！你为何要得知这令你不快的话语呢？”\
**Kakania**: The Satyr laughed in response. "Children of mischance and misery! You are asking for an answer you wish not to hear."

**卡卡尼亚**：“那顶完美的便是你无法得到的：不曾被分娩，不曾存在——彻底的虚无！”\
**Kakania**: "And what is best is beyond your reach: to never be born, to never exist, to be nothing!"

**卡卡尼亚**：“但你仍有机会获得次等的完美——即刻迎接死亡。”\
**Kakania**: "But you still have the next best thing: die, and do it soon."

卡卡尼亚捂住脸，刺耳的笑声从她的指尖流出。\
Kakania covers her face, a piercing laugh escaping through her fingertips.

还有落雨般的泪水。\
Accompanied shortly after by tears.

**卡卡尼亚**：……我不在乎自己是否能够在“暴雨”中幸存。\
**Kakania**: I don't care if I could make it through the "Storm."

**卡卡尼亚**：我的末日……已经提前到来过了。\
**Kakania**: My end ... is already upon me.

**马库斯**：医生……\
**Marcus**: Doctor ...

**卡卡尼亚**：倘若我要这样耻辱地苟活，我宁可和世界一起毁灭。\
**Kakania**: I'd rather die here than to spend the rest of my life running from the "Storm."

**卡卡尼亚**：您去避难吧，马库斯小姐，我还有想做的事。\
**Kakania**: Get to safety, Ms. Marcus. I still have things to do.

**卡卡尼亚**：很抱歉，我们无法成为同事了。\
**Kakania**: It's a shame that we won't get to be colleagues.

她毅然转身，绝无回头。\
She turns resolutely, not once looking back.

但年轻的学徒也并未劝阻。\
But the young apprentice does not stop her.

她在想一件更重要的事。\
She is thinking of something more important.

**马库斯**：“我去林间寻觅，西勒诺斯。”\
**Marcus**: "Seeking Silenus in the woods ..."

**马库斯**：——西奥菲尔的诗，也是在这种绝望的心情中写下的吗？\
**Marcus**: Did Theophil write the poem in the same misery and despair?

**马库斯**：那他又为何把遗作命名为《拯救》……？\
**Marcus**: Then why did he call the painting The Salvation?

**马库斯**：他焚烧了自己和几乎所有的画，又为何独独留下它？还有那些格格不入的笔触……\
**Marcus**: He set fire to every piece of his work, but why leave this one out? And this strange way of drawing ...

思绪前所未有地清明。\
Her thoughts are clearer than ever before.

愧疚，疯狂，自责，焚烧一切的仇恨，还有无止境的思绪漫游。\
Guilt, madness, blame, a hatred that burns through everything, raging through her thoughts.

过去曾填充那张书页的，色彩纷杂的信息们，它们全都离开了。\
The past that once filled that page, it was gone now.

因为已经不再有人能替她做出抉择。\
Now no one would make her decisions for her.

**马库斯**：海因里希说我分享给了“你们”拯救之道，带“你们”面见了引导之人……\
**Marcus**: Heinrich said he showed the path to salvation and brought "you all" to the Guiding One ...

**马库斯**：拯救……拯救……难道说……\
**Marcus**: Salvation ... salvation ... Could it be ...

“我并不畏惧牺牲。我害怕的是一无所知地死去。”\
"What really scared me was not the threat to my life, but the possibility of dying ignorant."

闭上眼。\
She closes her eyes.

过去所阅读的一切信息，顺着因药剂而汹涌的血脉，尽数汇聚在眼前。\
All the information she has read in the past, along with the surging blood from the potion, converges before her eyes.

**马库斯**：……如果我成功了，便能阻止线索人物死亡。\
**Marcus**: "If I succeed, I can prevent the death of someone who holds the clues."

**马库斯**：即使我牺牲了，也将能使卡卡尼亚彻底背向伊索尔德。\
**Marcus**: "Even if I die, I'll still turn Kakania completely against Isolde."

**马库斯**：您取回的理性，是这么指引的吗，霍夫曼女士……？\
**Marcus**: This was your plan, madam ...?

“我并不畏惧牺牲。我害怕的是一无所知地死去。”\
"What really scared me was not the threat to my life, but the possibility of dying ignorant."

**马库斯**：——那么，我读懂了。\
**Marcus**: I know what to do now.

她猛地睁开眼睛，叫住转身离去的背影。\
She opens her eyes wide, calling out to the figure as she is about to leave.

**马库斯**：等一下，医生！我想到了一个可能性！\
**Marcus**: Doctor, wait! There might be another way!

卡卡尼亚并未理会。她已下了决心。\
But Kakania does not listen. She has made up her mind.

**马库斯**：——不要步入幽微！\
**Marcus**: ... Don't fall into darkness!

**卡卡尼亚**：——！\
**Kakania**: —!

离开的身影被拉住了，马库斯的面孔上是前所未有的决心。\
The departing figure is held back. Marcus fights with an unprecedented determination.

**马库斯**：不要走向疯狂，也不要走向绝望，医生。\
**Marcus**: Don't let madness or despair take over, doctor.

**马库斯**：这一切还没有结束，我的任务还没有结束……！\
**Marcus**: This is not the end. My mission is not over ...!

她将手伸进口袋，彻底按止本在疯狂响动，通知最后撤离警告的小小机器。\
She reaches into her pocket, silencing the small machine that has been frantically signaling the final evacuation warning.

**马库斯**：我们还有希望补救这一切——\
**Marcus**: There's still another way to end this ...

**马库斯**：用只有你和我才能做到的方法！\
**Marcus**: But it can only be done by you and me!

街道上一片火光。\
A blaze lights up the street, replacing the glow of dead electric lights.

人们在狂热的癔病中互相攻讦。\
People fight, throwing themselves into a frenzied hysteria.

如炸开的火药桶。\
The street looks like an exploded powder keg.

**勿忘我**：这个时代能在1914年的夏天之前消逝，已是引导之人最大的慈悲。\
**Forget Me Not**: The Guiding One is merciful in bringing this era to an end before the summer of 1914.

**勿忘我**：民族主义者们，世界主义者们，神秘主义者们，理性主义者们，进步主义者们，保守主义者们，狂热者们，旁观者们……\
**Forget Me Not**: Here, the nationalists, the internationalists, the arcanists, the rationalists, the progressives, the conservatives, the fanatics, the bystanders ...

**勿忘我**：他们狂妄地诉诸激情，坚信理念即是世界。\
**Forget Me Not**: They indulge in passion, insisting that it is their ideals that make up the world.

**勿忘我**：谁又能想到，秉持着进步和理性的明烛竟能走向充满硝烟的结局。\
**Forget Me Not**: Who would have thought that such a progressive and sensible era would end in a barbaric war?

**勿忘我**：而最终，他们都将被时代冲刷，如一粒尘埃。\
**Forget Me Not**: Yet in the end, like dust, they will be swept away and forgotten by time.

**勿忘我**：只有真正的信徒，能从末日大火中幸存下来。\
**Forget Me Not**: Only the true believers will survive the end.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

**勿忘我**：但我需提醒您……\
**Forget Me Not**: But I must regretfully remind you ...

**勿忘我**：即使您做出了杰出的功绩，杀害同伴也是逾越的。\
**Forget Me Not**: Killing one of our own, despite your merits, is a violation of the rules.

**勿忘我**：我会向引导之人通报这一点。\
**Forget Me Not**: I will report this to the Guiding One.

**伊索尔德**：……\
**Isolde**: ...

她的笑容依然完美而空洞。\
Her smile remains picture-perfect yet hollow.

**伊索尔德**：勿忘我先生，可以让我一个人待一会吗？\
**Isolde**: May I have a moment alone, Mr. Forget Me Not?

**伊索尔德**：我想最后再看看这座城市。\
**Isolde**: I want to look at this city one last time.

**勿忘我**：……随便你。\
**Forget Me Not**: ... Whatever you want.

勿忘我厌烦地走开了。

他早已腻味了这场空洞的谈话。\
Forget Me Not walks away in boredom.

伊索尔德独自伫立于街头。\
He has long tired of this maddening conversation.

人们狂欢、起舞，释放内心的压抑，拥抱原初的激情。\
Isolde stands alone on the street.

但她的目光并未映出任何图景。\
People around her celebrate, dance, releasing their inner repression, and their primal passions.

她只是在等待。\
But none of that matters to her.

等待天空沉坠。\
She is merely waiting.

视频3-卡卡尼亚出现 暂未上传\
Waiting for the sky to fall.

**伊索尔德**：——医生！\
**Isolde**: Doctor!

视频3结束

**卡卡尼亚**：……我想明白了，伊索尔德。\
**Kakania**: ... I've thought about this and made up my mind, Isolde.

**卡卡尼亚**：您的想法是正确的，我加入你们。\
**Kakania**: You were right. I will join you.

**伊索尔德**：……！\
**Isolde**: ...!

**伊索尔德**：我一直，一直在等您说出这句话……\
**Isolde**: I have been waiting to hear this for so, so long ...

**伊索尔德**：因为这原本就是您的梦想。现在，我终于可以把它还给您了……\
**Isolde**: I know this is what you want. Now, I can finally make your dream come true ...

**伊索尔德**：我……\
**Isolde**: I ...

卡卡尼亚递出手帕。\
Kakania extends a handkerchief.

拂去她喜悦的泪水。\
Wiping away her wild-eyed tears of joy.

**卡卡尼亚**：……在我们离开之前，我想最后缅怀一下旧世界。\
**Kakania**: Before we leave, I would like to take one last walk in this world.

**卡卡尼亚**：您能和我一起去一趟我的诊所吗？\
**Kakania**: Would you like to join me and walk to my clinic?

## 6TH-24 今夜星光灿烂 / E lucevan le stelle

**伊索尔德**：……您把这里包起来了。\
**Isolde**: You have everything wrapped up.

卡卡尼亚关上门，将末日的喧嚣拒之门外。\
Kakania shuts the door, dimming the apocalyptic clamor outside.

诊所依然杂乱、空旷、静谧。\
The clinic remains cluttered, empty, quiet.

只是不再有镜子的闪光。\
Only the mirrors no longer flash.

**卡卡尼亚**：是的，在那之后，我很恐惧看见镜子。\
**Kakania**: Yes. The mirror scares me after what happened.

**卡卡尼亚**：它会映出我丑恶的面容。\
**Kakania**: It truthfully reflects my ugly face, my disgusting soul.

**伊索尔德**：您并不丑恶，医生。您的梦想每时每刻都熠熠生辉。\
**Isolde**: You're not disgusting, doctor. How can someone disgusting have noble, high ideals like yours?

**卡卡尼亚**：是啊，所以我想，现在我可以揭开它了。\
**Kakania**: Hah, perhaps. Maybe you're right. It's time to lift the cloth.

卡卡尼亚猛地揭下了幕布。\
Kakania pulls back the curtain.

昏暗的房间一时骤亮。\
The dim room suddenly brightens.

**伊索尔德**：唔！\
**Isolde**: Ooh!

**伊索尔德**：好亮，您拉开了窗帘吗？\
**Isolde**: The light hurts, did you open the curtains?

**伊索尔德**：医生，我什么也看不到了！\
**Isolde**: Doctor, I can't see!

过度曝光的世界里，缓缓映出了一幅画作。\
An overexposed world slowly reveals a painting.

还有一个陌生的冷酷声音。\
And a strange, cold voice.

**卡卡尼亚**：看看这幅画，伊索尔德。\
**Kakania**: Look at this painting, Isolde.

**卡卡尼亚**：您是否想起了什么？\
**Kakania**: Does it remind you of anything?

**伊索尔德**：我看不清，医生……这里太亮了……\
**Isolde**: I can't see it clearly, doctor ... It's too bright in here ...

**伊索尔德**：您能把窗帘拉上吗？就一点……\
**Isolde**: Can you pull the curtains? Just a bit ...

**卡卡尼亚**：这是您哥哥的遗作，《拯救》。\
**Kakania**: This is the painting of your late brother, The Salvation.

**卡卡尼亚**：我们一直都忽视了一点，伊索尔德。直到海因里希死前说漏嘴。\
**Kakania**: We've overlooked a simple fact, Isolde. Until Heinrich's final words reminded us all.

**卡卡尼亚**：西奥菲尔的遗书充满切实的绝望，却又将自己的遗作命名为“拯救”。\
**Kakania**: Theophil wrote his note in despair, yet he called his last painting The Salvation.

**伊索尔德**：医生，这里太亮了，我们去其他地方说话好吗……？\
**Isolde**: Doctor, it's too bright in here. Can we please talk somewhere else?

她等待着那个人的眷顾与垂怜。\
She waits for a response of concern or pity.

但无人理会她的恳求。\
But she receives none.

**卡卡尼亚**：伊索尔德。我应当记得，贵族小姐只会唱歌是不够的，您的华尔兹跳得那样好，想必画笔也用得熟练。\
**Kakania**: How could I have missed this, Isolde? A noble lady such as you not only can sing and dance, but also draw.

**卡卡尼亚**：西奥菲尔出色，但不出彩；优秀，却不卓越。迪塔斯多夫家的通灵术多传于女性，您是比他更优秀的通灵者……\
**Kakania**: Theophil was a fine gentleman, but only fine. He was skilled, but not gifted. The women of the Dittarsdorfs have always been better mediums than the men. You're much more gifted than your brother ...

**卡卡尼亚**：我们该感谢你们吗？你们确实是兄妹，一个在绝望时发出呼喊，怜悯地将一切真实化为一首小诗传递给世人，将绝望的画作留给自己。\
**Kakania**: Should we be thankful of the two of you? You and your brother, a pair of messiahs of this era. One of you cried out and revealed the truth in a pitiful poem, and kept his despair in the form of art.

**伊索尔德**：呜呜……医生……\
**Isolde**: Ugh ... Doctor ...

**卡卡尼亚**：而另一个……“剜掉那最上层的油彩，露出底色，重新塑造它们”。\
**Kakania**: And the other ... wished to "scrape the paint off the top, reveal its true colors, and reshape it."

**卡卡尼亚**：……也就是你，伊索尔德小姐。你将那层绝望的底色剜去，放上了自己的怜悯。\
**Kakania**: That's you, Isolde. You tried to scrape off the despair and reshape the world with your compassionate, pitying hands.

**卡卡尼亚**：他将它创造，而你令其惊艳。\
**Kakania**: He created the art, and you completed it.

**卡卡尼亚**：是你们兄妹二人垂怜世人，共同创作了这幅画。\
**Kakania**: You and your brother are the co-creators of this painting, out of your pity for this world.

**卡卡尼亚**：——所以它幸免于难，在大火中被保全了。\
**Kakania**: ... And that's why it was the only work that survived the fire.

**卡卡尼亚**：是这样吗？告诉我，伊索尔德！\
**Kakania**: Am I right, Isolde? Tell me!

卡卡尼亚掷地有声。\
Kakania's words carry weight.

**卡卡尼亚**：你们二人在海因里希的引荐下，面见了重塑之手的领袖。你们目睹了那个奇迹的术式，见证了那拯救的一幕。\
**Kakania**: With Heinrich's help, the two of you met the leader of Manus Vindictae. You saw the miracle, you were shown the path to salvation.

**卡卡尼亚**：而可怜的、绝望的西奥菲尔，他无法承受这样的痛苦：他和你一样背负名为贵族的诅咒，既有向下俯瞰的傲慢，也有同情众生的怜悯。\
**Kakania**: But poor Theophil could not accept what he was told. Like you, he was cursed by his noble blood. He sympathized with the world, yet he still clung to the privileges of nobility.

**卡卡尼亚**：他不想加入重塑之手，又不想让战争来临。\
**Kakania**: He didn't want to work with Manus Vindictae, but he didn't want war either.

**卡卡尼亚**：他挣扎过，而当自己是被施恩者时，他只能书写出绝望。\
**Kakania**: He had his struggles. As a beneficiary of the salvation, writing of despair was his only way to vent.

**卡卡尼亚**：他宁愿在痛苦中了结自己——他伸出手，想带着你一起解脱。\
**Kakania**: He had to take his life to end the pain. And he wanted you to join him, so that you and he would be free of the torment together.

**卡卡尼亚**：但他忘了，你的生活本就是废墟，他在乎的一切，你都未曾拥有。世界的毁灭对于你，只是从一个废墟去另一个废墟。\
**Kakania**: But he overlooked the fact that, unlike him, you were already living in despair. Everything he had and cared about had never been yours. The destruction of this world meant nothing to you.

**伊索尔德**：我，我的头很痛……\
**Isolde**: My, my head really hurts ...

**卡卡尼亚**：所以你开了那一枪，出于对他的怜悯。\
**Kakania**: So you pulled the trigger on him, out of pity.

**伊索尔德**：我什么都看不清……您能让它变暗一点吗？\
**Isolde**: I can't see anything ... Can you please dim the room?

**卡卡尼亚**：——看着这幅画！看看这些镜子，伊索尔德！\
**Kakania**: Look at this painting! Look at these mirrors, Isolde!

**卡卡尼亚**：重塑之手的领袖给你看了什么？！“拯救之道”具体是什么？！是一个咒语吗？是一句术式吗？！\
**Kakania**: What did the leader of Manus Vindictae show you?! What is "the path to salvation"?! Is it a spell? A ritual?!

**卡卡尼亚**：——你是唯一知道这些事的人！！！\
**Kakania**: You're the only one who knows!!!

**马库斯**：医生，您不能再过度使用神秘术了……！\
**Marcus**: Doctor, you must stop using the mirror!

**马库斯**：这样强制显像，你们的精神都会崩溃的！\
**Marcus**: You will both collapse if you continue to force her!

**卡卡尼亚**：……没有办法了。\
**Kakania**: I'm running out of options.

**卡卡尼亚**：我要对她使用催眠。\
**Kakania**: I have to hypnotize her.

**伊索尔德**：……！\
**Isolde**: ...!

**伊索尔德**：您要对我使用催眠？哈哈哈……您……最厌恶催眠的卡卡尼亚医生，为此不惜和他人发起决斗的克拉拉小姐……要对我使用催眠……？！\
**Isolde**: Hypnotize me? Hahaha ... You, Ms. Klara, the doctor who resents hypnosis and had even fought a duel to stop it ... you are going to use it ... on me?!

**伊索尔德**：因为我是疯癫的、无理性的女人！恶毒、肮脏的巫婆！被诅咒的、不可沟通的神秘学家吗？！\
**Isolde**: Why? Because I'm a hysterical, irrational woman? The wicked witch? The cursed, inconsolable arcanist?!

**伊索尔德**：您为何要，要这样对待我……？！\
**Isolde**: Why, why are you like this to me?!

**卡卡尼亚**：……放轻松，伊索尔德小姐。\
**Kakania**: Please calm yourself, Isolde.

**卡卡尼亚**：请看这块怀表。\
**Kakania**: And fix your eyes on this watch.

**伊索尔德**：为什么？！是因为我又做错了吗？是因为我病得无药可救吗？\
**Isolde**: Why?! Did I do something wrong again? Am I hopelessly incurable?

**伊索尔德**：那您为什么，为什么，不能治好我呢……！！！\
**Isolde**: Why, why couldn't you, cure me?!

**伊索尔德**：您为什么不愿意再一次……从废墟中……拯救我呢……？\
**Isolde**: Can't you ... save me from despair ... one more time ...?

她望着这个美丽的女孩。\
She looks at the beautiful girl, her once-friend.

却不知如何拯救她。\
But she doesn't know how to save her.

**卡卡尼亚**：……睡吧，伊索尔德。\
**Kakania**: Sleep, Isolde.

**卡卡尼亚**：去那安然的居所，永夜的故乡。\
**Kakania**: To the peaceful place, to the home of night.

**伊索尔德**：…………\
**Isolde**: ...

**伊索尔德**：您真是世界上最残酷的人……\
**Isolde**: You're the cruelest of all ...

**伊索尔德**：倘若您已经下了决心，为何又要对我如此温柔呢……？\
**Isolde**: If you've made up your mind and think I'm guilty ... Why do you treat me so gently?

**伊索尔德**：如果这就是您的拯救的话……\
**Isolde**: If this is the salvation you brought ...

**伊索尔德**：我也……甘之如饴。\
**Isolde**: I will ... embrace it with joy.

她轻轻唱起了熟悉的歌谣。\
She begins a familiar aria, singing with all her heart.

不是作为任何人，而是作为她自己。\
Her voice at last not some guise or act, but her true self.

我献上珠宝 装饰圣母的衣摆\
I adorned the Madonna's mantle with jewels.

我将歌声献给天上的群星 令其璀璨\
And I gave my song to the stars, to the sky, which smiled more beautifully because of it.

在这绝望的时刻\
In the hour of sorrow.

主啊 为何 为何\
Why, oh why, Lord.

您为何对我如此残酷无情——\
Why do you repay me thus?

歌声从未离开过她。\
The song never left her.

**伊索尔德**：看啊，医生……\
**Isolde**: Look, doctor ...

**伊索尔德**：今夜……星光灿烂……\
**Isolde**: The stars ... are shining ...

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：现在，告诉我，伊索尔德。\
**Kakania**: Now, tell me, Isolde.

**卡卡尼亚**：你看着这幅画，想起了什么？\
**Kakania**: What do you think of when you look at this painting?

影像出现在镜中。\
Images appear in the mirror.

清晰，明亮，伴随着海潮的回声。\
Clear, bright, and accompanied by the echo of the tide.

**阿尔卡纳**：我喜欢你们小团体的名字，“魔圈”……\
**Arcana**: I am intrigued by the name of your little group. "The Circle" ...

**西奥菲尔**：是的，我们每个人的内部都存在一种神秘的力量。我们在这股力量中获得了自己的上帝，并通过它与严苛的自然作对。\
**Theophil**: Yes, unlike other animals, there's a power in every one of us. It's the source of our instinct. Following it, man survived the cruelty of nature.

**西奥菲尔**：为了敬畏这股非凡，原始人便在自己的周围画了一个魔圈，将它视作神力的象征，作为从自然独立出去的宣言。\
**Theophil**: In awe of this extraordinary power, the first of man drew a magical circle on the ground, symbolizing a higher power, and declaring that man would no longer be at the mercy of nature.

**西奥菲尔**：而这——就是最初的圆，最初的巫术，最初的艺术！\
**Theophil**: That was the first circle. The first magic, the first art!

**阿尔卡纳**：呵呵……\
**Arcana**: Heh heh ...

**阿尔卡纳**：很有趣的看法。\
**Arcana**: An interesting take.

**阿尔卡纳**：恰好，我这里也有一个圆。\
**Arcana**: I happened to have a circle too.

**阿尔卡纳**：这也是一个古老的奇迹，一个拯救的魔圈。\
**Arcana**: This is also an ancient miracle, a circle of salvation.

**阿尔卡纳**：它会庇佑被拣选者越过雨幕。\
**Arcana**: It shelters the chosen ones from the falling rain,

**阿尔卡纳**：抵达应许之地。\
**Arcana**: and sees them to the promised land.

模糊的呢喃自镜中发出。\
A vague murmur emanates from the mirror.

宛如远古的回声。\
Like an ancient echo.

**马库斯**：……！就是这个！\
**Marcus**: Yes! That's it!

**马库斯**：我看到了！医生！我听见了！\
**Marcus**: I saw it! Doctor! I heard it!

**马库斯**：我“阅读”到了免疫“暴雨”的术式，我们成功了！！！\
**Marcus**: I "read" the "Storm" immunity ritual! We did it!!!

**卡卡尼亚**：……\
**Kakania**: ...

**卡卡尼亚**：终于……\
**Kakania**: Finally ...

卡卡尼亚精疲力尽地跌坐在地。\
Kakania falls to the ground, exhausted.

马库斯再次打开了通讯器。\
Marcus, ready now to face the communicator again, activates it.

这一次，它带来的终于不再是坏消息。\
This time, though, it brings good news.

**露西**：前线发来消息，有人传回了重塑之手的免疫术式。\
**Lucy**: News from the frontline. They have sent home the "Storm" immunity ritual.

**露西**：诸位，开工吧。\
**Lucy**: Get to work, people.

**露西**：——从现在开始，到“暴雨”落下的22个小时里。整个世界都是我们的试验场。\
**Lucy**: In the 22 hours before the "Storm" arrives, the whole world is our proving ground.
